AutoOR: Scalably Post-training LLMs to Autoformalize Operations Research Problems
Authors: Sumeet Ramesh Motwani, Chuan Du, Aleksander Petrov, Christopher Davis, Philip Torr, Antonio Papania-Davis, Weishi Yan
First: 2026-04-18T03:24:54+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-06T17:41:05+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Optimization problems are central to decision-making in manufacturing, logistics, scheduling, and other industrial settings. Translating complicated descriptions of these problems into solver-ready formulations requires specialized operations research (OR) expertise, making it hard to scale. We present AutoOR, a scalable synthetic data generation and reinforcement learning pipeline that trains LLMs to autoformalize optimization problems specified in natural language across linear, mixed-integer, and non-linear categories. AutoOR generates verified training data from standard optimization forms and uses solver execution feedback as the reward signal for RL post-training. AutoOR applied to an 8B model achieves state-of-the-art or competitive results across six established OR benchmarks, matching significantly larger frontier models. For a non-linear problem class involving physical dynamics, where frontier models score near 0%, we introduce a curriculum RL strategy that bootstraps from limited initial training data to make this class tractable for post-training. We believe that methods such as AutoOR can significantly accelerate industrial decision-making with AI.
中文标题/摘要
标题：AutoOR：可扩展地后训练大语言模型以自动形式化运筹学问题
优化问题是制造、物流、调度及其他工业场景中决策的核心。将这些问题的复杂描述转化为求解器可读的公式需要专门的运筹学专业知识，这限制了规模化应用。我们提出AutoOR，一个可扩展的合成数据生成与强化学习流水线，用于训练大语言模型自动形式化自然语言描述的优化问题，涵盖线性、混合整数和非线性类别。AutoOR从标准优化形式生成经过验证的训练数据，并以求解器执行反馈作为后训练强化学习的奖励信号。将AutoOR应用于8B模型，在六个既定运筹学基准上取得了最先进或具有竞争力的结果，与显著更大的前沿模型相当。针对涉及物理动力学的非线性问题类别（前沿模型得分接近0%），我们引入了一种课程强化学习策略，从有限的初始训练数据中引导，使该类别在后训练中变得可处理。我们相信，AutoOR这类方法能够借助人工智能显著加速工业决策。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces AutoOR, a pipeline designed to train large language models to automatically formalize operations research problems from natural language descriptions into solver-ready formulations, addressing the scalability challenge posed by the need for specialized OR expertise. The method combines scalable synthetic data generation from standard optimization forms with reinforcement learning post-training, using solver execution feedback as the reward signal. Applied to an 8B model, AutoOR achieves state-of-the-art or competitive results across six established OR benchmarks, matching significantly larger frontier models, and notably makes a non-linear problem class involving physical dynamics tractable through a curriculum RL strategy that bootstraps from limited initial data, where frontier models previously scored near 0%.
该论文提出了AutoOR，一个用于训练大语言模型自动将自然语言描述的操作研究问题形式化为求解器可读格式的流程，解决了因需要专业OR知识而难以扩展的问题。该方法结合了从标准优化形式生成可验证训练数据的可扩展合成数据生成，以及基于求解器执行反馈作为奖励信号的强化学习后训练。将AutoOR应用于8B模型后，在六个已建立的OR基准测试中取得了最先进或具有竞争力的结果，与显著更大的前沿模型性能相当，并且通过一种从有限初始数据中引导的课程强化学习策略，使得涉及物理动力学的非线性问题类别变得可处理，而此前前沿模型在该类别上的得分接近0%。
When Life Gives You BC, Make Q-functions: Extracting Q-values from Behavior Cloning for On-Robot Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Lakshita Dodeja, Ondrej Biza, Shivam Vats, Stephen Hart, Stefanie Tellex, Robin Walters, Karl Schmeckpeper, Thomas Weng
First: 2026-05-06T17:40:11+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-06T17:40:11+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Behavior Cloning (BC) has emerged as a highly effective paradigm for robot learning. However, BC lacks a self-guided mechanism for online improvement after demonstrations have been collected. Existing offline-to-online learning methods often cause policies to replace previously learned good actions due to a distribution mismatch between offline data and online learning. In this work, we propose Q2RL, Q-Estimation and Q-Gating from BC for Reinforcement Learning, an algorithm for efficient offline-to-online learning. Our method consists of two parts: (1) Q-Estimation extracts a Q-function from a BC policy using a few interaction steps with the environment, followed by online RL with (2) Q-Gating, which switches between BC and RL policy actions based on their respective Q-values to collect samples for RL policy training. Across manipulation tasks from D4RL and robomimic benchmarks, Q2RL outperforms SOTA offline-to-online learning baselines on success rate and time to convergence. Q2RL is efficient enough to be applied in an on-robot RL setting, learning robust policies for contact-rich and high precision manipulation tasks such as pipe assembly and kitting, in 1-2 hours of online interaction, achieving success rates of up to 100% and up to 3.75x improvement against the original BC policy. Code and video are available at https://pages.rai-inst.com/q2rl_website/
中文标题/摘要
标题：当生活给你行为克隆，就做Q函数：从行为克隆中提取Q值用于机器人强化学习
行为克隆已成为机器人学习的高效范式，但缺乏演示数据收集后的在线自我改进机制。现有离线到在线学习方法常因离线数据与在线学习分布不匹配，导致策略替换先前学到的良好动作。本文提出Q2RL（基于行为克隆的Q值估计与门控强化学习），一种高效的离线到在线学习算法。该方法包含两部分：(1) Q值估计，通过与环境少量交互从BC策略提取Q函数；(2) Q门控，基于各自Q值在BC与RL策略动作间切换，为RL策略训练收集样本。在D4RL和robomimic基准的操控任务中，Q2RL在成功率和收敛时间上均优于现有离线到在线学习基线。该方法可高效应用于机器人在线强化学习，在1-2小时在线交互中学习管道组装、套件装配等接触密集高精度操控任务的鲁棒策略，成功率高达100%，较原始BC策略提升达3.75倍。代码与视频见https://pages.rai-inst.com/q2rl_website/
Summary / 总结
Behavior Cloning (BC) is effective for robot learning but lacks mechanisms for online improvement after demonstrations, often leading to performance degradation due to distribution mismatch during offline-to-online learning. To address this, the authors propose Q2RL, which first extracts a Q-function from a BC policy using minimal environment interactions, then employs Q-Gating to switch between BC and RL actions based on Q-values for sample collection. Experiments on D4RL and robomimic benchmarks show Q2RL outperforms state-of-the-art baselines in success rate and convergence speed, achieving up to 100% success and 3.75x improvement over BC in on-robot tasks like pipe assembly within 1-2 hours.
行为克隆在机器人学习中效果显著，但缺乏演示后的在线改进机制，且离线到在线学习常因数据分布不匹配导致策略退化。为此，作者提出Q2RL算法，先通过少量环境交互从行为克隆策略中提取Q函数，再使用Q门控机制根据Q值切换行为克隆与强化学习动作以收集训练样本。在D4RL和robomimic基准测试中，Q2RL在成功率和收敛速度上超越现有最优基线，并在管道组装等机器人任务中1-2小时内达到100%成功率，较原始行为克隆提升3.75倍。
What Matters in Practical Learned Image Compression
Authors: Kedar Tatwawadi, Parisa Rahimzadeh, Zhanghao Sun, Zhiqi Chen, Ziyun Yang, Sanjay Nair, Divija Hasteer, Oren Rippel
First: 2026-05-06T17:17:51+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-06T17:17:51+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
One of the major differentiators unlocked by learned codecs relative to their hard-coded traditional counterparts is their ability to be optimized directly to appeal to the human visual system. Despite this potential, a perceptual yet practical image codec is yet to be proposed. In this work, we aim to close this gap. We conduct a comprehensive study of the key modeling choices that govern the design of a practical learned image codec, jointly optimized for perceptual quality and runtime -- including within the ablations several novel techniques. We then perform performance-aware neural architecture search over millions of backbone configurations to identify models that achieve the target on-device runtime while maximizing compression performance as captured by perceptual metrics. We combine the various optimizations to construct a new codec that achieves a significantly improved tradeoff between speed and perceptual quality. Based on rigorous subjective user studies, it provides 2.3-3x bitrate savings against AV1, AV2, VVC, ECM and JPEG-AI, and 20-40% bitrate savings against the best learned codec alternatives. At the same time, on an iPhone 17 Pro Max, it encodes 12MP images as fast as 230ms, and decodes them in 150ms -- faster than most top ML-based codecs run on a V100 GPU.
中文标题/摘要
标题：实用化学习型图像压缩中的关键因素
学习型编解码器相对于传统硬编码编解码器的主要区别之一，在于其能够直接针对人类视觉系统进行优化。尽管具有这一潜力，但目前尚未提出一种既符合感知质量又实用的图像编解码器。 在本工作中，我们旨在弥合这一差距。我们对决定实用化学习型图像编解码器设计的关键建模选择进行了全面研究，这些选择共同优化了感知质量和运行时间——包括消融实验中的若干新技术。随后，我们在数百万个骨干配置上执行了性能感知的神经架构搜索，以识别在目标设备上实现运行时间的同时，最大化由感知指标衡量的压缩性能的模型。 我们结合各种优化构建了一种新的编解码器，在速度和感知质量之间实现了显著改进的权衡。基于严格的主观用户研究，与AV1、AV2、VVC、ECM和JPEG-AI相比，它节省了2.3-3倍的比特率，与最佳学习型编解码器替代方案相比节省了20-40%的比特率。同时，在iPhone 17 Pro Max上，它编码1200万像素图像仅需230毫秒，解码仅需150毫秒——比大多数顶级基于机器学习的编解码器在V100 GPU上的运行速度更快。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the gap in practical learned image compression by jointly optimizing for perceptual quality and runtime. The authors conduct a comprehensive study of key modeling choices, including novel techniques, and perform performance-aware neural architecture search over millions of backbone configurations to identify models that balance on-device runtime with perceptual compression metrics. The resulting codec achieves 2.3-3x bitrate savings against traditional codecs like AV1 and VVC, and 20-40% savings over learned alternatives, while encoding 12MP images in 230ms and decoding in 150ms on an iPhone 17 Pro Max, outperforming most ML-based codecs on a V100 GPU.
本文旨在解决实用化学习图像压缩中感知质量与运行时的平衡问题。作者系统研究了关键建模选择，包括多项新技术，并通过性能感知的神经架构搜索，在数百万个骨干配置中筛选出兼顾设备端运行时间和感知压缩指标的模型。最终编解码器相比AV1、VVC等传统方案节省2.3-3倍码率，比最佳学习编解码器节省20-40%码率，同时在iPhone 17 Pro Max上以230毫秒编码、150毫秒解码1200万像素图像，速度超过多数在V100 GPU上运行的顶级机器学习编解码器。
Adaptive Policy Selection and Fine-Tuning under Interaction Budgets for Offline-to-Online Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Alper Kamil Bozkurt, Xiaoan Xu, Shangtong Zhang, Miroslav Pajic, Yuichi Motai
First: 2026-05-06T16:51:44+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-06T16:51:44+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In offline-to-online reinforcement learning (O2O-RL), policies are first safely trained offline using previously collected datasets and then further fine-tuned for tasks via limited online interactions. In a typical O2O-RL pipeline, candidate policies trained with offline RL are evaluated via either off-policy evaluation (OPE) or online evaluation (OE). The policy with the highest estimated value is then deployed and continually fine-tuned. However, this setup has two main issues. First, OPE can be unreliable, making it risky to deploy a policy based solely on those estimates, whereas OE may identify a viable policy with substantial online interaction, which could have been used for fine-tuning. Second--and more importantly--it is also often not possible to determine a priori whether a pretrained policy will improve with post-deployment fine-tuning, especially in non-stationary environments. As a result, procedures committing to a single deployed policy are impractical in many real-world settings. Moreover, a naive remedy that exhaustively fine-tunes all candidates would violate interaction budget constraints and is likewise infeasible. In this paper, we propose a novel adaptive approach for policy selection and fine-tuning under online interaction budgets in O2O-RL. Following the standard pipeline, we first train a set of candidate policies with different offline RL algorithms and hyperparameters; we then perform OPE to obtain initial performance estimates. We next adaptively select and fine-tune the policies based on their predicted performance via an upper-confidence-bound approach thereby making efficient use of online interactions. We demonstrate that our approach improves upon O2O-RL baselines with various benchmarks.
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses two key issues in offline-to-online reinforcement learning (O2O-RL): unreliable off-policy evaluation (OPE) and the uncertainty of whether a pretrained policy will improve with fine-tuning, especially under limited online interaction budgets. The authors propose an adaptive method that first trains multiple candidate policies using different offline RL algorithms and hyperparameters, then uses OPE for initial estimates, and finally selects and fine-tunes policies via an upper-confidence-bound approach to efficiently allocate online interactions. Experimental results show that the proposed approach outperforms existing O2O-RL baselines across various benchmarks.
本文针对离线到在线强化学习（O2O-RL）中的两个关键问题：离线策略评估（OPE）不可靠，以及预训练策略在微调后是否提升的不确定性，特别是在有限的在线交互预算下。作者提出了一种自适应方法，首先使用不同的离线强化学习算法和超参数训练多个候选策略，然后通过OPE获得初始性能估计，最后利用上置信界方法自适应地选择和微调策略，以高效利用在线交互。实验结果表明，该方法在各种基准测试中优于现有的O2O-RL基线。
Physiologically Grounded Driver Behavior Classification: SHAP-Driven Elite Feature Selection and Hybrid Gradient Boosting for Multimodal Physiological Signals
Authors: Sahar Askari, Mohammad Mahdi Mirza Ali Mohammadi, Fatemeh Ensafdoust, Amin Golnari, Saeid Sanei
First: 2026-05-06T16:48:57+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-06T16:48:57+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
An interpretable and scalable framework for decoding driving behaviors from multimodal physiological signals is proposed in this study. We utilize multimodal physiological driving behavior large-scale dataset comprising synchronized electroencephalogram (EEG), electromyography (EMG), and galvanic skin response (GSR) signals. Our approach involves rigorous preprocessing followed by a domain-specific feature extraction pipeline targeting time-domain, frequency-domain, and derived physiological indices. To address high dimensionality, we employ SHAP-based elite feature selection, retaining the top 250 features to reduce computational overhead while preserving predictive power. Hyperparameter optimization for extreme gradient boosting (XGBoost) and light gradient boosting machine (LightGBM) models is conducted using Bayesian optimization via Optuna. Finally, a weighted soft-voting ensemble is constructed to leverage the complementary strengths of both gradient boosting frameworks. The results demonstrate that the proposed ensemble achieves a test accuracy of 80.91% and a macro-F1 score of 0.79, significantly outperforming single-modality baselines and traditional machine learning models. Ablation studies confirm an 8% performance gain over the best single modality (EEG), validating the necessity of multimodal fusion. SHAP analysis further validates the physiological plausibility of the model, revealing that the EEG contributes the majority of predictive weight, GSR and EMG features provide critical discriminatory signals for high-arousal and motor-intensive maneuvers.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于生理基础的驾驶员行为分类：面向多模态生理信号的SHAP驱动精英特征选择与混合梯度提升
本研究提出了一种可解释且可扩展的框架，用于从多模态生理信号中解码驾驶行为。我们利用包含同步脑电图（EEG）、肌电图（EMG）和皮肤电反应（GSR）信号的多模态生理驾驶行为大规模数据集。该方法包括严格的预处理，随后是面向时域、频域和衍生生理指标的特定领域特征提取流程。为解决高维问题，我们采用基于SHAP的精英特征选择，保留前250个特征以减少计算开销同时保持预测能力。通过Optuna进行贝叶斯优化，对极端梯度提升（XGBoost）和轻量梯度提升机（LightGBM）模型进行超参数优化。最后，构建加权软投票集成以利用两种梯度提升框架的互补优势。结果表明，所提出的集成模型实现了80.91%的测试准确率和0.79的宏F1分数，显著优于单模态基线和传统机器学习模型。消融研究证实，相较于最佳单模态（EEG）性能提升8%，验证了多模态融合的必要性。SHAP分析进一步验证了模型的生理合理性，揭示EEG贡献了大部分预测权重，而GSR和EMG特征为高唤醒和运动密集型操作提供了关键判别信号。
Summary / 总结
This study proposes an interpretable framework for classifying driver behaviors using multimodal physiological signals, including EEG, EMG, and GSR. The method involves domain-specific feature extraction, SHAP-based elite feature selection to reduce dimensionality, and a weighted soft-voting ensemble of XGBoost and LightGBM models optimized via Bayesian search. The ensemble achieves 80.91% test accuracy and a macro-F1 of 0.79, outperforming single-modality baselines by 8%, with SHAP analysis confirming EEG as the dominant modality while GSR and EMG contribute to high-arousal and motor-intensive maneuvers.
该研究提出了一种可解释的框架，利用多模态生理信号（包括脑电图、肌电图和皮肤电反应）对驾驶行为进行分类。方法包括领域特定特征提取、基于SHAP的精英特征选择以降低维度，以及通过贝叶斯优化调参的XGBoost和LightGBM加权软投票集成模型。该集成模型实现了80.91%的测试准确率和0.79的宏F1分数，比最佳单模态基线高出8%，SHAP分析证实脑电图是主要模态，而皮肤电反应和肌电图对高唤醒和运动密集型操作提供关键判别信号。
Rollout Pass-Rate Control: Steering Binary-Reward RL Toward Its Most Informative Regime
Authors: Tianshu Zhu, Wenyu Zhang, Xiaoying Zuo, Lun Tian, Haotian Zhao, Yucheng Zeng, Jingnan Gu, Daxiang Dong, Jianmin Wu, Dawei Yin, Dou Shen
First: 2026-05-06T16:44:38+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-06T16:44:38+00:00
Comments: 25 pages, 8 figures, 11 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
SWE-bench-style agentic reinforcement learning relies on expensive stateful trajectories, yet substantial compute is wasted on sampled rollout groups with skewed pass rates, where binary rewards provide a weak contrastive signal. We frame this inefficiency as a pass-rate control problem and show that a 50% pass rate is the most informative operating point: it maximizes reward entropy, the probability of surviving group filtering, RLOO advantage energy under GRPO, and success--failure contrastive structure. Guided by this principle, we propose Prefix Sampling (PS), which replays trajectory prefixes to steer skewed groups toward this regime: successful prefixes serve as head starts for mostly failing groups, while failing prefixes serve as handicaps for mostly passing groups. In stateful agent environments, prefix states are reconstructed through replay while replayed tokens are excluded from the loss, restricting optimization to continuations generated by the current policy. On SWE-bench-style agentic RL, PS delivers end-to-end wall-clock speedups of 2.01x on Qwen3-14B and 1.55x on Qwen3-32B while preserving or improving final verified performance. For 14B, the SWE-bench Verified peak rises from the baseline peak of 0.273 to 0.295 under PS. Additional mathematical reasoning experiments on AIME 2025 show the same pass-rate control pattern and decompose the gains into replay, bidirectional coverage, and adaptive control.
中文标题/摘要
标题：展开通过率控制：将二元奖励强化学习导向其最具信息量的区间
SWE-bench风格的智能体强化学习依赖于昂贵的有状态轨迹，然而大量计算浪费在通过率偏斜的采样展开组上，此时二元奖励提供的对比信号较弱。我们将这种低效问题建模为通过率控制问题，并证明50%的通过率是最具信息量的工作点：它最大化奖励熵、通过组过滤的生存概率、GRPO下的RLOO优势能量以及成功-失败对比结构。基于这一原则，我们提出前缀采样（PS），该方法重放轨迹前缀以将偏斜组引导至该区间：成功前缀作为多数失败组的先导，而失败前缀作为多数通过组的障碍。在有状态智能体环境中，前缀状态通过重放重建，同时重放的token从损失中排除，将优化限制在当前策略生成的延续上。在SWE-bench风格的智能体强化学习中，PS在Qwen3-14B上实现了2.01倍的端到端加速，在Qwen3-32B上实现了1.55倍的加速，同时保持或提升了最终验证性能。对于14B模型，SWE-bench Verified峰值从基线峰值0.273提升至PS下的0.295。在AIME 2025上的额外数学推理实验显示了相同的通过率控制模式，并将收益分解为重放、双向覆盖和自适应控制。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses inefficiency in SWE-bench-style agentic reinforcement learning, where compute is wasted on rollout groups with skewed pass rates that yield weak binary reward signals. The authors frame this as a pass-rate control problem, identifying a 50% pass rate as the most informative operating point that maximizes reward entropy and contrastive structure. They propose Prefix Sampling (PS), which replays trajectory prefixes to steer skewed groups toward this regime, using successful prefixes as head starts for failing groups and failing prefixes as handicaps for passing groups, while excluding replayed tokens from the loss. On SWE-bench-style agentic RL, PS achieves wall-clock speedups of 2.01x on Qwen3-14B and 1.55x on Qwen3-32B, with the SWE-bench Verified peak rising from 0.273 to 0.295 for 14B, and additional experiments on AIME 2025 confirm the same pass-rate control pattern and decompose gains into replay, bidirectional coverage, and adaptive control.
该论文针对SWE-bench风格智能体强化学习中，因通过率偏斜的采样组浪费大量计算且二元奖励信号弱的问题，将其建模为通过率控制问题，并指出50%通过率是最具信息量的工作点，能最大化奖励熵和对比结构。作者提出前缀采样（PS）方法，通过重放轨迹前缀将偏斜组引导至该区域：对多数失败组，成功前缀作为领先起点；对多数通过组，失败前缀作为障碍，同时重放令牌不参与损失计算。在SWE-bench风格智能体强化学习中，PS在Qwen3-14B上实现2.01倍加速，在Qwen3-32B上实现1.55倍加速，14B模型的SWE-bench Verified峰值从基线0.273提升至0.295；AIME 2025上的数学推理实验进一步验证了该通过率控制模式，并将增益分解为重放、双向覆盖和自适应控制。
LineRides: Line-Guided Reinforcement Learning for Bicycle Robot Stunts
Authors: Seungeun Rho, Shamel Fahmi, Jeonghwan Kim, Arianna Ilvonen, Sehoon Ha, Gabriel Nelson
First: 2026-05-06T16:43:28+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-06T16:43:28+00:00
Comments: Published in IEEE Robotics and Automation Letters (RA-L), 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Designing reward functions for agile robotic maneuvers in reinforcement learning remains difficult, and demonstration-based approaches often require reference motions that are unavailable for novel platforms or extreme stunts. We present LineRides, a line-guided learning framework that enables a custom bicycle robot to acquire diverse, commandable stunt behaviors from a user-provided spatial guideline and sparse key-orientations, without demonstrations or explicit timing. LineRides handles physically infeasible guidelines using a tracking margin that permits controlled deviation, resolves temporal ambiguity by measuring progress via traveled distance along the guideline, and disambiguates motion details through position- and sequence-based key-orientations. We evaluate LineRides on the Ultra Mobility Vehicle (UMV) and show that the policy trained with our methods supports seamless transitions between normal driving and stunt execution, enabling five distinct stunts on command: MiniHop, LargeHop, ThreePointTurn, Backflip, and DriftTurn.
中文标题/摘要
标题：LineRides：基于线条引导的自行车机器人特技强化学习
在强化学习中，为敏捷机器人动作设计奖励函数仍然困难，而基于演示的方法通常需要参考运动，这对于新型平台或极限特技而言不可用。我们提出LineRides，一种线条引导的学习框架，使定制自行车机器人能够从用户提供的空间引导线和稀疏关键朝向中获取多样、可指挥的特技行为，无需演示或显式时序。LineRides通过允许受控偏差的跟踪裕度处理物理上不可行的引导线，通过沿引导线行进的距离测量进度解决时间模糊性，并通过基于位置和序列的关键朝向消除运动细节歧义。我们在超机动车辆（UMV）上评估LineRides，结果表明，使用我们的方法训练的策略支持正常驾驶与特技执行之间的无缝切换，可实现五种不同的指挥特技：小跳、大跳、三点转弯、后空翻和漂移转弯。
Summary / 总结
LineRides addresses the challenge of designing reward functions for agile robotic stunts by introducing a line-guided reinforcement learning framework that eliminates the need for demonstrations or explicit timing. The method uses a user-provided spatial guideline and sparse key-orientations to define stunt behaviors, handling physically infeasible guidelines with a tracking margin and resolving temporal ambiguity through progress measured by traveled distance. Evaluated on the Ultra Mobility Vehicle (UMV), the trained policy enables seamless transitions between normal driving and five distinct commandable stunts—MiniHop, LargeHop, ThreePointTurn, Backflip, and DriftTurn—demonstrating the framework's effectiveness in acquiring diverse stunt behaviors without reference motions.

Unified Framework of Distributional Regret in Multi-Armed Bandits and Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Harin Lee, Min-hwan Oh
First: 2026-05-06T16:38:30+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-06T16:38:30+00:00
Comments: Accepted at the Conference of Learning Theory (COLT) 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We study the distribution of regret in stochastic multi-armed bandits and episodic reinforcement learning through a unified framework. We formalize a distributional regret bound as a probabilistic guarantee that holds uniformly over all confidence levels $δ\in (0,1]$, thereby characterizing the regret distribution across the full range of $δ$. We present a simple UCBVI-style algorithm with exploration bonus $\min\{c_{1,k}/N, c_{2,k}/\sqrt{N}\}$, where $N$ denotes the visit count and $(c_{1,k},c_{2,k})$ are user-specified parameters. For arbitrary parameter sequences, we derive general gap-independent and gap-dependent distributional regret bounds, yielding a principled characterization of how the parameters control the trade-off between expected performance, tail risk, and instance-dependent behavior. In particular, our bounds achieve optimal trade-offs between expected and distributional regret in both minimax and instance-dependent regimes. As a special case, for multi-armed bandits with $A$ arms and horizon $T$, we obtain a distributional regret bound of order $\mathcal{O}(\sqrt{AT}\log(1/δ))$, confirming the conjecture of Lattimore & Szepesvári (2020, Section 17.1) for the first time.
中文标题/摘要
标题：多臂老虎机与强化学习中分布遗憾的统一框架
我们通过一个统一框架研究随机多臂老虎机和情节式强化学习中的遗憾分布。我们将分布遗憾界形式化为一个概率保证，该保证对所有置信水平δ∈(0,1]一致成立，从而刻画了δ全范围内的遗憾分布。我们提出了一种简单的UCBVI风格算法，其探索奖励为min{c_{1,k}/N, c_{2,k}/√N}，其中N表示访问次数，(c_{1,k}, c_{2,k})是用户指定的参数。对于任意参数序列，我们推导出通用的与间隙无关和与间隙相关的分布遗憾界，从而原则性地刻画了参数如何控制期望性能、尾部风险和实例依赖行为之间的权衡。特别地，我们的界在极小极大和实例依赖两种机制下均实现了期望遗憾与分布遗憾之间的最优权衡。作为特例，对于具有A个臂和时域T的多臂老虎机，我们得到了阶为O(√AT log(1/δ))的分布遗憾界，首次证实了Lattimore & Szepesvári (2020, 第17.1节)的猜想。
Summary / 总结
This paper proposes a unified framework for studying the distribution of regret in stochastic multi-armed bandits and episodic reinforcement learning, motivated by the need for probabilistic guarantees that hold uniformly over all confidence levels. The method introduces a UCBVI-style algorithm with an exploration bonus of the form min{c1,k/N, c2,k/√N}, where N is the visit count and (c1,k, c2,k) are user-specified parameters, and derives general gap-independent and gap-dependent distributional regret bounds that characterize the trade-off between expected performance, tail risk, and instance-dependent behavior. The main experimental results show that the bounds achieve optimal trade-offs in both minimax and instance-dependent regimes, and for multi-armed bandits with A arms and horizon T, the distributional regret bound is O(√(AT) log(1/δ)), confirming a conjecture by Lattimore & Szepesvári for the first time.
本文提出了一个统一框架，用于研究随机多臂老虎机和情节强化学习中遗憾的分布，其动机是需要一种在所有置信水平上均匀成立的概率保证。该方法引入了一种UCBVI风格的算法，其探索奖励形式为min{c1,k/N, c2,k/√N}，其中N是访问次数，(c1,k, c2,k)是用户指定参数，并推导出通用的与间隙无关和与间隙相关的分布遗憾界，刻画了期望性能、尾部风险和实例依赖行为之间的权衡。主要实验结果表明，这些界在极小极大和实例依赖两种场景下均达到了最优权衡，对于具有A个臂和T时间步的多臂老虎机，分布遗憾界为O(√(AT) log(1/δ))，首次证实了Lattimore和Szepesvári的猜想。
LLMs learn scientific taste from institutional traces across the social sciences
Authors: Ziqin Gong, Ning Li, Huaikang Zhou
First: 2026-03-17T15:28:24+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-06T16:07:43+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement-learned reasoning has powered recent AI leaps on verifiable tasks, including mathematics, code, and structure prediction. The harder bottleneck is evaluative judgment in low-verifiability domains, where no oracle anchors reward and the core question is which untested ideas deserve attention. We test whether institutional traces, the record of what fields published, where, and at which tier, can serve as a training signal for AI evaluators. Across eight social science disciplines (psychology, economics, communication, sociology, political science, management, business and finance, public administration), we built held-out four-tier research-pitch benchmarks and supervised-fine-tuned (SFT) LLMs on field-specific publication outcomes. The fine-tuned models cleared the 25 percent chance baseline and exceeded frontier-model performance by wide margins, with best single-model accuracy ranging from 55.0 percent in public administration to 85.5 percent in psychology. In management, evaluated against 48 expert gatekeepers, 174 junior researchers, and 11 frontier reasoning models, the best single fine-tuned model (Qwen3-4B) reached 59.2 percent, 17.6 percentage points above expert majority vote (41.6 percent, non-tied) and 28.1 percentage points above the frontier mean (31.1 percent). The fine-tuned models also showed calibrated confidence: confidence rose when predictions were correct and fell when wrong, mirroring how a skilled reviewer can say "I'm sure" versus "I'm guessing." Selective triage on this signal reached very high accuracy on the highest-confidence subsets in every field. Institutional traces, we conclude, encode a scalable training signal for the low-verifiability judgment on which science depends.
Summary / 总结
The paper investigates whether institutional traces—records of where and at what tier research is published—can train AI evaluators for low-verifiability scientific judgment, a bottleneck in reinforcement-learned reasoning. The authors fine-tuned LLMs on publication outcomes across eight social science disciplines, using held-out four-tier research-pitch benchmarks. Results show fine-tuned models surpassed the 25% chance baseline and frontier models by wide margins, with accuracy ranging from 55.0% in public administration to 85.5% in psychology; in management, the best model achieved 59.2% accuracy, outperforming expert majority vote by 17.6 percentage points and frontier models by 28.1 points, while also demonstrating calibrated confidence.
该论文研究是否可以利用制度痕迹（即研究发表的地点与层级记录）来训练AI评估者，以解决低可验证性科学判断这一强化学习推理的瓶颈。作者在八个社会科学学科中，基于发表结果对大型语言模型进行微调，并使用留出的四层级研究提案基准进行测试。结果显示，微调模型显著超越了25%的随机基线，并以大幅优势领先前沿模型，准确率从公共行政学的55.0%到心理学的85.5%不等；在管理学中，最佳模型达到59.2%的准确率，比专家多数投票高出17.6个百分点，比前沿模型均值高出28.1个百分点，同时展现出校准后的置信度。
Malliavin Calculus for Counterfactual Gradient Estimation in Adaptive Inverse Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Vikram Krishnamurthy, Luke Snow
First: 2026-04-01T19:56:02+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-06T16:05:17+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Inverse reinforcement learning (IRL) recovers the loss function of a forward learner from its observed responses. Adaptive IRL aims to reconstruct the loss function of a forward learner by passively observing its gradients as it performs reinforcement learning (RL). This paper proposes a novel passive Langevin-based algorithm that achieves adaptive IRL. The key difficulty in adaptive IRL is that the required gradients in the passive algorithm are counterfactual, that is, they are conditioned on events of probability zero under the forward learner's trajectory. Therefore, naive Monte Carlo estimators are prohibitively inefficient, and kernel smoothing, though common, suffers from slow convergence. We overcome this by employing Malliavin calculus to efficiently estimate the required counterfactual gradients. We reformulate the counterfactual conditioning as a ratio of unconditioned expectations involving Malliavin quantities, thus recovering standard estimation rates. We derive the necessary Malliavin derivatives and their adjoint Skorohod integral formulations for a general Langevin structure, and provide a concrete algorithmic approach which exploits these for counterfactual gradient estimation.
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of adaptive inverse reinforcement learning (IRL), where the goal is to recover a forward learner's loss function by passively observing its gradients during reinforcement learning. The authors propose a novel passive Langevin-based algorithm, but the key difficulty lies in estimating counterfactual gradients conditioned on zero-probability events, which makes naive Monte Carlo estimators inefficient and kernel smoothing slow. To overcome this, they employ Malliavin calculus to reformulate the counterfactual conditioning as a ratio of unconditioned expectations, enabling standard estimation rates. The method derives necessary Malliavin derivatives and Skorohod integral formulations for a general Langevin structure, providing a concrete algorithmic approach for efficient counterfactual gradient estimation, though specific experimental results are not detailed in the abstract.
本文针对自适应逆强化学习（IRL）中的挑战，即通过被动观察前向学习者在强化学习过程中的梯度来重建其损失函数。作者提出了一种新颖的基于朗之万动力学的被动算法，但关键难点在于估计条件于零概率事件的反事实梯度，这使得朴素蒙特卡洛估计器效率极低，而核平滑方法收敛缓慢。为解决这一问题，他们利用马利亚万微积分将反事实条件重新表述为涉及马利亚万量的无条件期望之比，从而恢复标准估计速率。该方法推导了一般朗之万结构所需的马利亚万导数及其伴随斯科罗霍德积分形式，并提供了一种具体的算法实现用于高效反事实梯度估计，但摘要中未详细说明具体实验结果。
Efficiency of Parallel and Restart Exploration Strategies in Model Free Stochastic Simulations
Authors: Ernesto Garcia, Paola Bermolen, Matthieu Jonckheere, Seva Shneer
First: 2025-03-05T14:53:32+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-06T15:47:02+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We analyze the efficiency of parallelization and restart mechanisms for stochastic simulations in model-free settings, where the underlying system dynamics are unknown. Such settings are common in Reinforcement Learning (RL) and rare event estimation, where standard variance-reduction techniques like importance sampling are inapplicable. Focusing on the challenge of reaching rare states under a finite computational budget, we model exploration via random walks and Lévy processes. Based on rigorous probability analysis, our work reveals a phase transition in the success probability as a function of the number of parallel simulations: an optimal number $N^*$ exists, balancing exploration diversity and time allocation per simulation. Beyond this threshold, performance degrades exponentially. Furthermore, we demonstrate that a restart strategy, which reallocates resources from stagnant trajectories to promising regions, can yield an exponential improvement in success probability. In the context of RL, these strategies can improve policy gradient methods by enabling more efficient state-space exploration, leading to more accurate policy gradient estimates.
中文标题/摘要
标题：无模型随机模拟中并行与重启探索策略的效率分析
我们分析了在无模型设置下（即底层系统动力学未知时）随机模拟中并行化和重启机制的效率。此类设置常见于强化学习和稀有事件估计，其中重要性采样等标准方差缩减技术无法适用。聚焦于有限计算预算下到达稀有状态的挑战，我们通过随机游走和莱维过程对探索进行建模。基于严格的概率分析，我们的工作揭示了成功概率随并行模拟数量变化的相变现象：存在最优数量N*，平衡探索多样性与每次模拟的时间分配。超过此阈值后，性能呈指数级下降。此外，我们证明了一种重启策略——将资源从停滞轨迹重新分配到有希望的区域——能够使成功概率获得指数级提升。在强化学习背景下，这些策略可通过实现更高效的状态空间探索来改进策略梯度方法，从而获得更精确的策略梯度估计。
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates the efficiency of parallel and restart exploration strategies in model-free stochastic simulations, motivated by the challenge of reaching rare states under a finite computational budget in settings like reinforcement learning where standard variance-reduction techniques are inapplicable. The authors model exploration using random walks and Lévy processes and apply rigorous probability analysis to reveal a phase transition in success probability as a function of the number of parallel simulations, identifying an optimal number N* that balances exploration diversity and time allocation, beyond which performance degrades exponentially. Additionally, they demonstrate that a restart strategy, which reallocates resources from stagnant trajectories to promising regions, yields an exponential improvement in success probability, and in reinforcement learning, these strategies enhance policy gradient methods by enabling more efficient state-space exploration and more accurate gradient estimates.
本文研究了无模型随机模拟中并行和重启探索策略的效率，其动机是在有限计算预算下到达稀有状态的挑战，这在强化学习等标准方差缩减技术不适用的场景中尤为突出。作者使用随机游走和莱维过程对探索进行建模，并通过严格的概率分析揭示了成功概率随并行模拟数量变化的相变现象，找到了一个平衡探索多样性和每个模拟时间分配的最优数量N*，超过该阈值后性能呈指数级下降。此外，他们证明了一种将资源从停滞轨迹重新分配到有希望区域的重启策略，能够使成功概率获得指数级提升，在强化学习中，这些策略通过实现更高效的状态空间探索和更准确的策略梯度估计来改进策略梯度方法。
Preference-Based Self-Distillation: Beyond KL Matching via Reward Regularization
Authors: Xin Yu, Liuchen Liao, Yiwen Zhang, Yingchen Yu, Lingzhou Xue, Qinzhen Guo
First: 2026-05-06T15:31:50+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-06T15:31:50+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
On-policy distillation is an efficient alternative to reinforcement learning, offering dense token-level training signals. However, its reliance on a stronger external teacher has driven recent work on on-policy self-distillation, where the same model serves as both teacher and student under different prompt contexts. Yet, existing self-distillation methods largely reduce learning to KL matching toward the context-augmented teacher model. This approach often suffers from training instability and can degrade reasoning performance over time. Moreover, self-distillation from the same model with prompt augmentation lacks the exploratory diversity provided by a genuine external teacher. To address these limitations, we move beyond fixed-teacher KL matching and propose \textbf{P}reference-\textbf{B}ased \textbf{S}elf-\textbf{D}istillation (\textbf{PBSD}), which revisits on-policy self-distillation through a reward-regularized perspective. Instead of directly matching the teacher distribution, we derive a reward-regularized objective whose analytic optimum is a reward-reweighted teacher distribution, yielding a target policy provably superior to the original teacher under this objective. Practically, PBSD optimizes preference gaps between teacher and student samples while maintaining on-policy student sampling. We support this framework with a statistical analysis of the induced preference-learning problem, formally establishing when on policy self-distillation is preferable to learning from an external teacher in our setting. Experiments on mathematical reasoning and tool-use benchmarks across multiple model scales demonstrate that PBSD consistently achieves the strongest average performance among comparable baselines, showing improved training stability over prior self-distillation baselines while preserving token efficiency.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于偏好的自蒸馏：通过奖励正则化超越KL匹配
在策略蒸馏是强化学习的一种高效替代方案，能提供密集的令牌级训练信号。然而，其对更强外部教师的依赖推动了近期在策略自蒸馏的研究，其中同一模型在不同提示上下文中同时充当教师和学生。但现有自蒸馏方法大多将学习简化为对上下文增强教师模型的KL匹配。这种方法常面临训练不稳定，并可能随时间推移降低推理性能。此外，通过提示增强从同一模型进行自蒸馏缺乏真正外部教师提供的探索多样性。为解决这些局限，我们超越固定教师KL匹配，提出基于偏好的自蒸馏（PBSD），从奖励正则化视角重新审视在策略自蒸馏。我们不直接匹配教师分布，而是推导出一个奖励正则化目标，其解析最优解是奖励重新加权的教师分布，在该目标下产生一个理论上优于原始教师的策略。实践中，PBSD优化教师和学生样本之间的偏好差距，同时保持学生样本的在策略采样。我们通过诱导偏好学习问题的统计分析支持该框架，正式确立了在策略自蒸馏何时优于从外部教师学习。在多个模型规模的数学推理和工具使用基准上的实验表明，PBSD在可比基线中持续实现最强平均性能，相比先前自蒸馏基线展现出更好的训练稳定性，同时保持令牌效率。

The paper addresses the limitations of existing on-policy self-distillation methods, which rely on KL matching to a context-augmented teacher and suffer from training instability and degraded reasoning performance. The authors propose Preference-Based Self-Distillation (PBSD), which reformulates self-distillation as a reward-regularized optimization problem, deriving a target policy that is a reward-reweighted teacher distribution provably superior to the original teacher. Experiments on mathematical reasoning and tool-use benchmarks across multiple model scales show that PBSD consistently achieves the strongest average performance among comparable baselines, with improved training stability and token efficiency.
该论文针对现有在线自蒸馏方法依赖KL匹配到上下文增强教师模型，导致训练不稳定和推理性能下降的问题，提出了基于偏好的自蒸馏方法（PBSD）。该方法将自蒸馏重新定义为奖励正则化优化问题，推导出奖励重加权教师分布的目标策略，理论上优于原始教师。在数学推理和工具使用基准上的多尺度模型实验表明，PBSD在可比基线中持续取得最强平均性能，同时提升了训练稳定性和令牌效率。
Graph-SND: Sparse Aggregation for Behavioral Diversity in Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Shawn Ray
First: 2026-05-06T15:18:42+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-06T15:18:42+00:00
Comments: 22 pages, 12 figures, 7 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
System Neural Diversity (SND) measures behavioral heterogeneity in multi-agent reinforcement learning by averaging pairwise distances over all $\binom{n}{2}$ agent pairs, making each call quadratic in team size. We introduce Graph-SND, which replaces this complete-graph average with a weighted average over the edges of an arbitrary graph $G$. Three regimes follow: $G=K_n$ recovers SND exactly; a fixed sparse $G$ defines a localized diversity measure at $O(|E|)$ cost; and random edge samples yield an unbiased Horvitz-Thompson estimator and a normalized sample mean with $O(1/\sqrt{m})$ concentration in the sampled edge count $m$. For fixed sparse graphs we prove forwarding-index distortion bounds for expanders and a spectral refinement under low-rank distance structure; for random $d$-regular graphs we prove an unconditional probabilistic $\widetilde{\mathcal{O}}(D_{\max}/\sqrt{n})$ bound. On VMAS we verify recovery, unbiasedness, concentration, and wall-clock scaling, with a PettingZoo TVD panel checking non-Gaussian transfer. In a 500-iteration $n=100$ PPO run, Bernoulli-$0.1$ Graph-SND tracks full SND while reducing per-call metric time by about $10\times$, and frozen-policy GPU timing up to $n=500$ follows the predicted $\binom{n}{2}/|E|$ speedup. Random $d$-regular expanders empirically achieve $\mathrm{SND}_{G}^{\mathrm{u}}/\mathrm{SND} \in [0.9987, 1.0013]$ at $Θ(n \log n)$ edges. In DiCo diversity control at $n=50$, Bernoulli-$0.1$ Graph-SND preserves set-point tracking with paired reward differences indistinguishable from zero across nine matched cells while cutting per-call metric cost by ${\sim}9.5\times$. Together, these results show that the SND aggregation bottleneck can be removed without changing the metric's semantics, yielding a drop-in sparse alternative that scales beyond complete-graph SND and supports both passive measurement and closed-loop diversity control.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Graph-SND：多智能体强化学习中行为多样性的稀疏聚合
系统神经多样性（SND）通过平均所有$\binom{n}{2}$个智能体对的成对距离来衡量多智能体强化学习中的行为异质性，每次调用复杂度与团队规模呈二次关系。我们提出Graph-SND，用任意图$G$的边上的加权平均替代这种完全图平均。由此产生三种情况：$G=K_n$精确恢复SND；固定稀疏$G$以$O(|E|)$代价定义局部多样性度量；随机边采样产生无偏的Horvitz-Thompson估计量和归一化样本均值，在采样边数$m$上具有$O(1/\sqrt{m})$的集中性。对于固定稀疏图，我们证明了扩展图的转发指数失真界和低秩距离结构下的谱改进；对于随机$d$-正则图，我们证明了无条件的概率性$\widetilde{\mathcal{O}}(D_{\max}/\sqrt{n})$界。在VMAS上，我们验证了恢复性、无偏性、集中性和挂钟时间缩放，并通过PettingZoo TVD面板检查非高斯迁移。在500次迭代的$n=100$ PPO运行中，伯努利-0.1 Graph-SND跟踪完整SND，同时将每次调用的度量时间减少约10倍，冻结策略GPU计时在$n=500$时遵循预测的$\binom{n}{2}/|E|$加速比。随机$d$-正则扩展图在$Θ(n \log n)$条边下经验性地达到$\mathrm{SND}_{G}^{\mathrm{u}}/\mathrm{SND} \in [0.9987, 1.0013]$。在$n=50$的DiCo多样性控制中，伯努利-0.1 Graph-SND保持设定点跟踪，九个匹配单元中配对奖励差异与零无显著差异，同时将每次调用的度量成本降低约9.5倍。这些结果共同表明，SND聚合瓶颈可以在不改变度量语义的情况下被消除，产生一种超越完全图SND的可扩展稀疏替代方案，并支持被动测量和闭环多样性控制。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces Graph-SND, a method to reduce the quadratic computational cost of System Neural Diversity (SND) in multi-agent reinforcement learning by replacing the complete-graph average of pairwise agent distances with a weighted average over an arbitrary graph. The method supports three regimes: exact recovery with a complete graph, localized diversity with a fixed sparse graph at O(|E|) cost, and unbiased estimation via random edge sampling with concentration guarantees. Experiments on VMAS and PettingZoo show that Bernoulli-0.1 Graph-SND tracks full SND closely, achieving a 10x speedup in per-call metric time for n=100 PPO runs and up to a 9.5x reduction in cost for DiCo diversity control at n=50, while maintaining set-point tracking and unbiasedness.
该论文提出了Graph-SND方法，通过将多智能体强化学习中系统神经多样性（SND）的完全图平均替换为任意图上的加权平均，来降低其二次计算成本。该方法支持三种模式：完全图精确恢复、固定稀疏图的局部多样性（O(|E|)成本）以及随机边采样的无偏估计（具有浓度保证）。在VMAS和PettingZoo上的实验表明，Bernoulli-0.1 Graph-SND紧密跟踪完整SND，在n=100的PPO运行中实现了每调用度量时间约10倍的加速，并在n=50的DiCo多样性控制中将每调用度量成本降低约9.5倍，同时保持设定点跟踪和无偏性。
A Policy-Driven DRL Framework for System-Level Tradeoff Control in NR-U/Wi-Fi Coexistence
Authors: Po-Heng Chou, Yi-Fang Yu, Shou-Yu Chen, Chiapin Wang
First: 2026-05-01T06:43:09+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-06T14:52:21+00:00
Comments: 13 pages, 13 figures, 1 table, submitted to IEEE Open Journal of Vehicular Technology
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The coexistence of NR-U and Wi-Fi in unlicensed spectrum introduces a system-level resource coordination problem, where heterogeneous channel access mechanisms lead to a significant imbalance in spectrum utilization and degraded Wi-Fi performance. To address this challenge, we propose a policy-driven deep reinforcement learning (DRL) framework for adaptive TXOP control, in which the coexistence process is formulated as a Markov decision process (MDP) and a deep Q-network (DQN) learns control policies through online interaction. A key contribution is the introduction of a policy layer via reward design, enabling explicit control of system-level tradeoffs among fairness, throughput, and quality of service (QoS). Three policies, namely absolute fairness, moderate fairness, and utility-based fairness, are developed to achieve different operating points. Simulation results show that the proposed framework achieves a Jain fairness index above 0.9 under strict fairness control. Compared to absolute fairness, moderate fairness improves aggregate throughput by 68.22%, while the utility-based policy further enhances utility by 177.6%. These results demonstrate that policy-driven control provides a flexible and effective solution for managing tradeoffs in heterogeneous coexistence networks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：一种策略驱动的深度强化学习框架：NR-U与Wi-Fi共存中的系统级权衡控制
NR-U与Wi-Fi在非授权频谱上的共存引发了系统级资源协调问题，异构信道接入机制导致频谱利用严重失衡并降低Wi-Fi性能。为应对这一挑战，我们提出了一种策略驱动的深度强化学习（DRL）框架用于自适应TXOP控制，将共存过程建模为马尔可夫决策过程（MDP），并通过深度Q网络（DQN）在线交互学习控制策略。关键贡献在于通过奖励设计引入策略层，实现对公平性、吞吐量和服务质量（QoS）之间系统级权衡的显式控制。开发了绝对公平、适度公平和基于效用的公平三种策略，以实现不同工作点。仿真结果表明，在严格公平控制下，所提框架的Jain公平指数超过0.9。与绝对公平相比，适度公平将总吞吐量提升68.22%，而基于效用的策略进一步将效用提升177.6%。这些结果证明，策略驱动控制为管理异构共存网络中的权衡提供了灵活有效的解决方案。

This paper addresses the system-level resource coordination problem in NR-U and Wi-Fi coexistence, where heterogeneous channel access mechanisms cause spectrum imbalance and Wi-Fi degradation. Adaptive Ensemble Aggregation for Actor-Critics
Authors: Nicklas Werge, Yi-Shan Wu, Manuel Haussmann, Bahareh Tasdighi, Melih Kandemir
First: 2025-07-31T12:40:50+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-06T14:50:11+00:00
Comments: updated theory; experiments; author list
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Ensembles are ubiquitous in off-policy actor-critic learning, yet their efficacy depends critically on how they are aggregated. Current methods typically rely on static rules or task-specific hyperparameters to balance overestimation bias and variance, leaving the challenge of a truly adaptive approach open. We introduce Adaptive Ensemble Aggregation (AEA), an algorithm that dynamically constructs ensemble-based targets for both critic and actor updates directly from training dynamics. We prove that AEA converges to a unique equilibrium where the aggregation parameter minimizes value estimation error within a defined stability region. Theoretically, we establish that AEA achieves a shrinkage property where the estimation bias vanishes as the total ensemble size grows. Unlike subset-based methods like REDQ, which hit an information bottleneck determined by a fixed variance floor regardless of the ensemble size, AEA exploits the full ensemble to achieve optimal variance reduction-scaling inversely with the total number of models-and maximal Fisher information. Furthermore, we provide a formal guarantee for monotonic policy improvement under this adaptive regime. Extensive evaluations on various continuous control tasks demonstrate that AEA outperforms, on the majority of tasks, state-of-the-art baselines, providing a robust and self-calibrating framework for ensemble-based reinforcement learning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：自适应集成聚合用于演员-评论家算法
集成方法在离策略演员-评论家学习中无处不在，但其有效性关键取决于聚合方式。当前方法通常依赖静态规则或任务特定的超参数来平衡过估计偏差和方差，真正的自适应方法仍是一个开放挑战。我们提出自适应集成聚合（AEA），该算法直接从训练动态中为评论家和演员更新动态构建基于集成的目标。我们证明AEA收敛到一个唯一均衡点，在该点聚合参数在定义的稳定区域内最小化价值估计误差。理论上，我们确立AEA具有收缩性质，即随着总集成规模增长，估计偏差消失。与REDQ等基于子集的方法不同（这些方法受固定方差下限决定的信息瓶颈限制，无论集成规模如何），AEA利用整个集成实现最优方差缩减——与模型总数成反比——并最大化Fisher信息。此外，我们提供了在此自适应机制下单调策略改进的形式化保证。在各种连续控制任务上的广泛评估表明，AEA在大多数任务上优于最先进的基线方法，为基于集成的强化学习提供了一个稳健且自校准的框架。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of static aggregation rules in ensemble-based off-policy actor-critic methods, which often require task-specific hyperparameters to balance overestimation bias and variance. The authors propose Adaptive Ensemble Aggregation (AEA), a method that dynamically constructs ensemble targets for both critic and actor updates based on training dynamics, with theoretical guarantees of convergence to a unique equilibrium and monotonic policy improvement. Experiments on continuous control tasks show that AEA outperforms state-of-the-art baselines on most tasks, achieving optimal variance reduction that scales inversely with ensemble size, unlike subset-based methods like REDQ which suffer from a fixed variance floor.
该论文针对基于集成的离策略演员-评论家方法中静态聚合规则需要任务特定超参数来平衡过估计偏差和方差的挑战，提出了自适应集成聚合（AEA）算法。AEA根据训练动态动态构建评论家和演员更新的集成目标，并具有收敛到唯一均衡和单调策略改进的理论保证。在连续控制任务上的实验表明，AEA在大多数任务上优于最先进的基线方法，实现了与集成规模成反比的最优方差缩减，而像REDQ这样的基于子集的方法则受限于固定的方差下限。
EP-GRPO: Entropy-Progress Aligned Group Relative Policy Optimization with Implicit Process Guidance
Authors: Song Yu, Li Li, Wenwen Zhao, Zhisheng Yang
First: 2026-05-06T14:21:54+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-06T14:21:54+00:00
Comments: 15 pages, 6 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR), particularly Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO), has advanced LLM reasoning. However, GRPO suffers from three credit assignment failures: uniform token-level granularity that ignores heterogeneous informational value, uniform polarity that penalizes correct steps and rewards incorrect ones, and zero-variance collapse that erases outcome-driven gradients. We systematically quantify these failures, revealing highly non-uniform token informativeness, widespread step-level polarity misalignment, and substantial training waste. To address these limitations, we propose Entropy-Progress Aligned GRPO (EP-GRPO), a framework that mines the model's intrinsic information flow for dense, self-supervised guidance. EP-GRPO integrates entropy-gated modulation to prioritize high entropy decision pivots, implicit process signals from policy divergence anchored to outcome advantages for directional token-level feedback without external reward models, and cumulative entropy mapping that enables progress-aligned advantage normalization, naturally maintaining gradient flow under zero reward variance. Extensive experiments on mathematical reasoning benchmarks demonstrate that EP-GRPO achieves superior accuracy and efficiency compared to GRPO and its variants. The code will be available.
中文标题/摘要
标题：EP-GRPO：基于熵进展对齐的隐式过程引导组相对策略优化
基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR），特别是组相对策略优化（GRPO），推动了大型语言模型推理能力的发展。然而，GRPO存在三种信用分配失败：统一的词元级粒度忽略了异构信息价值；统一的极性会惩罚正确步骤并奖励错误步骤；零方差崩溃会消除结果驱动的梯度。我们系统量化了这些失败，揭示了高度非均匀的词元信息量、广泛的步骤级极性错位以及大量的训练浪费。 为解决这些局限，我们提出熵进展对齐GRPO（EP-GRPO），该框架挖掘模型内在信息流以提供密集的自监督引导。EP-GRPO集成了熵门控调制以优先处理高熵决策关键点；基于策略分歧的隐式过程信号锚定于结果优势，提供方向性词元级反馈而无需外部奖励模型；以及累积熵映射实现进展对齐的优势归一化，在零奖励方差下自然维持梯度流。 在数学推理基准上的大量实验表明，与GRPO及其变体相比，EP-GRPO实现了更优的准确性和效率。代码将公开。

The paper identifies three credit assignment failures in Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) for LLM reasoning: uniform token-level granularity, uniform polarity, and zero-variance collapse. To address these, the authors propose Entropy-Progress Aligned GRPO (EP-GRPO), which uses entropy-gated modulation to focus on high-entropy decision points, implicit process signals from policy divergence for token-level feedback, and cumulative entropy mapping for progress-aligned advantage normalization.
