该论文指出了GRPO在LLM推理中的三种信用分配失败：统一的token级粒度、统一的极性以及零方差崩溃。为解决这些问题，作者提出了EP-GRPO框架，通过熵门控调制聚焦高熵决策点、利用策略分歧的隐式过程信号提供token级反馈，以及累积熵映射实现进度对齐的优势归一化。在数学推理基准上的实验表明，EP-GRPO在准确性和效率上均优于GRPO及其变体。
On the Influence of the Feature Computation Budget on Per-Instance Algorithm Selection for Black-Box Optimization
Authors: Koen van der Blom, Diederick Vermetten
First: 2026-05-06T14:15:34+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-06T14:15:34+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Per-instance algorithm selection (PIAS) takes advantage of complementarity between a set of algorithms by deciding which algorithm to run on a given instance. This decision is based on features of the instances, which, in the context of black-box optimization (BBO), require a part of the optimization budget to be computed. This raises two questions: (a) from which fraction of the budget spent on feature computation does PIAS become worth it for BBO, and (b) which fraction of the budget optimizes the tradeoff between feature accuracy and PIAS performance. To this end, we perform a broad study where PIAS with varying sampling budgets for feature computation is compared to the single best algorithm on a broad range of algorithm selection scenarios. These scenarios consist of two portfolio sizes, three problem sets, 4 dimensionalities, and 10 target budgets. We find that PIAS is viable for the majority of tested scenarios, even when as much as a quarter of the total budget is spent on feature computation. The tradeoff for the fraction of the budget spent on feature computation to maximize the benefit of PIAS is highly dependent on the specific AS scenario. Further, on average 20 percent of PIAS loss to the virtual best solver is explained by the budget spent on feature computation, highlighting the importance of properly accounting for the feature budget.
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates the viability of per-instance algorithm selection (PIAS) for black-box optimization when feature computation consumes part of the optimization budget. The authors systematically compare PIAS using varying sampling budgets for feature extraction against the single best algorithm across diverse scenarios, including different portfolio sizes, problem sets, dimensionalities, and target budgets. The results show that PIAS remains beneficial in most cases even when up to a quarter of the total budget is spent on features, though the optimal fraction for maximizing PIAS gains varies significantly by scenario, and on average 20 percent of PIAS performance loss relative to the virtual best solver is attributable to the feature budget.
本文研究了在黑箱优化中，当特征计算消耗部分优化预算时，基于实例的算法选择（PIAS）的可行性。作者通过系统比较使用不同采样预算进行特征提取的PIAS与单一最优算法在多种场景（包括不同组合规模、问题集、维度和目标预算）下的表现。实验结果表明，即使将高达四分之一的预算用于特征计算，PIAS在大多数情况下仍然有效，但最大化PIAS收益的最佳预算比例因场景而异，且平均而言，PIAS相对于虚拟最优求解器的性能损失中有20%可归因于特征预算。
DVPO: Distributional Value Modeling-based Policy Optimization for LLM Post-Training
Authors: Dingwei Zhu, Zhiheng Xi, Shihan Dou, Yuhui Wang, Sixian Li, Junjie Ye, Honglin Guo, Shichun Liu, Chenhao Huang, Yajie Yang, Junlin Shang, Senjie Jin, Ming Zhang, Jiazheng Zhang, Caishuang Huang, Yunke Zhang, Yuran Wang, Tao Gui
First: 2025-12-03T14:48:38+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-06T14:15:19+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) has shown strong performance in LLM post-training, but real-world deployment often involves noisy or incomplete supervision. In such settings, complex and unreliable supervision signals can destabilize training and harm generalization. While existing approaches such as worst-case optimization (e.g., RFQI, CQL) and mean-based methods (e.g., PPO, GRPO) can improve stability, they often overlook generalization and may produce overly conservative policies, leading to uneven performance across diverse real scenarios. To this end, we introduce DVPO (Distributional Value Modeling with Risk-aware Policy Optimization), a new RL framework that combines conditional risk theory with distributional value modeling to better balance robustness and generalization. DVPO learns token-level value distributions to provide fine-grained supervision, and applies an asymmetric risk regularization to shape the distribution tails: it contracts the lower tail to dampen noisy negative deviations, while expanding the upper tail to preserve exploratory diversity. Across extensive experiments and analysis in multi-turn dialogue, math reasoning, and scientific QA, DVPO consistently outperforms PPO, GRPO, and robust Bellman-based PPO under noisy supervision, showing its potential for LLM post-training in the real-world.
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces DVPO, a reinforcement learning framework for LLM post-training that addresses the challenges of noisy or incomplete supervision signals which can destabilize training and harm generalization. DVPO combines conditional risk theory with distributional value modeling to learn token-level value distributions, applying an asymmetric risk regularization that contracts the lower tail to dampen noisy negative deviations while expanding the upper tail to preserve exploratory diversity. Extensive experiments in multi-turn dialogue, math reasoning, and scientific QA demonstrate that DVPO consistently outperforms PPO, GRPO, and robust Bellman-based PPO under noisy supervision, showing its potential for real-world LLM post-training.
该论文提出了DVPO框架，用于解决大语言模型后训练中因噪声或不完整监督信号导致的训练不稳定和泛化能力下降问题。DVPO结合条件风险理论与分布价值建模，学习词元级别的价值分布，并采用非对称风险正则化：收缩分布下尾以抑制噪声负偏差，同时扩展上尾以保持探索多样性。在多轮对话、数学推理和科学问答等广泛实验与分析中，DVPO在噪声监督下始终优于PPO、GRPO及基于鲁棒贝尔曼的PPO，展示了其在真实场景中大语言模型后训练的潜力。
Learning to Orchestrate Agents in Natural Language with the Conductor
Authors: Stefan Nielsen, Edoardo Cetin, Peter Schwendeman, Qi Sun, Jinglue Xu, Yujin Tang
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-12-04T02:23:13+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-06T14:06:21+00:00
Comments: To appear at the 14th International Conference on Learning Representations (ICLR 2026)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Powerful large language models (LLMs) from different providers have been expensively trained and finetuned to specialize across varying domains. In this work, we introduce a new kind of Conductor model trained with reinforcement learning to automatically discover powerful coordination strategies among LLMs. Our Conductor learns not only to design targeted communication topologies for effective agent-to-agent collaboration, but also to prompt engineer focused instructions to the LLMs to maximally leverage their individual capabilities. We show that, by learning optimal coordination strategies over pools of powerful worker LLMs, a 7B Conductor achieves significant performance gains beyond any individual worker, attaining state-of-the-art results in challenging reasoning benchmarks, such as LiveCodeBench and GPQA. By training with randomized agent pools, our conductor effectively adapts to arbitrary sets of open- and closed-source agents, meeting any user requirements. Furthermore, allowing the Conductor to select itself as a worker gives rise to recursive topologies, elevating performance with a new form of dynamic test-time scaling through online iterative adaptation. More broadly, ours is among the early work demonstrating language model coordination can be unlocked through RL, where powerful coordination strategies emerge naturally in LLMs through pure end-to-end reward maximization.
中文标题/摘要
标题：学习使用指挥者以自然语言编排智能体
来自不同提供商的强大大型语言模型（LLM）经过昂贵的训练和微调，专门针对不同领域。在这项工作中，我们引入了一种新型的指挥者模型，通过强化学习训练，自动发现LLM之间的强大协调策略。我们的指挥者不仅学会设计针对性的通信拓扑以实现有效的智能体间协作，还能对LLM进行提示工程，聚焦指令以最大化利用其各自能力。我们证明，通过学习在强大的工作LLM池上的最优协调策略，一个7B参数的指挥者实现了超越任何单个工作者的显著性能提升，在LiveCodeBench和GPQA等具有挑战性的推理基准测试中达到了最先进的结果。通过使用随机化的智能体池进行训练，我们的指挥者有效适应任意组合的开源和闭源智能体，满足任何用户需求。此外，允许指挥者选择自身作为工作者产生了递归拓扑，通过在线迭代适应实现了动态测试时缩放的新形式，从而提升了性能。更广泛地说，我们的工作是最早证明语言模型协调可以通过强化学习解锁的研究之一，其中强大的协调策略通过纯粹的端到端奖励最大化在LLM中自然涌现。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces the Conductor, a 7B language model trained with reinforcement learning to automatically orchestrate coordination among multiple large language models (LLMs). The method learns to design optimal communication topologies and prompt engineer targeted instructions for each worker LLM, enabling effective agent-to-agent collaboration. Experimental results show that the Conductor achieves state-of-the-art performance on challenging reasoning benchmarks like LiveCodeBench and GPQA, surpassing any individual worker, and adapts to arbitrary sets of open- and closed-source agents. Additionally, allowing the Conductor to select itself as a worker enables recursive topologies and dynamic test-time scaling, demonstrating that coordination strategies can emerge through pure end-to-end reward maximization.
该论文提出了Conductor模型，这是一个通过强化学习训练的7B参数语言模型，用于自动协调多个大型语言模型（LLM）之间的协作。该方法学习设计最优的通信拓扑结构，并为每个工作LLM生成针对性的提示工程指令，从而实现高效的智能体间协作。实验结果表明，Conductor在LiveCodeBench和GPQA等具有挑战性的推理基准测试中取得了最先进的性能，超越了任何单个工作模型，并能适应任意组合的开源和闭源智能体。此外，允许Conductor选择自身作为工作模型可形成递归拓扑结构，实现动态测试时扩展，证明了通过纯粹的端到端奖励最大化可以自然涌现出强大的协调策略。
Modular Reinforcement Learning For Cooperative Swarms
Authors: Erel Shtossel, Gal A. Kaminka
First: 2026-05-06T14:05:36+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-06T14:05:36+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
A cooperative robot swarm is a collective of computationally-limited robots that share a common goal. Each robot can only interact with a small subset of its peers, without knowing how this affects the collective utility. Recent advances in distributed multi-agent reinforcement learning have demonstrated that it is possible for robots to learn how to interact effectively with others, in a manner that is aligned with the common goal, despite each robot learning independently of others. However, this requires each robot to represent a potentially combinatorial number of interaction states, challenging the memory capabilities of the robots. This paper proposes an alternative approach for representing spatial interaction states for multi-robot reinforcement learning in swarms. A modular (decomposed) representation is used, where each feature of the state is handled by a separate learning procedure, and the results aggregated. We demonstrate the efficacy of the approach in numerous experiments with simulated robot swarms carrying out foraging.
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of cooperative robot swarms where computationally-limited robots must learn to interact effectively without centralized coordination, but face memory constraints due to combinatorial interaction states. The authors propose a modular reinforcement learning approach that decomposes spatial interaction states into separate features, each handled by an independent learning procedure, with results aggregated to guide collective behavior. Experiments in simulated foraging tasks demonstrate that this modular representation significantly reduces memory requirements while maintaining or improving swarm coordination performance compared to traditional methods.
该论文针对计算能力有限的协作机器人群体在缺乏中央协调时需学习有效交互的挑战，指出传统方法因交互状态组合爆炸而超出机器人内存限制。作者提出一种模块化强化学习方案，将空间交互状态分解为独立特征，每个特征由单独的学习过程处理并聚合结果以指导群体行为。在模拟觅食任务中的实验表明，这种模块化表示显著降低了内存需求，同时保持或提升了群体协调性能，优于传统方法。
DFPO: Scaling Value Modeling via Distributional Flow towards Robust and Generalizable LLM Post-Training
Authors: Dingwei Zhu, Zhiheng Xi, Shihan Dou, Jiahan Li, Chenhao Huang, Junjie Ye, Sixian Li, Mingxu Chai, Yuhui Wang, Yajie Yang, Ming Zhang, Jiazheng Zhang, Shichun Liu, Caishuang Huang, Yunke Zhang, Yuran Wang, Tao Gui, Xipeng Qiu, Qi Zhang, Xuanjing Huang
First: 2026-02-05T17:07:42+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-06T14:04:43+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Training reinforcement learning (RL) systems in real-world environments remains challenging due to noisy supervision and poor out-of-domain (OOD) generalization, especially in LLM post-training. Recent distributional RL methods improve robustness by modeling values with multiple quantile points, but they still learn each quantile independently as a scalar. This results in rough-grained value representations that lack fine-grained conditioning on state information, struggling under complex and OOD conditions. We propose DFPO (Distributional Value Flow Policy Optimization with Conditional Risk and Consistency Control), a robust distributional RL framework that models values as continuous flows across time steps. By scaling value modeling through learning of a value flow field instead of isolated quantile predictions, DFPO captures richer state information for more accurate advantage estimation. To stabilize training under noisy feedback, DFPO further integrates conditional risk control and consistency constraints along value flow trajectories. Experiments on dialogue, math reasoning, and scientific tasks show that DFPO outperforms PPO, FlowRL, and other robust baselines under noisy supervision, achieving improved training stability and generalization.
中文标题/摘要
标题：DFPO：通过分布流扩展价值建模以实现鲁棒且可泛化的LLM后训练
在真实环境中训练强化学习系统仍面临挑战，主要源于噪声监督和较差的域外泛化能力，尤其在LLM后训练中。近期分布强化学习方法通过多分位点建模价值提升了鲁棒性，但每个分位点仍被独立学习为标量，导致价值表示粗糙，缺乏对状态信息的细粒度条件化，在复杂和域外条件下表现不佳。我们提出DFPO（带条件风险与一致性控制的分布价值流策略优化），一种鲁棒的分布强化学习框架，将价值建模为跨时间步的连续流。通过学习价值流场而非孤立的分位点预测来扩展价值建模，DFPO捕获更丰富的状态信息以实现更精确的优势估计。为在噪声反馈下稳定训练，DFPO进一步沿价值流轨迹整合条件风险控制与一致性约束。在对话、数学推理和科学任务上的实验表明，DFPO在噪声监督下优于PPO、FlowRL及其他鲁棒基线，实现了更优的训练稳定性和泛化能力。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces DFPO, a distributional reinforcement learning framework designed to improve robustness and generalization in LLM post-training under noisy supervision. Existing distributional RL methods model values as independent scalar quantiles, leading to coarse value representations that fail under complex and out-of-domain conditions. DFPO addresses this by modeling values as continuous flows across time steps, learning a value flow field that captures richer state information for more accurate advantage estimation, and further integrates conditional risk control and consistency constraints to stabilize training. Experiments on dialogue, math reasoning, and scientific tasks demonstrate that DFPO outperforms PPO, FlowRL, and other robust baselines, achieving superior training stability and generalization.
该论文提出了DFPO，一种分布强化学习框架，旨在提升大语言模型后训练在噪声监督下的鲁棒性和泛化能力。现有分布强化学习方法将价值建模为独立标量分位数，导致价值表示粗糙，难以应对复杂和域外条件。DFPO通过将价值建模为时间步上的连续流，学习价值流场以捕获更丰富的状态信息，实现更准确的优势估计，并整合条件风险控制和一致性约束来稳定训练。在对话、数学推理和科学任务上的实验表明，DFPO优于PPO、FlowRL等鲁棒基线，实现了更好的训练稳定性和泛化性能。
Reinforcement Learning for Compositional Generalization with Outcome-Level Optimization
Authors: Xiyan Fu, Wei Liu
First: 2026-05-06T13:47:31+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-06T13:47:31+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Compositional generalization refers to correctly interpret novel combinations of known primitives, which remains a major challenge. Existing approaches often rely on supervised fine-tuning, which encourages models to imitate target outputs. This token-level training paradigm fails to capture the global compositional structure required for generalizing to unseen combinations. In this work, we investigate whether compositional generalization can instead be improved through outcome-level reinforcement learning. We adopt Group Relative Policy Optimization to optimize models based on feedback on their final outputs. Within this framework, we explore both a simple binary outcome reward and a composite reward that provides additional composition feedback. Experiments on multiple compositional benchmarks show that reinforcement learning improves compositional generalization compared to supervised fine-tuning. Further analysis reveals that supervised models tend to overfit frequent training compositions, whereas reinforcement learning improves compositional generalization by reshaping the output distribution, particularly for more complex composition types.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向组合泛化的结果级优化强化学习
组合泛化指正确理解已知基元的新颖组合，这仍是一项重大挑战。现有方法通常依赖监督微调，鼓励模型模仿目标输出。这种词元级训练范式无法捕捉泛化到未见组合所需的全局组合结构。本研究探讨能否通过结果级强化学习改进组合泛化。我们采用组相对策略优化，基于最终输出反馈优化模型。在此框架下，我们探索了简单的二元结果奖励和提供额外组合反馈的复合奖励。多个组合基准实验表明，与监督微调相比，强化学习提升了组合泛化能力。进一步分析显示，监督模型倾向于过拟合频繁出现的训练组合，而强化学习通过重塑输出分布（尤其是针对更复杂的组合类型）改进了组合泛化。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of compositional generalization, where models must correctly interpret novel combinations of known primitives. The authors propose using outcome-level reinforcement learning, specifically Group Relative Policy Optimization, instead of traditional supervised fine-tuning that focuses on token-level imitation. They explore both a simple binary reward and a composite reward with additional composition feedback. Experiments on multiple compositional benchmarks demonstrate that reinforcement learning improves compositional generalization over supervised fine-tuning, with analysis showing that supervised models overfit frequent compositions while reinforcement learning reshapes the output distribution to better handle complex types.
本文针对组合泛化这一挑战，即模型需正确解释已知基元的新组合，提出使用结果级强化学习（具体为组相对策略优化）替代传统的监督微调（后者侧重于词元级模仿）。作者探索了简单二元奖励和包含额外组合反馈的复合奖励。在多个组合基准上的实验表明，强化学习相比监督微调能提升组合泛化能力，分析显示监督模型会过拟合常见组合，而强化学习通过重塑输出分布更好地处理复杂组合类型。
Deep Learning in Astrophysics
Authors: Yuan-Sen Ting
Venue: Annual Review of Astronomy and Astrophysics, 2026, Vol. 64
First: 2025-10-12T17:31:46+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-06T13:37:18+00:00
Comments: Published in Annual Review of Astronomy and Astrophysics, Volume 64. This is the authors' version. The published version is available at https://doi.org/10.1146/annurev-astro-051024-021708
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Deep learning has generated diverse perspectives in astronomy, with ongoing discussions between proponents and skeptics motivating this review. We examine how neural networks complement classical statistics, extending our data analytical toolkit for modern surveys. Astronomy offers unique opportunities through encoding physical symmetries, conservation laws, and differential equations directly into architectures, creating models that generalize beyond training data. Yet challenges persist as unlabeled observations number in billions while confirmed examples with known properties remain scarce and expensive. This review demonstrates how deep learning incorporates domain knowledge through architectural design, with built-in assumptions guiding models toward physically meaningful solutions. We evaluate where these methods offer genuine advances versus claims requiring careful scrutiny. - Neural architectures overcome bias-variance trade-offs among scalability, expressivity, and data efficiency by encoding physical symmetries and conservation laws into network structure, enabling learning from limited labeled data. - Simulation-based inference and anomaly detection extract information from complex, non-Gaussian distributions where analytical likelihoods fail, enabling field-level cosmological analysis and systematic discovery of rare phenomena. - Multiscale neural modeling bridges resolution gaps in astronomical simulations, learning effective subgrid physics from expensive high-fidelity runs to enhance large-volume calculations where direct computation remains prohibitive. - Emerging paradigms-reinforcement learning for telescope operations, foundation models learning from minimal examples, and large language model agents for research automation-show promise though are still developing in astronomical applications.
中文标题/摘要
标题：天体物理学中的深度学习
深度学习在天文学中引发了多元视角，支持者与怀疑者之间的持续讨论推动了本综述的撰写。我们考察了神经网络如何补充经典统计学，为现代巡天扩展数据分析工具库。天文学通过将物理对称性、守恒定律和微分方程直接编码到架构中，提供了独特机遇，从而创建出能超越训练数据进行泛化的模型。然而，挑战依然存在：未标记观测数据数以十亿计，而已知属性的确认样本既稀少又昂贵。本综述展示了深度学习如何通过架构设计融入领域知识，其内置假设引导模型走向物理上有意义的解。我们评估了这些方法在哪些方面提供了真正的进步，而哪些主张需要仔细审视。 - 神经架构通过将物理对称性和守恒定律编码到网络结构中，克服了可扩展性、表达能力和数据效率之间的偏差-方差权衡，从而能够从有限的标记数据中学习。 - 基于模拟的推断和异常检测从解析似然函数失效的复杂非高斯分布中提取信息，实现了场级宇宙学分析和罕见现象的系统性发现。 - 多尺度神经建模弥合了天文模拟中的分辨率差距，从昂贵的高保真运行中学习有效的亚网格物理，以增强直接计算仍不可行的大体积计算。 - 新兴范式——用于望远镜操作的强化学习、从极少量示例中学习的基础模型，以及用于研究自动化的大型语言模型智能体——虽在天文学应用中仍在发展，但已展现出前景。
Summary / 总结
This review examines the integration of deep learning into astrophysics, motivated by ongoing debates between proponents and skeptics regarding its utility. The method focuses on how neural networks complement classical statistics by encoding physical symmetries, conservation laws, and differential equations directly into architectures, enabling models to generalize beyond training data despite the scarcity of labeled examples. Key experimental results demonstrate that such architectures overcome bias-variance trade-offs, simulation-based inference handles complex non-Gaussian distributions for field-level cosmological analysis, multiscale neural modeling bridges resolution gaps in simulations, and emerging paradigms like reinforcement learning and foundation models show promise for telescope operations and research automation.
本综述探讨了深度学习在天体物理学中的整合，其动机源于支持者与怀疑者之间关于其效用的持续辩论。方法侧重于神经网络如何通过将物理对称性、守恒定律和微分方程直接编码到架构中，来补充经典统计学，使模型能够在标记样本稀缺的情况下泛化到训练数据之外。主要实验结果表明，此类架构克服了偏差-方差权衡，基于模拟的推理处理复杂非高斯分布以进行场级宇宙学分析，多尺度神经建模弥合了模拟中的分辨率差距，而强化学习和基础模型等新兴范式在望远镜操作和研究自动化方面展现出前景。
Strat-Reasoner: Reinforcing Strategic Reasoning of LLMs in Multi-Agent Games
Authors: Yidong He, Yutao Lai, Pengxu Yang, Jiarui Gan, Jiexin Wang, Yi Cai, Mengchen Zhao
First: 2026-05-06T13:35:14+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-06T13:35:14+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
While Large Language Models (LLMs) excel in certain reasoning tasks, they struggle in multi-agent games where the final outcome depends on the joint strategies of all agents. In multi-agent games, the non-stationarity of other agents brings significant challenges on the evaluation of the reasoning process and the credit assignment over multiple reasoning steps. Existing single-agent reinforcement learning (RL) approaches and their multi-agent extensions fail to address these challenges as they do not incorporate other agents in the reasoning process. In this work, we propose Strat-Reasoner, a novel RL-based framework that improves LLMs' strategic reasoning ability in multi-agent games. We introduce a novel recursive reasoning paradigm where an agent's reasoning also integrates other agents' reasoning processes. To provide effective reward signals for the intermediate reasoning sequences, we employ a centralized Chain-of-Thought (CoT) comparison module to evaluate the reasoning quality. Finally, we compute an accurate hybrid advantage and develop a group-relative RL approach to optimize the LLM policy. Experimental results show that Strat-Reasoner substantially improves strategic abilities of underlying LLMs, achieving 22.1\% average performance improvements across various multi-agent games.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Strat-Reasoner：在多智能体博弈中强化大语言模型的战略推理能力
尽管大语言模型（LLM）在某些推理任务中表现出色，但在最终结果取决于所有智能体联合策略的多智能体博弈中，它们仍面临挑战。在多智能体博弈中，其他智能体的非平稳性给推理过程的评估和跨多步推理的信用分配带来了显著困难。现有的单智能体强化学习（RL）方法及其多智能体扩展未能解决这些挑战，因为它们未将其他智能体纳入推理过程。在本工作中，我们提出Strat-Reasoner，一种基于强化学习的新型框架，用于提升LLM在多智能体博弈中的战略推理能力。我们引入了一种新颖的递归推理范式，其中智能体的推理也整合了其他智能体的推理过程。为了为中间推理序列提供有效的奖励信号，我们采用集中式思维链（CoT）比较模块来评估推理质量。最后，我们计算精确的混合优势，并开发了一种群体相对强化学习方法以优化LLM策略。实验结果表明，Strat-Reasoner显著提升了底层LLM的战略能力，在各种多智能体博弈中实现了平均22.1%的性能提升。
Summary / 总结
Large language models (LLMs) struggle in multi-agent games due to the non-stationarity of other agents, which complicates reasoning evaluation and credit assignment. To address this, the authors propose Strat-Reasoner, a reinforcement learning framework that introduces a recursive reasoning paradigm, integrating other agents' reasoning into an agent's own process. A centralized Chain-of-Thought comparison module evaluates intermediate reasoning quality, and a group-relative RL approach optimizes the policy using hybrid advantage. Experiments show Strat-Reasoner improves strategic reasoning by 22.1% on average across various multi-agent games.
大型语言模型在多智能体游戏中表现不佳，因为其他智能体的非平稳性使推理评估和信用分配变得复杂。为此，作者提出Strat-Reasoner，一种强化学习框架，采用递归推理范式，将其他智能体的推理过程融入自身推理中。通过集中式思维链比较模块评估中间推理质量，并利用混合优势的群体相对强化学习方法优化策略。实验表明，Strat-Reasoner在多种多智能体游戏中的战略推理能力平均提升22.1%。
Delta-Based Neural Architecture Search: LLM Fine-Tuning via Code Diffs
Authors: Santosh Premi Adhikari, Radu Timofte, Dmitry Ignatov
First: 2026-05-06T13:32:05+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-06T13:32:05+00:00
Comments: 19 pages, 4 figures, 7 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) show strong potential for neural architecture generation, yet existing approaches produce complete model implementations from scratch -- computationally expensive and yielding verbose code. We propose Delta-Code Generation, where fine-tuned LLMs generate compact unified diffs (deltas) to refine baseline architectures rather than synthesizing entire models. Our pipeline iteratively fine-tunes the LLM via LoRA on curated architectures from the LEMUR dataset, with MinHash-Jaccard novelty filtering for structural diversity. We evaluate three 7B-class LLMs -- DeepSeek-Coder-7B, Qwen2.5-Coder-7B, and Mistral-7B -- across six datasets (CIFAR-10, CIFAR-100, MNIST, SVHN, ImageNette, CelebA) using a 22-cycle protocol (1,100 candidates per LLM). All three substantially surpass the full-generation baseline (50.6% valid rate, 42.3% mean first-epoch accuracy): DeepSeek-Coder reaches 75.3% valid rate and 65.8% mean accuracy; Qwen2.5-Coder 72.1%/64.6%; Mistral 66.6%/66.1%. On CIFAR-10, best first-epoch accuracies reach 85.5% (Mistral), 85.2% (DeepSeek), 80.6% (Qwen) -- well above 63.98% full generation and 71.5% for the concurrent approach of Gu et al. Output lengths are 30-50 lines versus 200+ for full generation (75-85% reduction). A 50-epoch study confirms the 1-epoch proxy preserves rankings (Mistral: Spearman $ρ$ = 0.926). Delta-based generation is a token-efficient, multi-domain, LLM-agnostic alternative to full-model synthesis for LLM-driven NAS.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于差异的神经架构搜索：通过代码差异微调大语言模型
大语言模型在神经架构生成方面展现出强大潜力，但现有方法从头生成完整模型实现——计算成本高且代码冗长。我们提出差异代码生成方法，通过微调大语言模型生成紧凑的统一差异（增量）来优化基线架构，而非合成完整模型。我们的流程利用LoRA在LEMUR数据集的精选架构上迭代微调大语言模型，并通过MinHash-Jaccard新颖性过滤确保结构多样性。我们评估了三款7B级大语言模型——DeepSeek-Coder-7B、Qwen2.5-Coder-7B和Mistral-7B——在六个数据集（CIFAR-10、CIFAR-100、MNIST、SVHN、ImageNette、CelebA）上采用22轮协议（每款大语言模型生成1100个候选）。三者均显著超越完整生成基线（50.6%有效率，42.3%平均第一轮准确率）：DeepSeek-Coder达到75.3%有效率和65.8%平均准确率；Qwen2.5-Coder为72.1%/64.6%；Mistral为66.6%/66.1%。在CIFAR-10上，最佳第一轮准确率达到85.5%（Mistral）、85.2%（DeepSeek）、80.6%（Qwen）——远高于完整生成的63.98%和Gu等人同期方法的71.5%。输出长度为30-50行，而完整生成超过200行（减少75-85%）。一项50轮研究证实，1轮代理保持排名（Mistral：斯皮尔曼ρ=0.926）。基于差异的生成是大语言模型驱动神经架构搜索中一种令牌高效、多领域、模型无关的完整模型合成替代方案。
Regime-Conditioned Evaluation in Multi-Context Bayesian Optimization
Authors: Noel Thomas
Venue: NeurIPS 2026
First: 2026-05-06T13:27:00+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-06T13:27:00+00:00
Comments: 42 pages, 9 figures. NeurIPS 2026 submission
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Published transfer-BO comparisons often estimate an average treatment effect of acquisition choice over hidden regime variables, while practitioners need the conditional effect for their specific prior quality, budget ratio, and metric. An audit of 40 transfer-BO papers from NeurIPS, ICML, ICLR, AISTATS, UAI, TMLR, JMLR, and AutoML-Conf (2022-2025) finds that 98% never vary B/|A| as a controlled axis. On the same GDSC2 benchmark, changing only the budget reverses the ranking: at B=50, Greedy outperforms UCB by 0.050 Hit@1, while at B=100, UCB outperforms Greedy by 0.035. We capture this transition with the Portable Regime Score PRS=(B/|A|)(1-rho), where rho is the prior rank correlation and can be estimated from pilot contexts before the main comparison. Across 79 conditions spanning chemistry, drug-response biology, and HPO, a hierarchical model gives beta=0.50 (p=1.1e-9), and 19% of conditions fall in an equivalence zone where |advantage|<0.01 Hit@1. In five published reversal cases, PRS predicts the winner from pre-comparison observables. A No-Free-Leaderboard proposition explains why unconditional rankings are unstable: when CATE changes sign across regimes, the reported ATE becomes a function of benchmark mixture. RegimePlanner, which estimates rho online and switches acquisition accordingly, wins all 16 HPO-B search spaces at B=100 and exceeds the matched {Greedy,UCB} per-context oracle on GDSC2 by 18%. Pre-registered predictions achieve 27/40=67.5% overall accuracy and above 90% within EMA prior families. The practical protocol is simple: report B/|A|, rho, K, and metric alongside any claimed acquisition advantage.
中文标题/摘要
标题：多上下文贝叶斯优化中的条件化评估
已发表的迁移贝叶斯优化比较通常估计采集函数选择对隐藏机制变量的平均处理效应，而实践者需要针对其特定先验质量、预算比率和指标的条件效应。对来自NeurIPS、ICML、ICLR、AISTATS、UAI、TMLR、JMLR和AutoML-Conf（2022-2025）的40篇迁移贝叶斯优化论文进行审计发现，98%从未将B/|A|作为受控轴进行变化。在相同的GDSC2基准上，仅改变预算就会逆转排名：在B=50时，Greedy比UCB高出0.050 Hit@1；而在B=100时，UCB比Greedy高出0.035。我们通过便携式机制评分PRS=(B/|A|)(1-rho)捕捉这一转变，其中rho是先验秩相关性，可在主要比较前从试点上下文中估计。在涵盖化学、药物反应生物学和HPO的79个条件下，层次模型给出beta=0.50（p=1.1e-9），19%的条件落在|优势|<0.01 Hit@1的等价区域。在五个已发表的逆转案例中，PRS从比较前可观测变量预测获胜者。无免费排行榜命题解释了无条件排名不稳定的原因：当CATE在不同机制间改变符号时，报告的ATE成为基准混合的函数。RegimePlanner在线估计rho并相应切换采集函数，在B=100时赢得所有16个HPO-B搜索空间，并在GDSC2上超过匹配的{Greedy,UCB}每上下文预言机18%。预注册预测达到27/40=67.5%的整体准确率，在EMA先验族内超过90%。实用协议很简单：报告B/|A|、rho、K和指标，同时声明任何采集优势。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the instability of transfer Bayesian optimization rankings due to hidden regime variables like prior quality and budget ratio. The authors propose the Portable Regime Score (PRS), defined as (B/|A|)(1-rho), to predict acquisition function performance based on budget B, search space size |A|, and prior rank correlation rho. In experiments across 79 conditions, a hierarchical model yields beta=0.50 (p=1.1e-9), with 19% of conditions showing negligible advantage. The RegimePlanner method, which estimates rho online and switches acquisition accordingly, wins all 16 HPO-B search spaces at B=100 and exceeds the matched oracle on GDSC2 by 18%. Pre-registered predictions achieve 67.5% overall accuracy and over 90% within EMA prior families.
本文针对迁移贝叶斯优化中因先验质量和预算比等隐藏机制变量导致的排名不稳定问题。作者提出了便携机制分数（PRS），定义为(B/|A|)(1-rho)，用于基于预算B、搜索空间大小|A|和先验秩相关系数rho预测采集函数性能。在涵盖79个条件的实验中，层次模型得到beta=0.50（p=1.1e-9），19%的条件处于优势可忽略的等价区域。RegimePlanner方法在线估计rho并切换采集函数，在B=100时赢得所有16个HPO-B搜索空间，并在GDSC2上超过匹配的oracle 18%。预注册预测达到67.5%总体准确率，在EMA先验族中超过90%。
ANO: A Principled Approach to Robust Policy Optimization
Authors: Yiheng Zhang, Yiming Wang, Kaiyan Zhao, Zhenglin Wan, Jiayu Chen, Leong Hou U
First: 2026-05-04T08:15:52+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-06T13:24:45+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO) dominates reinforcement learning and LLM alignment but relies on a "hard clipping" mechanism that discards valuable gradients. Conversely, unconstrained methods like SPO expose the optimization to unbounded updates, causing severe instability and policy collapse during extreme outlier encounters. To resolve this dilemma, we introduce a principled design space for policy optimization, demonstrating that a robust estimator must inherently suppress outliers while maintaining a smooth restoration force. Guided by these geometric principles, we derive Anchored Neighborhood Optimization (ANO), a novel method that seamlessly replaces hard clipping with a redescending gradient mechanism. Extensive evaluations demonstrate ANO's empirical superiority across diverse domains. In continuous (MuJoCo) and discrete (Atari) control, ANO establishes a robust state-of-the-art, uniquely preventing policy collapse even under highly aggressive learning rates ($1 \times 10^{-3}$). Furthermore, in LLM alignment (RLHF), ANO explicitly eliminates the catastrophic KL divergence explosion inherent to unconstrained methods, dominating PPO, SPO, and GRPO in head-to-head win rates.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ANO：一种稳健策略优化的原则性方法
近端策略优化（PPO）在强化学习和大型语言模型对齐中占据主导地位，但其依赖的“硬裁剪”机制会丢弃有价值的梯度。相反，像SPO这样的无约束方法会使优化面临无界更新，在极端异常值遭遇时导致严重不稳定和策略崩溃。为解决这一困境，我们引入了一个原则性的策略优化设计空间，证明稳健估计器必须内在抑制异常值，同时保持平滑的恢复力。在这些几何原理的指导下，我们推导出锚定邻域优化（ANO），这是一种新颖的方法，用再下降梯度机制无缝替代硬裁剪。广泛评估表明ANO在多个领域具有经验优越性。在连续（MuJoCo）和离散（Atari）控制中，ANO建立了稳健的最新技术水平，即使在高度激进的学习率（$1 \times 10^{-3}$）下也能独特地防止策略崩溃。此外，在LLM对齐（RLHF）中，ANO明确消除了无约束方法固有的灾难性KL散度爆炸，在直接对比胜率上优于PPO、SPO和GRPO。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the dilemma in policy optimization where Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO) discards valuable gradients due to hard clipping, while unconstrained methods like SPO cause instability and policy collapse from unbounded updates. The authors propose a principled design space for robust policy optimization, deriving Anchored Neighborhood Optimization (ANO) which replaces hard clipping with a redescending gradient mechanism that suppresses outliers while maintaining smooth restoration. Extensive experiments show ANO achieves state-of-the-art performance in continuous (MuJoCo) and discrete (Atari) control, uniquely preventing policy collapse even at aggressive learning rates of 1e-3, and in LLM alignment (RLHF), it eliminates KL divergence explosion and dominates PPO, SPO, and GRPO in win rates.
该论文针对策略优化中的困境，即近端策略优化（PPO）因硬裁剪机制丢弃有价值梯度，而SPO等无约束方法因无界更新导致不稳定和策略崩溃。作者提出了一种原则性的鲁棒策略优化设计空间，推导出锚定邻域优化（ANO），该方法用红下降梯度机制替代硬裁剪，在抑制异常值的同时保持平滑恢复力。大量实验表明，ANO在连续控制（MuJoCo）和离散控制（Atari）中达到最先进性能，即使在1e-3的激进学习率下也能独特地防止策略崩溃；在LLM对齐（RLHF）中，它消除了无约束方法固有的KL散度爆炸，并在胜率上优于PPO、SPO和GRPO。
A Harmonic Mean Formulation of Average Reward Reinforcement Learning in SMDPs
Authors: Erel Shtossel, Alicia Vidler, Uri Shaham, Gal A. Kaminka
First: 2026-05-06T13:16:42+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-06T13:16:42+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recent research has revived and amplified interest in algorithms for undiscounted average reward reinforcement learning in infinite-horizon, non-episodic (continuing) tasks. Semi-Markov decision processes (SMDPs) are of particular interest. In SMDPs, discrete actions stochastically generate both rewards and durations, and the objective is to optimize the average reward rate. Existing algorithms approach this by optimizing the ratio of rewards to durations. However, when rewards and durations are non-stationary (in the infinite horizon), this can be incorrect. This paper presents a novel modified harmonic mean operator that correctly computes reward rates even under such conditions. This yields model-free learning algorithms that can work with SMDPs, while maintaining robustness to non-stationary reward and duration distributions over time. We prove theoretical properties of the modified harmonic mean operator, and empirically demonstrate its efficacy in comparison to existing algorithms.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SMDP中平均奖励强化学习的调和均值公式
近期研究重新激发并强化了对无限时域、非回合制（持续性）任务中无折扣平均奖励强化学习算法的兴趣。半马尔可夫决策过程（SMDP）尤为引人关注。在SMDP中，离散动作随机产生奖励和持续时间，目标是优化平均奖励率。现有算法通过优化奖励与持续时间的比率来逼近这一目标。然而，当奖励和持续时间在无限时域中非平稳时，这种方法可能不正确。本文提出一种新颖的修正调和均值算子，即使在非平稳条件下也能正确计算奖励率。这产生了适用于SMDP的无模型学习算法，同时保持对随时间变化的非平稳奖励和持续时间分布的鲁棒性。我们证明了修正调和均值算子的理论性质，并通过实验展示了其相较于现有算法的有效性。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of optimizing average reward rates in infinite-horizon, non-episodic Semi-Markov decision processes (SMDPs), where existing ratio-based algorithms fail under non-stationary reward and duration distributions. The authors propose a novel modified harmonic mean operator that correctly computes reward rates even in such conditions, enabling model-free learning algorithms robust to temporal non-stationarity. Theoretical properties of the operator are proven, and empirical results demonstrate its superior efficacy over existing algorithms in handling non-stationary environments.
本文针对无限时域、非回合制半马尔可夫决策过程（SMDP）中平均奖励率优化问题，指出现有基于比率的算法在奖励和持续时间非平稳时存在缺陷。作者提出一种新型修正调和平均算子，能在非平稳条件下正确计算奖励率，从而开发出对时间非平稳性具有鲁棒性的无模型学习算法。理论证明了该算子的性质，实验结果表明其在处理非平稳环境时优于现有算法。
Overcoming Environmental Meta-Stationarity in MARL via Adaptive Curriculum and Counterfactual Group Advantage
Authors: Weiqiang Jin, Yang Liu, Shixiang Tang, Jinhu Qi, Wentao Zhang, Junli Wang, Biao Zhao, Hongyang Du
First: 2025-06-09T08:38:18+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-06T13:16:33+00:00
Comments: 23 pages; 15figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) has reached competitive performance on cooperative tasks against scripted adversaries, yet most methods train agents at a single fixed difficulty throughout the entire run. We term this static-difficulty regime environmental meta-stationarity and show that it caps policy generalization and steers learning toward shallow local optima. To break this regime, we propose CL-MARL, a dynamic curriculum learning framework that adapts opponent strength online from win-rate signals, advancing or regressing the task as agents master it. Its scheduler, FlexDiff, fuses momentum-based trend estimation with sliding-window dual-curve monitoring of training and evaluation returns, yielding stable difficulty transitions without manual tuning. Because a moving curriculum amplifies non-stationarity and sparsifies global rewards, we introduce the Counterfactual Group Relative Policy Advantage (CGRPA), which extends GRPO-style group-relative optimization with counterfactual baselines to disentangle each agent's contribution under shifting team dynamics. On the StarCraft Multi-Agent Challenge (SMAC), CL-MARL attains a 40% mean win rate on the super-hard maps with an average episode return of 17.85, exceeding the QMIX, OW-QMIX, DER, EMC, and MARR baselines by +2.94 on average, while reaching its peak win rate roughly 1.28faster on 8m_vs_9m and 1.42 faster on 3s5z_vs_3s6z than the strongest baseline. The implementation is publicly available at https://github.com/NICE-HKU/CL2MARL-SMAC.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过自适应课程与反事实群体优势克服多智能体强化学习中的环境元平稳性
多智能体强化学习在对抗脚本化对手的合作任务中已取得竞争性表现，但大多数方法在整个训练过程中以单一固定难度训练智能体。我们将这种静态难度机制称为环境元平稳性，并表明它会限制策略泛化能力，使学习偏向浅层局部最优。为打破该机制，我们提出CL-MARL，一种动态课程学习框架，通过胜率信号在线调整对手强度，在智能体掌握任务时推进或回退任务难度。其调度器FlexDiff融合基于动量的趋势估计与训练和评估回报的滑动窗口双曲线监控，无需手动调参即可实现稳定的难度过渡。由于移动课程会放大非平稳性并稀疏化全局奖励，我们引入反事实群体相对策略优势（CGRPA），将GRPO风格的群体相对优化扩展至反事实基线，以在动态团队动态下解耦每个智能体的贡献。在星际争霸多智能体挑战（SMAC）中，CL-MARL在超困难地图上达到40%的平均胜率，平均回合回报为17.85，比QMIX、OW-QMIX、DER、EMC和MARR基线平均高出+2.94，同时在8m_vs_9m地图上达到峰值胜率的速度比最强基线快约1.28倍，在3s5z_vs_3s6z地图上快1.42倍。实现代码已公开于https://github.com/NICE-HKU/CL2MARL-SMAC。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the problem of environmental meta-stationarity in multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL), where agents are trained at a fixed difficulty level, limiting policy generalization and leading to shallow local optima. To overcome this, the authors propose CL-MARL, a dynamic curriculum learning framework that adapts opponent strength online based on win-rate signals, using a scheduler called FlexDiff that combines momentum-based trend estimation with sliding-window dual-curve monitoring for stable difficulty transitions. Additionally, they introduce the Counterfactual Group Relative Policy Advantage (CGRPA) to handle non-stationarity and sparse global rewards by extending GRPO-style optimization with counterfactual baselines. On the StarCraft Multi-Agent Challenge (SMAC), CL-MARL achieves a 40% mean win rate on super-hard maps with an average episode return of 17.85, outperforming baselines like QMIX and OW-QMIX by +2.94 on average, and reaching peak win rates roughly 1.28x faster on 8m_vs_9m and 1.42x faster on 3s5z_vs_3s6z than the strongest baseline.
该论文针对多智能体强化学习中的环境元平稳性问题，即智能体在固定难度下训练导致策略泛化受限并陷入浅层局部最优。为此，作者提出CL-MARL动态课程学习框架，通过胜率信号在线调整对手强度，并设计FlexDiff调度器，结合动量趋势估计和滑动窗口双曲线监控实现稳定难度过渡。同时引入反事实群体相对策略优势（CGRPA），通过反事实基线扩展GRPO式群体相对优化，以应对非平稳性和稀疏全局奖励。在星际争霸多智能体挑战（SMAC）中，CL-MARL在超困难地图上达到40%平均胜率和17.85平均回合回报，平均超越QMIX、OW-QMIX等基线+2.94，并在8m_vs_9m和3s5z_vs_3s6z地图上分别以约1.28倍和1.42倍速度达到峰值胜率。
CAP: Controllable Alignment Prompting for Unlearning in LLMs
Authors: Zhaokun Wang, Jinyu Guo, Jingwen Pu, Hongli Pu, Meng Yang, Xunlei Chen, Jie Ou, Wenyi Li, Guangchun Luo, Wenhong Tian
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2026-04-23T03:42:41+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-06T12:16:51+00:00
Comments: Accpeted to ACL 2026 Main Conference
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) trained on unfiltered corpora inherently risk retaining sensitive information, necessitating selective knowledge unlearning for regulatory compliance and ethical safety. However, existing parameter-modifying methods face fundamental limitations: high computational costs, uncontrollable forgetting boundaries, and strict dependency on model weight access. These constraints render them impractical for closed-source models, yet current non-invasive alternatives remain unsystematic and reliant on empirical experience. To address these challenges, we propose the Controllable Alignment Prompting for Unlearning (CAP) framework, an end-to-end prompt-driven unlearning paradigm. CAP decouples unlearning into a learnable prompt optimization process via reinforcement learning, where a prompt generator collaborates with the LLM to suppress target knowledge while preserving general capabilities selectively. This approach enables reversible knowledge restoration through prompt revocation. Extensive experiments demonstrate that CAP achieves precise, controllable unlearning without updating model parameters, establishing a dynamic alignment mechanism that overcomes the transferability limitations of prior methods.
中文标题/摘要
标题：CAP：面向大语言模型遗忘的可控对齐提示方法
在未经过滤的语料上训练的大语言模型固有地存在保留敏感信息的风险，因此需要选择性知识遗忘以满足法规遵从和伦理安全要求。然而，现有的参数修改方法面临根本性局限：高计算成本、不可控的遗忘边界以及对模型权重访问的严格依赖。这些限制使得它们无法应用于闭源模型，而当前的非侵入式替代方案仍缺乏系统性且依赖经验。为解决这些挑战，我们提出了面向遗忘的可控对齐提示（CAP）框架，这是一种端到端的提示驱动遗忘范式。CAP通过强化学习将遗忘解耦为可学习的提示优化过程，其中提示生成器与大语言模型协作，在选择性抑制目标知识的同时保留通用能力。该方法通过撤销提示实现可逆的知识恢复。大量实验表明，CAP无需更新模型参数即可实现精确、可控的遗忘，建立了一种克服先前方法可迁移性局限的动态对齐机制。
Summary / 总结
Large language models trained on unfiltered data risk retaining sensitive information, but existing unlearning methods are computationally expensive, have uncontrollable forgetting boundaries, and require model weight access, making them unsuitable for closed-source models. To address this, the authors propose the Controllable Alignment Prompting for Unlearning (CAP) framework, which uses reinforcement learning to optimize a learnable prompt that suppresses target knowledge while preserving general capabilities, without modifying model parameters. Experiments show that CAP achieves precise and controllable unlearning, and allows reversible knowledge restoration through prompt revocation, overcoming the transferability limitations of prior methods.
大型语言模型在未经过滤的数据上训练可能保留敏感信息，但现有的遗忘方法计算成本高、遗忘边界不可控且依赖模型权重访问，不适用于闭源模型。为此，作者提出了可控对齐提示遗忘（CAP）框架，通过强化学习优化可学习提示，在抑制目标知识的同时保留通用能力，且无需修改模型参数。实验表明，CAP实现了精确可控的遗忘，并可通过撤销提示恢复知识，克服了先前方法的可迁移性限制。
Improving FMQA via Initial Training Data Design Considering Marginal Bit Coverage in One-Hot Encoding
Authors: Taiga Hayashi, Yuya Seki, Kotaro Terada, Yosuke Mukasa, Shuta Kikuchi, Shu Tanaka
First: 2026-05-06T12:16:34+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-06T12:16:34+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Factorization machine with quadratic-optimization annealing (FMQA) is a black-box optimization method that combines a factorization machine (FM) surrogate with QUBO-based search by an Ising machine. When FMQA is applied to integer or discretized continuous variables via one-hot encoding, uniform random initial sampling can leave many binary variables never active in the initial training data, and the corresponding FM parameters receive no direct gradient updates from the observed responses. We address this by designing the initial training data to achieve complete marginal bit coverage, namely, ensuring that every binary variable obtained by one-hot encoding takes the value one at least once. We use two space-filling sampling methods, Latin hypercube sampling (LHS) and the Sobol' sequence, yielding LHS-FMQA and Sobol'-FMQA. On the human-powered aircraft wing-shape optimization benchmark with 17 and 32 design variables, both proposed methods achieved numerically higher mean final cruising speeds than the baseline FMQA, with the advantage more pronounced on the 32-variable problem.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于独热编码中边际比特覆盖的初始训练数据设计改进FMQA
因子机与二次优化退火（FMQA）是一种结合因子机（FM）代理模型与基于伊辛机的QUBO搜索的黑箱优化方法。当FMQA通过独热编码应用于整数或离散连续变量时，均匀随机初始采样可能导致许多二元变量在初始训练数据中从未激活，相应的FM参数无法从观测响应中获得直接梯度更新。我们通过设计初始训练数据以实现完全边际比特覆盖来解决这一问题，即确保独热编码得到的每个二元变量至少取一次值1。我们采用两种空间填充采样方法：拉丁超立方采样（LHS）和Sobol'序列，分别得到LHS-FMQA和Sobol'-FMQA。在具有17个和32个设计变量的人力飞行器翼型优化基准测试中，两种提出的方法在数值上均实现了比基线FMQA更高的平均最终巡航速度，且在32变量问题上优势更为显著。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses a limitation in Factorization Machine with Quadratic-Optimization Annealing (FMQA) for black-box optimization, where uniform random initial sampling in one-hot encoding often leaves many binary variables never active, preventing their FM parameters from receiving direct gradient updates. To solve this, the authors propose designing the initial training data to ensure complete marginal bit coverage, meaning every binary variable is active at least once, using Latin hypercube sampling (LHS) and Sobol' sequence to create LHS-FMQA and Sobol'-FMQA. 该论文针对基于因子机与二次优化退火（FMQA）的黑箱优化方法中，均匀随机初始采样在独热编码下常导致许多二元变量从未激活，从而使其FM参数无法从观测响应中获得直接梯度更新的问题。为此，作者提出通过设计初始训练数据实现完全边际位覆盖，即确保每个二元变量至少激活一次，采用拉丁超立方采样（LHS）和Sobol'序列生成LHS-FMQA和Sobol'-FMQA方法。在包含17个和32个设计变量的人力飞行器机翼形状优化基准测试中，两种方法均实现了比基线FMQA更高的平均最终巡航速度，且在32变量问题上优势更明显。
Reward-Decomposed Reinforcement Learning for Immersive Video Role-Playing
Authors: Miao Wang, Yuling Shi, Yijiang Li, Yeheng Chen, Xiaodong Gu, Bin Li, Bo Gao, Yaduan Ruan
First: 2026-05-06T10:32:23+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-06T10:32:23+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Text-based role-playing models can imitate character styles, yet they often fail to reflect a scene's atmosphere and evolving tension, both essential for immersive applications such as Virtual Reality (VR) games and interactive narratives. We study video-grounded role-playing dialogue and introduce EBM-RL (Eye-Brain-Mouth Reinforcement Learning), a decoupled GRPO-based framework that explicitly separates observation ([perception]), reasoning ([think]), and utterance ([answer]). This structure promotes human-like sensory grounding by compelling the model to first attend to visual cues, then form internal interpretations, and finally generate context-appropriate dialogue. EBM-RL integrates four complementary rewards: (i) CLIP-based scene-text alignment to improve ambiance and emotion; (ii) a Perceptual-Cognitive reward that encourages [perception] and [think] processes that increase the likelihood of the reference response; (iii) answer accuracy to ensure faithfulness; and (iv) a dense format reward to enforce the desired structured output. Extensive experiments demonstrate that EBM-RL substantially outperforms text-only role-playing baselines and larger-scale vision-language models on our immersive role-playing benchmark, delivering simultaneous gains in visual-atmosphere consistency and character authenticity. Beyond the role-playing domain, EBM-RL also exhibits strong zero-shot generalization: without any additional fine-tuning, it consistently improves performance on out-of-domain VideoQA benchmarks. We additionally release an open-source dataset for video-grounded role-playing dialogue.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向沉浸式视频角色扮演的奖励分解强化学习
基于文本的角色扮演模型能够模仿角色风格，但往往难以反映场景氛围和不断变化的紧张感，而这些对于虚拟现实（VR）游戏和交互式叙事等沉浸式应用至关重要。我们研究了以视频为基础的角色扮演对话，并引入了EBM-RL（眼-脑-口强化学习），这是一种基于解耦GRPO的框架，明确分离了观察（[感知]）、推理（[思考]）和话语（[回答]）。该结构通过迫使模型首先关注视觉线索，然后形成内部解释，最后生成符合上下文的对话，从而促进类人的感官基础。 EBM-RL整合了四种互补奖励：（i）基于CLIP的场景-文本对齐，以改善氛围和情感；（ii）感知-认知奖励，鼓励增加参考响应可能性的[感知]和[思考]过程；（iii）答案准确性，以确保忠实性；以及（iv）密集格式奖励，以强制执行所需的结构化输出。 大量实验表明，在我们的沉浸式角色扮演基准测试中，EBM-RL显著优于纯文本角色扮演基线和更大规模的视觉语言模型，同时在视觉-氛围一致性和角色真实性方面取得了同步提升。在角色扮演领域之外，EBM-RL还表现出强大的零样本泛化能力：无需任何额外微调，它就能持续提升在域外VideoQA基准测试上的性能。我们还发布了一个用于视频基础角色扮演对话的开源数据集。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the limitation of text-based role-playing models in capturing scene atmosphere and evolving tension for immersive applications like VR games. The authors propose EBM-RL (Eye-Brain-Mouth Reinforcement Learning), a decoupled GRPO-based framework that explicitly separates perception, reasoning, and utterance generation to enhance sensory grounding. The method integrates four rewards: CLIP-based scene-text alignment, a Perceptual-Cognitive reward, answer accuracy, and a dense format reward. Extensive experiments show that EBM-RL significantly outperforms text-only baselines and larger vision-language models on an immersive role-playing benchmark, achieving improvements in visual-atmosphere consistency and character authenticity, and also demonstrates strong zero-shot generalization on out-of-domain VideoQA benchmarks.
该论文针对文本型角色扮演模型在捕捉场景氛围和动态张力方面的不足，这些对于VR游戏等沉浸式应用至关重要。作者提出了EBM-RL（眼-脑-口强化学习），一种基于解耦GRPO的框架，明确分离感知、推理和话语生成，以增强感官基础。该方法整合了四种奖励：基于CLIP的场景-文本对齐、感知-认知奖励、答案准确性和密集格式奖励。大量实验表明，EBM-RL在沉浸式角色扮演基准上显著优于纯文本基线和更大规模的视觉语言模型，在视觉氛围一致性和角色真实性上取得提升，并在域外VideoQA基准上展现出强大的零样本泛化能力。
SPHERE: Mitigating the Loss of Spectral Plasticity in Mixture-of-Experts for Deep Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Lirui Luo, Guoxi Zhang, Hongming Xu, Cong Fang, Qing Li
Venue: ICML 2026
First: 2026-05-06T10:02:53+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-06T10:02:53+00:00
Comments: Accepted to ICML 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In deep reinforcement learning (DRL), an agent is trained from a stream of experience. In a continual learning setting, such agents can suffer from plasticity loss: their ability to learn new skills from new experiences diminishes over training. Recently, Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) networks have been reported to enable scaling laws and facilitate the learning of diverse skills. However, in continual reinforcement learning settings, their performance can degenerate as learning proceeds, indicating a loss of plasticity. To address this, building on Neural Tangent Kernel (NTK) theory, we formalize the plasticity loss in MoE policies as a loss of spectral plasticity. We then derive a tractable proxy for spectral plasticity, one expressible in terms of individual expert feature matrices. Leveraging this proxy, we introduce SPHERE, a practical Parseval penalty tailored for MoE-based policies that alleviates the loss of spectral plasticity. On MetaWorld and HumanoidBench, SPHERE improves average success under continual RL by 133% and 50% over an unregularized MoE baseline, while maintaining higher spectral plasticity throughout training.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SPHERE：缓解深度强化学习中混合专家模型的频谱可塑性损失
在深度强化学习中，智能体通过经验流进行训练。在持续学习场景下，此类智能体会遭遇可塑性损失：其从新经验中学习新技能的能力随训练过程逐渐衰退。近期研究表明，混合专家网络能够实现规模定律并促进多样化技能的学习。然而在持续强化学习环境中，其性能会随学习进程退化，表明存在可塑性损失。为解决此问题，我们基于神经正切核理论，将MoE策略中的可塑性损失形式化为频谱可塑性损失。进而推导出频谱可塑性的可计算代理指标，该指标可用单个专家特征矩阵表示。利用该代理指标，我们提出SPHERE——一种专为MoE策略设计的实用Parseval惩罚项，可缓解频谱可塑性损失。在MetaWorld和HumanoidBench基准测试中，与未正则化的MoE基线相比，SPHERE在持续强化学习下的平均成功率分别提升133%和50%，并在整个训练过程中保持更高的频谱可塑性。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the loss of plasticity in Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) networks for deep reinforcement learning, where agents gradually lose the ability to learn new skills from ongoing experience streams. The authors formalize this problem as a loss of spectral plasticity using Neural Tangent Kernel theory and derive a tractable proxy based on individual expert feature matrices. They propose SPHERE, a practical Parseval penalty that regularizes MoE policies to maintain spectral plasticity. Experiments on MetaWorld and HumanoidBench show that SPHERE improves average success rates by 133% and 50% respectively over an unregularized MoE baseline, while preserving higher spectral plasticity throughout training.

ELVIS: Ensemble-Calibrated Latent Imagination for Long-Horizon Visual MPC
Authors: Yurui Du, Pinhao Song, Yutong Hu, Renaud Detry
First: 2026-05-06T09:59:58+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-06T09:59:58+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
A central challenge of visual control with model-based reinforcement learning (RL) is reliable long-horizon planning: long rollouts with learned latent dynamics exhibit branching futures and multi-modal action-value distributions. In addition, compounding model errors amplified by visual occlusions make deep imagination brittle. We present ELVIS, a latent model predictive controller (MPC) designed to make long-horizon planning practical. ELVIS plans in a Dreamer-style recurrent state space model (RSSM) and replaces standard unimodal model predictive path integral (MPPI) with a Gaussian-mixture MPPI that maintains multiple coherent hypotheses over long horizons, avoiding mode averaging under branching rollouts. In parallel, ELVIS stabilizes deep imagination with a shared uncertainty-aware lambda-return: an ensemble of latent critics defines an upper-confidence-bound (UCB) score that gates a time-varying lambda, adaptively trading off bootstrapping versus look-ahead to limit compounding error during planning. The same return is used both to train an actor-critic prior from imagined rollouts and to score candidate trajectories inside GMM-MPPI, aligning RL objectives with the planner's long-horizon optimization. On fourteen DeepMind Control Suite visual tasks, ELVIS establishes state-of-the-art performance compared with TD-MPC2 and DreamerV3. Finally, ELVIS transfers zero-shot to a real-world sand-spraying task with severe occlusions, improving surface-quality metrics and demonstrating robustness beyond simulation.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ELVIS：面向长时域视觉模型预测控制的集成校准潜在想象
基于模型的强化学习（RL）在视觉控制中的一个核心挑战是实现可靠的长时域规划：使用学习到的潜在动力学进行长展开时，会出现分支未来和多模态动作价值分布。此外，视觉遮挡放大的复合模型误差使得深度想象变得脆弱。我们提出ELVIS，一种旨在使长时域规划实用的潜在模型预测控制器（MPC）。ELVIS在Dreamer风格的循环状态空间模型（RSSM）中进行规划，并用高斯混合MPPI替代标准单模态模型预测路径积分（MPPI），在长时域上维持多个连贯假设，避免分支展开下的模式平均。同时，ELVIS通过共享的不确定性感知λ回报稳定深度想象：一个潜在评论家集成定义了一个上置信界（UCB）分数，用于门控时变λ，自适应地权衡自举与前瞻，以限制规划中的复合误差。相同的回报既用于从想象展开中训练演员-评论家先验，也用于在GMM-MPPI内对候选轨迹评分，使RL目标与规划器的长时域优化对齐。在十四个DeepMind Control Suite视觉任务上，ELVIS相比TD-MPC2和DreamerV3取得了最先进的性能。最后，ELVIS零样本迁移到具有严重遮挡的真实世界喷砂任务，改善了表面质量指标，展示了超越仿真的鲁棒性。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces ELVIS, a latent model predictive controller designed to address the challenge of reliable long-horizon planning in visual model-based reinforcement learning, where compounding model errors and multi-modal action-value distributions degrade performance. The method employs a Dreamer-style recurrent state space model for latent dynamics, replacing standard unimodal MPPI with a Gaussian-mixture MPPI to maintain multiple coherent hypotheses and avoid mode averaging. Additionally, it stabilizes planning via an ensemble of latent critics that define an uncertainty-aware lambda-return, adaptively balancing bootstrapping and look-ahead to limit compounding errors. On fourteen DeepMind Control Suite visual tasks, ELVIS achieves state-of-the-art performance compared to TD-MPC2 and DreamerV3, and it transfers zero-shot to a real-world sand-spraying task with severe occlusions, improving surface-quality metrics and demonstrating robustness beyond simulation.

The Tsetlin Machine Goes Deep: Logical Learning and Reasoning With Graphs
Authors: Ole-Christoffer Granmo, Youmna Abdelwahab, Per-Arne Andersen, Karl Audun K. Borgersen, Paul F. A. Clarke, Kunal Dumbre, Ylva Grønningsæter, Vojtech Halenka, Runar Helin, Lei Jiao, Ahmed Khalid, Rebekka Omslandseter, Rupsa Saha, Mayur Shende, Xuan Zhang
First: 2025-07-20T09:16:31+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-06T09:54:23+00:00
Comments: 23 pages, 9 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Pattern recognition with concise and flat AND-rules makes the Tsetlin Machine (TM) both interpretable and efficient, while the power of Tsetlin automata enables accuracy comparable to deep learning on an increasing number of datasets. We introduce the Graph Tsetlin Machine (GraphTM) for learning interpretable deep clauses from graph-structured input. Moving beyond flat, fixed-length input, the GraphTM gets more versatile, supporting sequences, grids, relations, and multimodality. Through message passing, the GraphTM builds nested deep clauses to recognize sub-graph patterns with exponentially fewer clauses, increasing both interpretability and data utilization. For image classification, GraphTM preserves interpretability and achieves 3.86%-points higher accuracy on CIFAR-10 than a convolutional TM. For tracking action coreference, faced with increasingly challenging tasks, GraphTM outperforms other reinforcement learning methods by up to 20.6%-points. In recommendation systems, it tolerates increasing noise to a great extent, similar to a GCN. Finally, for viral genome sequence data, GraphTM is competitive with BiLSTM-CNN and GCN accuracy-wise, training ~2.5x faster than GCN. The GraphTM's application to these varied fields demonstrates how graph representation learning and deep clauses bring new possibilities for TM learning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Tsetlin机器深度化：基于图的逻辑学习与推理
模式识别通过简洁扁平的AND规则使Tsetlin机器（TM）兼具可解释性和高效性，而Tsetlin自动机的强大能力使其在越来越多数据集上的准确率可与深度学习媲美。我们提出图Tsetlin机器（GraphTM），用于从图结构输入中学习可解释的深层子句。超越扁平化固定长度输入后，GraphTM更具通用性，支持序列、网格、关系和多模态。通过消息传递，GraphTM构建嵌套深层子句，以指数级更少的子句识别子图模式，同时提升可解释性和数据利用率。在图像分类中，GraphTM保持可解释性，并在CIFAR-10上比卷积TM准确率高出3.86个百分点。在动作共指追踪中，面对日益复杂的任务，GraphTM比其他强化学习方法性能高出最多20.6个百分点。在推荐系统中，它能像图卷积网络（GCN）一样大幅容忍噪声增加。最后，在病毒基因组序列数据上，GraphTM在准确率上与BiLSTM-CNN和GCN相当，训练速度比GCN快约2.5倍。GraphTM在这些不同领域的应用展示了图表示学习和深层子句为TM学习带来的新可能性。

The paper introduces the Graph Tsetlin Machine (GraphTM), which extends the Tsetlin Machine to handle graph-structured input by using message passing to build nested deep clauses, enabling logical learning and reasoning with graphs. This method addresses the limitation of flat, fixed-length input in traditional TMs, allowing for more versatile pattern recognition across sequences, grids, relations, and multimodality. Experimental results show that GraphTM achieves 3.86% higher accuracy on CIFAR-10 than a convolutional TM, outperforms reinforcement learning methods by up to 20.6% in action coreference tracking, tolerates noise well in recommendation systems, and trains about 2.5 times faster than GCN on viral genome sequence data while maintaining competitive accuracy.
该论文提出了图Tsetlin机（GraphTM），通过消息传递构建嵌套深度子句，将Tsetlin机扩展到图结构输入，实现了基于图的逻辑学习与推理。该方法克服了传统TM仅能处理固定长度扁平输入的限制，支持序列、网格、关系和多模态等更通用的模式识别。实验结果表明，GraphTM在CIFAR-10上比卷积TM准确率提高3.86%，在动作共指追踪任务中比强化学习方法高出最多20.6%，在推荐系统中能较好容忍噪声，并在病毒基因组序列数据上训练速度比GCN快约2.5倍，同时保持有竞争力的准确率。
Load constrained wind farm flow control through multi-objective multi-agent reinforcement learning
Authors: Teodor Åstrand, Marcus Binder Nilsen, Iasonas Tsaklis, Tuhfe Göçmen, Pierre-Elouan Réthoré, Nikolay Dimitrov
First: 2026-04-13T12:39:26+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-06T09:38:54+00:00
Comments: Submitted to Journal of Physics: Conference Series (Torque 2026). This is the Accepted Manuscript version of an article accepted for publication in Journal of Physics: Conference Series. IOP Publishing Ltd is not responsible for any errors or omissions in this version of the manuscript or any version derived from it. This Accepted Manuscript is published under a CC BY licence
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This study presents a multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) framework for load-constrained wind farm flow control (WFFC). While wake steering can enhance total wind farm power, it often introduces increased structural loads on downstream turbines. To address this, we integrate an Independent Soft Actor-Critic (I-SAC) architecture with a data-driven, local inflow sector-averaged surrogate model to provide real-time estimates of Damage Equivalent Loads (DELs). By incorporating these estimates into a shaped reward function, turbine-specific agents are trained to maximize power production while adhering to specific load-increase thresholds ($Δ_{max}$) of 10%, 20%, and 30% relative to a baseline controller. The framework is implemented within the WindGym environment using the DYNAMIKS flow solver with Dynamic Wake Meandering (DWM) model to capture non-stationary wake physics. Results indicate that the MARL agents successfully learn collaborative policies that prioritise power gain while actively retreating from high-DEL control strategies.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于多目标多智能体强化学习的载荷约束风电场流动控制
本研究提出了一种用于载荷约束风电场流动控制（WFFC）的多智能体强化学习（MARL）框架。虽然尾流偏转可提升风电场总功率，但往往会导致下游风机结构载荷增加。为此，我们将独立软演员-评论家（I-SAC）架构与数据驱动的局部入流扇区平均代理模型相结合，以实时估算损伤等效载荷（DELs）。通过将这些估算值纳入塑形奖励函数，训练各风机专用智能体在遵守相对于基准控制器10%、20%和30%的特定载荷增加阈值（Δ_max）的同时最大化发电量。该框架在WindGym环境中实现，采用DYNAMIKS流动求解器与动态尾流蜿蜒（DWM）模型来捕捉非稳态尾流物理特性。结果表明，MARL智能体成功学习了优先考虑功率增益同时主动规避高DEL控制策略的协作策略。
Summary / 总结
This study proposes a multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) framework for load-constrained wind farm flow control, addressing the trade-off between power maximization and structural load increases caused by wake steering. The method integrates an Independent Soft Actor-Critic (I-SAC) architecture with a data-driven surrogate model that estimates Damage Equivalent Loads (DELs) in real time, using a shaped reward function to enforce load-increase thresholds of 10%, 20%, and 30% relative to a baseline. Experiments in the WindGym environment with the DYNAMIKS flow solver and Dynamic Wake Meandering model show that the MARL agents learn collaborative policies that prioritize power gain while avoiding high-DEL control strategies.
该研究提出了一种基于多智能体强化学习的负载约束风电场流动控制框架，旨在解决尾流偏转提升总功率与增加下游风机结构负载之间的矛盾。方法采用独立软演员-评论家架构结合数据驱动的局部入流扇区平均代理模型，实时估算等效损伤载荷，并通过设计奖励函数将负载增加阈值限制在基准控制器的10%、20%和30%以内。在WindGym环境及动态尾流蜿蜒模型上的实验表明，多智能体强化学习智能体学会了协作策略，优先提升功率同时主动规避高负载控制策略。
The Perceptual Bandwidth Bottleneck in Vision-Language Models: Active Visual Reasoning via Sequential Experimental Design
Authors: Anjie Liu, Ziqin Gong, Yan Song, Yuxiang Chen, Xiaolong Liu, Hengtong Lu, Kaike Zhang, Chen Wei, Jun Wang
Venue: ICML 2026
First: 2026-05-02T09:39:42+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-06T08:19:25+00:00
Comments: 27 pages, 5 figures, accepted at ICML 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Visual perception in modern Vision-Language Models (VLMs) is constrained by a perceptual bandwidth bottleneck: a broad field of view preserves global context but sacrifices the fine-grained details required for complex reasoning. We argue that high-resolution visual reasoning is therefore not only semantic reasoning but also task-relevant evidence acquisition under limited perceptual bandwidth. Inspired by active vision and information foraging, we formalise this process as sequential Bayesian optimal experimental design (S-BOED), where an agent decides which visual evidence to acquire before answering. Since exact Bayesian inference is intractable in continuous gigapixel spaces, we derive a tractable coverage--resolution objective as a proxy for task-relevant information gain. We instantiate this framework with FOVEA, a training-free procedure that refines VLM crop proposals through evidence-oriented probing. Experiments on high-resolution benchmarks show consistent gains over direct and ReAct-style baselines, with particularly strong improvements in search-dominated remote-sensing settings.
中文标题/摘要
标题：视觉-语言模型中的感知带宽瓶颈：通过序列实验设计实现主动视觉推理
现代视觉-语言模型（VLM）中的视觉感知受到感知带宽瓶颈的制约：宽视野保留了全局上下文，但牺牲了复杂推理所需的细粒度细节。我们认为，高分辨率视觉推理因此不仅是语义推理，也是在有限感知带宽下进行任务相关证据获取的过程。受主动视觉和信息觅食启发，我们将此过程形式化为序列贝叶斯最优实验设计（S-BOED），其中智能体在回答前决定获取哪些视觉证据。由于在连续千兆像素空间中精确贝叶斯推理不可行，我们推导出一个可处理的覆盖-分辨率目标作为任务相关信息增益的代理。我们通过FOVEA实例化该框架，这是一种无需训练的程序，通过证据导向的探测来优化VLM裁剪提案。在高分辨率基准上的实验表明，该方法相较于直接和ReAct式基线有一致提升，在搜索主导的遥感场景中改进尤为显著。
