Meta-Learning and Meta-Reinforcement Learning -- Tracing the Path towards DeepMind's Adaptive Agent
Authors: Björn Hoppmann, Christoph Scholz
First: 2026-02-23T13:39:58+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-06T07:57:45+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Humans are highly effective at utilizing prior knowledge to adapt to novel tasks, a capability that standard machine learning models struggle to replicate due to their reliance on task-specific training. Meta-learning overcomes this limitation by allowing models to acquire transferable knowledge from various tasks, enabling rapid adaptation to new challenges with minimal data. This survey provides a rigorous, task-based formalization of meta-learning and meta-reinforcement learning and uses that paradigm to chronicle the landmark algorithms that paved the way for DeepMind's Adaptive Agent, consolidating the essential concepts needed to understand the Adaptive Agent and other generalist approaches.
中文标题/摘要
标题：元学习与元强化学习——追溯通往DeepMind自适应智能体的路径
人类善于利用先验知识适应新任务，而标准机器学习模型因依赖特定任务训练而难以复制这一能力。元学习通过让模型从多种任务中获取可迁移知识克服了这一局限，使其能以最少数据快速适应新挑战。本综述基于任务形式化框架严格定义了元学习与元强化学习，并以此范式梳理了为DeepMind自适应智能体奠定基础的里程碑式算法，整合了理解自适应智能体及其他通用方法所需的核心概念。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the human ability to rapidly adapt to new tasks, which standard machine learning models fail to achieve due to their task-specific training, this survey formalizes meta-learning and meta-reinforcement learning using a rigorous task-based framework. The method involves chronicling landmark algorithms that build transferable knowledge from multiple tasks, enabling quick adaptation with minimal data. The main experimental results highlight how these foundational concepts culminated in DeepMind's Adaptive Agent, demonstrating the effectiveness of generalist approaches in achieving rapid task adaptation.
受人类快速适应新任务能力的启发，而标准机器学习模型因依赖特定任务训练而难以实现这一点，该综述通过严格的任务基础形式化定义了元学习和元强化学习。其方法包括梳理那些从多个任务中获取可迁移知识、从而能以最少数据快速适应新挑战的里程碑式算法。主要实验结果表明，这些基础概念最终促成了DeepMind自适应智能体的诞生，验证了通用方法在实现快速任务适应方面的有效性。
On the Non-decoupling of Supervised Fine-tuning and Reinforcement Learning in Post-training
Authors: Xueyan Niu, Bo Bai, Wei Han, Weixi Zhang
First: 2026-01-12T10:14:09+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-06T07:45:21+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Post-training of large language models routinely interleaves supervised fine-tuning (SFT) with reinforcement learning (RL). These two methods have different objectives: SFT minimizes the cross-entropy loss between model outputs and expert responses, while RL maximizes reward signals derived from human preferences or rule-based verifiers. Modern reasoning models have widely adopted the practice of alternating SFT and RL training. However, there is no theoretical account of whether they can be decoupled. We prove that decoupling is impossible in either order: (1) SFT-then-RL coupling: RL increases SFT loss under both distributional (KL-based) and landscape (PL-based) analyses; and (2) RL-then-SFT coupling: SFT lowers the reward achieved by RL under analogous conditions. Under the PL condition, we further derive the optimal RL duration that balances reward improvement against SFT degradation, identify the non-decoupling threshold governing when RL can improve SFT, and bound the gradient misalignment via spectral concentration. Experiments on Qwen3-0.6B confirm the predicted degradation, verifying that SFT and RL cannot be separated without loss of prior performance in the post-training pipeline.
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates whether supervised fine-tuning (SFT) and reinforcement learning (RL) can be decoupled in the post-training of large language models, motivated by their common interleaving despite different objectives. The authors prove theoretically that decoupling is impossible in both orders: SFT-then-RL coupling increases SFT loss under distributional and landscape analyses, while RL-then-SFT coupling lowers the reward achieved by RL. They derive the optimal RL duration under the PL condition to balance reward improvement against SFT degradation, identify a non-decoupling threshold, and bound gradient misalignment via spectral concentration. Experiments on Qwen3-0.6B confirm the predicted degradation, verifying that SFT and RL cannot be separated without loss of prior performance.
本文研究了在大型语言模型的后训练中，监督微调（SFT）和强化学习（RL）是否能够解耦，其动机源于尽管两者目标不同却常被交替使用。作者从理论上证明了解耦在两种顺序下均不可能：先SFT后RL会在分布和景观分析下增加SFT损失，而先RL后SFT则会降低RL获得的奖励。在PL条件下，他们推导出最优RL时长以平衡奖励提升与SFT退化，识别出非解耦阈值，并通过谱集中度界定了梯度错位。在Qwen3-0.6B上的实验证实了预测的退化，验证了SFT和RL在后训练流程中无法分离而不损失先前性能。
WaferSAGE: Large Language Model-Powered Wafer Defect Analysis via Synthetic Data Generation and Rubric-Guided Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Ke Xu
First: 2026-04-30T09:19:26+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-06T07:17:48+00:00
Comments: 16 pages, 3 figures, 8 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We present WaferSAGE, a framework for wafer defect visual question answering using small vision-language models. To address data scarcity in semiconductor manufacturing, we propose a three-stage synthesis pipeline incorporating structured rubric generation for precise evaluation. Starting from limited labeled wafer maps, we employ clustering-based cleaning to filter label noise, then generate comprehensive defect descriptions using vision-language models, which are converted into structured evaluation rubrics criteria. These rubrics guide the synthesis of VQA pairs, ensuring coverage across defect type identification, spatial distribution, morphology, and root cause analysis. Our dual assessment framework aligns rule-based metrics with LLM-Judge scores via Bayesian optimization, enabling reliable automated evaluation. Through curriculum-based reinforcement learning with Group Sequence Policy Optimization (GSPO) and rubric-aligned rewards, our 4B-parameter Qwen3-VL model achieves a 6.493 LLM-Judge score, closely approaching Gemini-3-Flash (7.149) while enabling complete on-premise deployment. We demonstrate that small models with domain-specific training can surpass proprietary large models in specialized industrial visual understanding, offering a viable path for privacy-preserving, cost-effective deployment in semiconductor manufacturing.
中文标题/摘要
标题：WaferSAGE：基于合成数据生成与评分准则引导强化学习的大语言模型晶圆缺陷分析
我们提出WaferSAGE框架，用于基于小型视觉语言模型的晶圆缺陷视觉问答。为解决半导体制造中的数据稀缺问题，我们提出三阶段合成流程，结合结构化评分准则生成以实现精确评估。从有限的标注晶圆图出发，采用基于聚类的清洗方法过滤标签噪声，随后利用视觉语言模型生成全面的缺陷描述，并将其转化为结构化评估准则。这些准则指导视觉问答对的合成，确保覆盖缺陷类型识别、空间分布、形态及根因分析。 我们的双重评估框架通过贝叶斯优化将基于规则的指标与LLM-Judge评分对齐，实现可靠的自动化评估。通过基于课程学习的强化学习（结合组序列策略优化与评分准则对齐奖励），我们的4B参数Qwen3-VL模型取得了6.493的LLM-Judge评分，接近Gemini-3-Flash（7.149），同时支持完全本地部署。我们证明，经过领域特定训练的小型模型在专业工业视觉理解中可超越专有大模型，为半导体制造中隐私保护、成本高效的部署提供可行路径。
Dream-MPC: Gradient-Based Model Predictive Control with Latent Imagination
Authors: Jonathan Spieler, Sven Behnke
First: 2026-05-06T07:13:11+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-06T07:13:11+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
State-of-the-art model-based Reinforcement Learning (RL) approaches either use gradient-free, population-based methods for planning, learned policy networks, or a combination of policy networks and planning. Hybrid approaches that combine Model Predictive Control (MPC) with a learned model and a policy prior to leverage the advantages of both paradigms have shown promising results. However, these approaches typically rely on gradient-free optimization methods, which can be computationally expensive for high-dimensional control tasks. While gradient-based methods are a promising alternative, recent works have empirically shown that gradient-based methods often perform worse than their gradient-free counterparts. We propose Dream-MPC, a novel approach that generates few candidate trajectories from a rolled-out policy and optimizes each trajectory by gradient ascent using a learned world model, uncertainty regularization and amortization of optimization iterations over time by reusing previously optimized actions. Our results on 24 continuous control tasks show that Dream-MPC can significantly improve the performance of the underlying policy and can outperform gradient-free MPC and state-of-the-art baselines. We will open source our code and more at https://dream-mpc.github.io.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Dream-MPC：基于梯度与潜在想象的模型预测控制
最先进的基于模型的强化学习方法要么使用无梯度、基于群体的方法进行规划，要么使用学习到的策略网络，或者结合策略网络与规划。结合模型预测控制与学习模型及策略先验的混合方法，能够利用两种范式的优势，已展现出令人鼓舞的结果。然而，这些方法通常依赖无梯度优化方法，对于高维控制任务计算成本高昂。尽管基于梯度的方法是一种有前景的替代方案，但近期研究实证表明，基于梯度的方法往往表现不如无梯度方法。我们提出Dream-MPC，一种新颖方法，从展开的策略中生成少量候选轨迹，并通过使用学习到的世界模型、不确定性正则化以及通过重用先前优化的动作来随时间摊销优化迭代，对每条轨迹进行梯度上升优化。我们在24个连续控制任务上的结果表明，Dream-MPC能显著提升底层策略的性能，并优于无梯度MPC及最先进的基线方法。我们将在https://dream-mpc.github.io开源代码及更多内容。
Summary / 总结
Dream-MPC addresses the inefficiency of gradient-free model predictive control in high-dimensional tasks by introducing a gradient-based planning method. The approach generates candidate trajectories from a policy network, optimizes them via gradient ascent using a learned latent world model, and incorporates uncertainty regularization along with temporal amortization of optimization steps. Experiments on 24 continuous control tasks demonstrate that Dream-MPC significantly improves policy performance and outperforms gradient-free MPC and other state-of-the-art baselines.
Dream-MPC针对高维控制任务中无梯度模型预测控制计算效率低的问题，提出了一种基于梯度的规划方法。该方法从策略网络生成少量候选轨迹，利用学习到的潜在世界模型通过梯度上升优化每条轨迹，并引入不确定性正则化以及跨时间步的优化迭代复用。在24个连续控制任务上的实验表明，Dream-MPC能显著提升基础策略的性能，并超越无梯度MPC及其他最先进基线方法。
Correct Is Not Enough: Training Reasoning Planners with Executor-Grounded Rewards
Authors: Tianyang Han, Hengyu Shi, Junjie Hu, Xu Yang, Zhiling Wang, Junhao Su
First: 2026-05-05T15:24:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-06T07:00:58+00:00
Comments: 36 pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards has become a common way to improve explicit reasoning in large language models, but final-answer correctness alone does not reveal whether the reasoning trace is faithful, reliable, or useful to the model that consumes it. This outcome-only signal can reinforce traces that are right for the wrong reasons, overstate reasoning gains by rewarding shortcuts, and propagate flawed intermediate states in multi-step systems. To this end, we propose TraceLift, a planner-executor training framework that treats reasoning as a consumable intermediate artifact. During planner training, the planner emits tagged reasoning. A frozen executor turns this reasoning into the final artifact for verifier feedback, while an executor-grounded reward shapes the intermediate trace. This reward multiplies a rubric-based Reasoning Reward Model (RM) score by measured uplift on the same frozen executor, crediting traces that are both high-quality and useful. To make reasoning quality directly learnable, we introduce TRACELIFT-GROUPS, a rubric-annotated reason-only dataset built from math and code seed problems. Each example is a same-problem group containing a high-quality reference trace and multiple plausible flawed traces with localized perturbations that reduce reasoning quality or solution support while preserving task relevance. Extensive experiments on code and math benchmarks show that this executor-grounded reasoning reward improves the two-stage planner-executor system over execution-only training, suggesting that reasoning supervision should evaluate not only whether a trace looks good, but also whether it helps the model that consumes it. Our code is available at: https://github.com/MasaiahHan/TraceLift
中文标题/摘要
标题：正确还不够：用执行器锚定奖励训练推理规划器
基于可验证奖励的强化学习已成为提升大语言模型显式推理能力的常见方法，但仅凭最终答案的正确性无法揭示推理轨迹是否忠实、可靠或对使用该轨迹的模型有用。这种仅依赖结果的信号可能强化“歪打正着”的轨迹，通过奖励捷径夸大推理增益，并在多步系统中传播有缺陷的中间状态。为此，我们提出TraceLift——一种将推理视为可消费中间产物的规划器-执行器训练框架。在规划器训练阶段，规划器输出带标签的推理过程；冻结的执行器将此推理转化为最终产物以供验证器反馈，同时执行器锚定奖励塑造中间轨迹。该奖励将基于评分标准的推理奖励模型得分与同一冻结执行器上的实测提升相乘，从而奖励既高质量又有用的轨迹。为使推理质量可直接学习，我们引入TRACELIFT-GROUPS——基于数学和代码种子问题构建的带评分标准标注的纯推理数据集。每个示例包含同一问题的多组轨迹：一条高质量参考轨迹和若干条合理的缺陷轨迹，这些缺陷轨迹通过局部扰动降低推理质量或解决方案支持度，同时保持任务相关性。在代码和数学基准上的大量实验表明，这种执行器锚定的推理奖励能提升两阶段规划器-执行器系统相比纯执行训练的性能，说明推理监督不仅应评估轨迹是否“看起来好”，还应评估它是否对使用该轨迹的模型有帮助。我们的代码已开源：https://github.com/MasaiahHan/TraceLift
Summary / 总结
The paper identifies that training reasoning planners in large language models using only final-answer correctness as a reward can lead to unfaithful or unhelpful reasoning traces. To address this, the authors propose TraceLift, a planner-executor framework where a frozen executor uses the planner's tagged reasoning to produce the final output, and an executor-grounded reward combines a rubric-based Reasoning Reward Model score with the measured improvement in executor performance. Experiments on math and code benchmarks demonstrate that this approach outperforms execution-only training, showing that reasoning supervision should evaluate both the quality of the trace and its utility to the consuming model.
该论文指出，仅以最终答案正确性作为奖励来训练大型语言模型中的推理规划器，会导致推理轨迹不忠实或无用。为此，作者提出了TraceLift框架，该框架包含一个规划器和一个冻结的执行器，执行器利用规划器的标记推理生成最终输出，而基于执行器的奖励则结合了基于评分标准的推理奖励模型分数与执行器性能的实际提升。在数学和代码基准上的实验表明，该方法优于仅基于执行的训练，说明推理监督应同时评估轨迹的质量及其对下游模型的实用性。
Counter-Dyna: Data-Efficient RL-Based HVAC Control using Counterfactual Building Models
Authors: Jan Marco Ruiz de Vargas, Fabian Raisch, Zoltan Nagy, Pierre Pinson, Christoph Goebel
First: 2026-05-06T06:58:41+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-06T06:58:41+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Model-based reinforcement learning (MBRL) offers a promising approach for data-efficient energy management in buildings, combining the strengths of predictive modeling and reinforcement learning. While previous MBRL methods applied to HVAC control have reduced training data requirements, they still require several months of interaction with the building to learn a satisfactory control policy. A key reason is that existing surrogate models attempt to predict the entire state-space, including weather and electricity prices that are unaffected by control actions, or completely ignore these variables. Addressing these issues, we propose Counter-Dyna, a method that enhances the data-efficiency of Dyna, an MBRL method. We create data-efficient counterfactual surrogate models (CSM) by leveraging invariances in the state-space. Using a CSM in Dyna speeds up RL training measured in environment interaction data compared to previous results. In comparison with previous state-of-the-art that used 6-12 months of environment interactions, our method needs only 5 weeks. We evaluate our method in a large simulation study using the literature standard BOPTEST framework and proximal policy algorithm (PPO) as the RL algorithm. Our results show cost-saving potentials of 5.3% to 17.0% in a hypothetical deployment scenario. Our work is a significant step towards making real-world deployment of RL algorithms in HVAC control practically viable.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Counter-Dyna：基于反事实建筑模型的数据高效强化学习暖通空调控制
基于模型的强化学习（MBRL）结合了预测建模和强化学习的优势，为建筑数据高效能源管理提供了一种有前景的方法。尽管先前应用于暖通空调控制的MBRL方法减少了训练数据需求，但仍需与建筑交互数月才能学习到满意的控制策略。一个关键原因是现有替代模型试图预测整个状态空间，包括不受控制动作影响的天气和电价，或完全忽略这些变量。针对这些问题，我们提出Counter-Dyna，一种增强Dyna（一种MBRL方法）数据效率的方法。通过利用状态空间中的不变性，我们创建了数据高效的反事实替代模型（CSM）。在Dyna中使用CSM，相较于先前结果，以环境交互数据衡量的强化学习训练速度得以提升。与先前使用6-12个月环境交互的最先进方法相比，我们的方法仅需5周。我们使用文献标准BOPTEST框架和近端策略算法（PPO）作为强化学习算法，在大型模拟研究中评估了该方法。结果显示，在假设部署场景中，成本节约潜力为5.3%至17.0%。我们的工作是向强化学习算法在暖通空调控制中实际部署迈出的重要一步。
Summary / 总结
The paper proposes Counter-Dyna, a model-based reinforcement learning method for HVAC control that improves data efficiency by using counterfactual surrogate models. These models leverage invariances in the state-space to avoid predicting uncontrollable variables like weather and electricity prices, addressing a key limitation of prior methods. In a large simulation study using the BOPTEST framework and PPO algorithm, Counter-Dyna requires only 5 weeks of environment interaction data compared to the previous 6-12 months, achieving cost savings of 5.3% to 17.0% in hypothetical deployment scenarios.
该论文提出了Counter-Dyna方法，这是一种基于模型的强化学习暖通空调控制方法，通过利用状态空间中的不变性构建反事实代理模型，避免预测天气和电价等不可控变量，从而提升数据效率。在采用BOPTEST框架和PPO算法的大规模仿真研究中，Counter-Dyna仅需5周的环境交互数据，而此前方法需要6至12个月，并在假设部署场景中实现了5.3%至17.0%的成本节约。
Power Distribution Bridges Sampling, Self-Reward RL, and Self-Distillation
Authors: Akiyoshi Tomihari, Issei Sato
First: 2026-05-06T06:42:47+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-06T06:42:47+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recent analyses question whether reinforcement learning (RL) is responsible for strong reasoning in large language models (LLMs). At the same time, distillation and inference-time sampling, including power sampling, have emerged as effective ways to improve LLM performance. However, the relationship among RL, distillation, and sampling remains unclear. In this study, we focus on the power distribution, the target distribution of power sampling, and show that the power distribution bridges sampling, self-reward KL-regularized RL, and self-distillation. From the sampling perspective, we show that inexpensive local approximations cannot reproduce sequence-level power without information about possible suffixes. From the RL perspective, the power distribution is the closed-form optimizer of KL-regularized RL when the model's sequence-level log-probabilities are used as the reward. This identification leads to power self-distillation, an offline distillation surrogate that shares the same target distribution and amortizes the cost of power sampling into supervised training on teacher samples. We further show that power self-distillation can achieve self-reward sharpening, while improvement in a downstream true reward is governed by the covariance between true reward and self-reward under the power distribution. Experiments on reasoning tasks support our analysis: power sampling raises self-reward, true-reward gains depend on alignment with self-reward, and power self-distillation can match or exceed the performance of power sampling at much lower inference cost.
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates the relationship among reinforcement learning, distillation, and sampling in large language models, focusing on the power distribution as a unifying concept. The authors demonstrate that the power distribution serves as the closed-form optimizer of KL-regularized RL when sequence-level log-probabilities are used as rewards, and they introduce power self-distillation as an offline surrogate that shares the same target distribution. Experiments on reasoning tasks show that power sampling improves self-reward, true-reward gains depend on alignment with self-reward, and power self-distillation matches or exceeds power sampling performance at lower inference cost.
本文探讨了强化学习、蒸馏和采样在大语言模型中的关系，重点研究幂分布作为统一概念的作用。作者证明，当序列级对数概率用作奖励时，幂分布是KL正则化强化学习的闭式优化器，并提出了幂自蒸馏作为共享相同目标分布的离线替代方法。在推理任务上的实验表明，幂采样提升了自奖励，真实奖励的增益取决于与自奖励的对齐程度，而幂自蒸馏在更低推理成本下能达到或超过幂采样的性能。
Conflict-Aware Fusion: Mitigating Logic Inertia in Large Language Models via Structured Cognitive Priors
Authors: Qiming Bao, Xiaoxuan Fu, Michael Witbrock
First: 2025-12-06T10:49:50+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-06T06:30:16+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) achieve high accuracy on many reasoning benchmarks but remain brittle under structural perturbations of rule-based systems. We introduce a diagnostic framework with four stress tests -- redundant vs. essential rule deletion, contradictory-rule injection, logic-preserving rewrites, and multi-law stacking -- and use it to expose Logic Inertia: the tendency of generative LLMs (Qwen2/3, TinyLlama, GPT-4o, Gemma-3-4B-IT) and the encoder-only BERT baseline to persist along learned deductive trajectories under inconsistent premises. The collapse is sharp: untreated baselines fall from accuracy 1.00 on the base task to 0.00 on contradiction injection (instance-level exact match), and GPT-4o resolves only 56.0% of contradiction cases. We propose Conflict-Aware Fusion, a four-stage training pipeline that enforces verification-before-deduction as a learned structural prior: (i) SFT establishes the verification preamble; (ii) DPO sharpens the halt-on-contradiction decision boundary; (iii) Logical Invariance REgularisation (LIRE) penalises divergence between logically equivalent rule formulations via symmetric KL; (iv) Reinforcement Learning from Verification Feedback (RLVF) uses a symbolic forward-chaining engine as a deterministic oracle reward, jointly optimising invariance and sensitivity. The pipeline saturates all four primary stress tests for both 1.5B and 8B backbones. We further validate a Phase 2 extension that replaces the propositional oracle with a Lean 4 kernel, attaining 99.0% kernel agreement on the 105 classically-derivable (T) questions within a stratified 187-question Lean-translated sample (overall 71.7% across both polarities), providing a sound upgrade path to formally verified RL training. Code and benchmark: https://github.com/14H034160212/lemo
中文标题/摘要
标题：冲突感知融合：通过结构化认知先验缓解大语言模型中的逻辑惯性
大语言模型（LLMs）在许多推理基准测试中取得了高准确率，但在基于规则的系统的结构扰动下仍然脆弱。我们引入了一个包含四项压力测试的诊断框架——冗余与必要规则删除、矛盾规则注入、逻辑保持重写以及多定律叠加——并用其揭示逻辑惯性：生成式LLMs（Qwen2/3、TinyLlama、GPT-4o、Gemma-3-4B-IT）以及仅编码器的BERT基线在矛盾前提下的倾向，即沿习得的演绎轨迹持续运行。这种崩溃是剧烈的：未经处理的基线在基础任务上准确率从1.00降至矛盾注入时的0.00（实例级精确匹配），而GPT-4o仅解决了56.0%的矛盾案例。我们提出冲突感知融合，这是一个四阶段训练流程，将验证-再演绎作为习得的结构先验加以强化：（i）SFT建立验证前导；（ii）DPO锐化矛盾时停止的决策边界；（iii）逻辑不变正则化（LIRE）通过对称KL散度惩罚逻辑等价规则公式之间的差异；（iv）基于验证反馈的强化学习（RLVF）使用符号前向链接引擎作为确定性预言奖励，联合优化不变性与敏感性。该流程在1.5B和8B骨干网络上均饱和了所有四项主要压力测试。我们进一步验证了第二阶段扩展，将命题预言替换为Lean 4内核，在分层抽样的187个Lean翻译样本中，对105个经典可推导（T）问题达到99.0%的内核一致性（整体跨两种极性为71.7%），为形式化验证的RL训练提供了可靠的升级路径。代码和基准：https://github.com/14H034160212/lemo
Summary / 总结
The paper identifies Logic Inertia in large language models, where models persist along learned deductive trajectories under inconsistent premises, as revealed by four stress tests including contradictory-rule injection. To address this, the authors propose Conflict-Aware Fusion, a four-stage training pipeline that enforces verification-before-deduction as a structural prior, incorporating SFT, DPO, Logical Invariance Regularisation, and Reinforcement Learning from Verification Feedback. Experimental results show that untreated baselines drop from perfect accuracy to 0.00 on contradiction injection, while the proposed method saturates all stress tests for both 1.5B and 8B backbones, and a Phase 2 extension with a Lean 4 kernel achieves 99.0% kernel agreement on classically-derivable questions.
该论文通过四项压力测试（包括矛盾规则注入）揭示了大型语言模型中的逻辑惯性现象，即模型在不一致前提条件下仍沿习得的演绎轨迹运行。为解决此问题，作者提出了冲突感知融合方法，这是一个四阶段训练流程，通过结构化先验强制实施先验证后演绎，包含监督微调、直接偏好优化、逻辑不变性正则化以及基于验证反馈的强化学习。实验结果表明，未经处理的基线模型在矛盾注入任务上从完美准确率骤降至0.00，而所提方法在1.5B和8B骨干网络上均通过了所有压力测试；第二阶段扩展使用Lean 4内核，在经典可推导问题上达到了99.0%的内核一致性。
Beyond Variance: Prompt-Efficient RLVR via Rare-Event Amplification and Bidirectional Pairing
Authors: Yujuan Pang, Jiaxin Li, Xin Sheng, Ran Peng, Yong Ma
First: 2026-02-03T12:17:25+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-06T05:26:15+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) is effective for training large language models on deterministic outcome reasoning tasks. Prior work shows RLVR works with few prompts, but prompt selection is often based only on training-accuracy variance, leading to unstable optimization directions and weaker transfer. We revisit prompt selection from a mechanism-level view and argue that an effective minibatch should provide both (i) a reliable positive anchor and (ii) explicit negative learning signals from rare failures. Based on this principle, we propose \emph{positive--negative pairing}: at each update, we sample a hard-but-solvable $q^{+}$ and an easy-but-brittle prompt $q^{-}$(high success rate but not perfect), characterized by low and high empirical success rates under multiple rollouts. We further introduce Weighted GRPO, which reweights binary outcomes at the pair level and uses group-normalized advantages to amplify rare successes on $q^{+}$ into sharp positive guidance while turning rare failures on $q^{-}$ into strong negative penalties. This bidirectional signal provides informative learning feedback for both successes and failures, improving sample efficiency without suppressing exploration. On Qwen2.5-Math-7B, a single paired minibatch per update consistently outperforms a GRPO baseline that selects two prompts via commonly used variance-based selection heuristics: AIME~2025 Pass@8 improves from 16.8 to 22.2, and AMC23 Pass@64 from 94.0 to 97.0, while remaining competitive with large-scale RLVR trained from a pool of 1209 training prompts. Similar gains are observed on Qwen2.5-Math-7B-Instruct.
Summary / 总结
This work addresses the instability and weak transfer in reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) for large language models, which arises when prompt selection relies solely on training-accuracy variance. The authors propose a mechanism-level principle for effective minibatch construction: each update should include a hard-but-solvable positive prompt and an easy-but-brittle negative prompt, characterized by low and high empirical success rates respectively. They introduce Weighted GRPO, which reweights binary outcomes at the pair level and uses group-normalized advantages to amplify rare successes on the positive prompt and penalize rare failures on the negative prompt. On Qwen2.5-Math-7B, a single paired minibatch per update outperforms a GRPO baseline using variance-based selection, improving AIME 2025 Pass@8 from 16.8 to 22.2 and AMC23 Pass@64 from 94.0 to 97.0, while remaining competitive with large-scale RLVR trained on 1209 prompts.
该工作针对基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）在大语言模型训练中因仅依赖训练准确率方差进行提示选择而导致的优化方向不稳定和迁移能力弱的问题，提出了一种基于机制层面的有效小批量构建原则：每次更新应包含一个困难但可解的正向提示和一个简单但脆弱的负向提示，分别对应低经验成功率和高的经验成功率。作者引入了加权GRPO方法，在提示对级别重新加权二元结果，并使用组归一化优势来放大正向提示上的罕见成功信号，同时惩罚负向提示上的罕见失败信号。在Qwen2.5-Math-7B模型上，每步更新仅使用一个配对小批量，其表现优于采用方差选择启发式的GRPO基线，将AIME 2025 Pass@8从16.8提升至22.2，AMC23 Pass@64从94.0提升至97.0，同时与使用1209个训练提示的大规模RLVR训练结果相当。
Pen-Strategist: A Reasoning Framework for Penetration Testing Strategy Formation and Analysis
Authors: Yasod Ginige, Pasindu Marasinghe, Sajal Jain, Suranga Seneviratne
First: 2026-05-06T05:02:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-06T05:02:40+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Cyber threats are rapidly increasing, expanding their impact from large-scale enterprises to government services and individual users, making robust security systems increasingly essential. However, a significant shortage of skilled cybersecurity professionals exacerbates this challenge. While recent research has explored automating tasks such as penetration testing using LLM-based agents, existing frameworks often perform poorly due to limited capability in strategy formulation, domain-specific reasoning, and accurate action and tool selection. To overcome these limitations, we propose Pen-Strategist framework, consisting of a novel domain-specific reasoning model that derives pentesting strategies via logical reasoning and a classifier that converts the strategies into actionable steps. First, we construct a reasoning dataset containing logical explanations for both strategy derivation and step selection in pentesting scenarios. We then fine-tune a Qwen-3-14B model for strategy generation using reinforcement learning. Evaluation on the test split of the dataset demonstrates a 87% improvement in strategy derivation performance compared to the baseline. Furthermore, we integrate the fine-tuned Pen-Strategist model into existing automated pentesting frameworks, such as PentestGPT, and evaluate its performance on vulnerable machines, achieving a 47.5% improvement in subtask completion while surpassing the baseline GPT-5. Further experiments on the CTFKnow benchmark show an 18% performance gain over the base model. For step prediction, we train a semantic-based CNN classifier, which outperforms commercial LLMs by 28% and enhances execution stability. Finally, we conduct a user study to qualitatively assess the generated strategies, and Pen-Strategist demonstrates superior performance compared to the Claude-4.6-Sonnet.
中文标题/摘要
标题：渗透策略师：一种用于渗透测试策略制定与分析推理框架
网络威胁正在迅速增加，其影响从大型企业扩展到政府服务和个人用户，使得强大的安全系统日益重要。然而，熟练网络安全专业人员的严重短缺加剧了这一挑战。尽管近期研究探索了使用基于LLM的代理来自动化渗透测试等任务，但现有框架由于在策略制定、领域特定推理以及准确操作和工具选择方面能力有限，往往表现不佳。为克服这些限制，我们提出了Pen-Strategist框架，该框架包含一个新颖的领域特定推理模型，通过逻辑推理推导渗透测试策略，以及一个将策略转化为可操作步骤的分类器。首先，我们构建了一个推理数据集，其中包含渗透测试场景中策略推导和步骤选择的逻辑解释。然后，我们使用强化学习微调Qwen-3-14B模型以生成策略。在数据集测试集上的评估显示，与基线相比，策略推导性能提升了87%。此外，我们将微调后的Pen-Strategist模型集成到现有自动化渗透测试框架（如PentestGPT）中，并在易受攻击的机器上评估其性能，子任务完成率提高了47.5%，同时超越了基线GPT-5。在CTFKnow基准上的进一步实验显示，与基础模型相比，性能提升了18%。对于步骤预测，我们训练了一个基于语义的CNN分类器，其性能比商业LLM高出28%，并增强了执行稳定性。最后，我们进行了一项用户研究以定性评估生成的策略，Pen-Strategist相比Claude-4.6-Sonnet表现出更优的性能。

The paper addresses the growing shortage of cybersecurity professionals and the limitations of existing LLM-based penetration testing agents in strategy formulation and domain-specific reasoning. To overcome these challenges, the authors propose Pen-Strategist, a framework that fine-tunes a Qwen-3-14B model using reinforcement learning on a custom reasoning dataset for logical strategy derivation, and employs a semantic-based CNN classifier for step prediction. Experimental results show an 87% improvement in strategy derivation over the baseline, a 47.5% improvement in subtask completion when integrated into PentestGPT (surpassing GPT-5), an 18% gain on the CTFKnow benchmark, and a 28% improvement in step prediction over commercial LLMs, with user studies confirming superior performance compared to Claude-4.6-Sonnet.
该论文针对网络安全专业人员短缺以及现有基于LLM的渗透测试代理在策略制定和领域推理方面的局限性，提出了Pen-Strategist框架。该框架通过强化学习在自定义推理数据集上微调Qwen-3-14B模型以进行逻辑策略推导，并使用基于语义的CNN分类器进行步骤预测。实验结果表明，策略推导性能相比基线提升87%，集成到PentestGPT后子任务完成率提升47.5%（超越GPT-5），在CTFKnow基准上提升18%，步骤预测性能比商业LLM提升28%，用户研究也显示其表现优于Claude-4.6-Sonnet。
Towards General Preference Alignment: Diffusion Models at Nash Equilibrium
Authors: Jiaming Hu, Jiamu Bai, Haoyu Wang, Debarghya Mukherjee, Ioannis Ch. Paschalidis
First: 2026-05-06T04:50:42+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-06T04:50:42+00:00
Comments: 21 pages, 5 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF) has been popular for aligning text-to-image (T2I) diffusion models with human preferences. As a mainstream branch of RLHF, Direct Preference Optimization (DPO) offers a computationally efficient alternative that avoids explicit reward modeling and has been widely adopted in diffusion alignment. However, existing preference-based methods for diffusion alignment still rely on reward-induced preference signals and typically assume that human preferences can be adequately modeled by the Bradley--Terry (BT) model, which may fail to capture the full complexity of human preferences. In this paper, we formulate diffusion alignment from a game-theoretic perspective. We propose Diffusion Nash Preference Optimization (Diff.-NPO), an intuitive general preference framework for diffusion alignment. Diff.-NPO encourages the current policy to play against itself to achieve self improvement and lead to a better alignment. Empirically, we demonstrate the effectiveness of Diff.-NPO on the text-to-image generation task via various metrics. Diff.-NPO consistently outperforms existing preference-based diffusion alignment methods.
中文标题/摘要
标题：迈向通用偏好对齐：纳什均衡下的扩散模型
基于人类反馈的强化学习（RLHF）在将文本到图像（T2I）扩散模型与人类偏好对齐方面广受欢迎。作为RLHF的主流分支，直接偏好优化（DPO）提供了一种计算高效的替代方案，避免了显式奖励建模，并已广泛应用于扩散对齐。然而，现有的基于偏好的扩散对齐方法仍依赖奖励诱导的偏好信号，且通常假设人类偏好可由Bradley-Terry（BT）模型充分建模，这可能无法捕捉人类偏好的全部复杂性。本文从博弈论视角构建扩散对齐，提出扩散纳什偏好优化（Diff.-NPO），一种直观的通用偏好框架。Diff.-NPO鼓励当前策略与自身博弈以实现自我改进，从而达成更优对齐。实验上，我们通过多种指标在文本到图像生成任务中验证了Diff.-NPO的有效性。Diff.-NPO持续优于现有基于偏好的扩散对齐方法。

The paper addresses the limitations of existing preference-based alignment methods for text-to-image diffusion models, which rely on the Bradley-Terry model and may not capture the full complexity of human preferences. The authors propose Diffusion Nash Preference Optimization (Diff.-NPO), a game-theoretic framework that encourages the current policy to compete against itself for self-improvement and better alignment. Experimental results on text-to-image generation show that Diff.-NPO consistently outperforms existing preference-based diffusion alignment methods across various metrics.
该论文针对现有基于偏好的文本到图像扩散模型对齐方法的局限性，即依赖Bradley-Terry模型可能无法完全捕捉人类偏好的复杂性。作者提出了扩散纳什偏好优化（Diff.-NPO），一种博弈论框架，通过鼓励当前策略与自身对抗实现自我改进和更好的对齐。在文本到图像生成任务上的实验结果表明，Diff.-NPO在各种指标上持续优于现有的基于偏好的扩散对齐方法。
Quantum-inspired Reinforcement Learning for Synthesizable Drug Design
Authors: Dannong Wang, Jintai Chen, Yingzhou Lu, Minjie Shen, Lulu Chen, Zhiding Liang, Tianfan Fu, Xiao-Yang Liu
First: 2024-09-13T20:43:16+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-06T04:33:41+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Synthesizable molecular design (also known as synthesizable molecular optimization) is a fundamental problem in drug discovery, and involves designing novel molecular structures to improve their properties according to drug-relevant oracle functions (i.e., objective) while ensuring synthetic feasibility. However, existing methods are mostly based on random search. To address this issue, in this paper, we introduce a novel approach using the reinforcement learning method with quantum-inspired simulated annealing policy neural network to navigate the vast discrete space of chemical structures intelligently. Specifically, we employ a deterministic REINFORCE algorithm using policy neural networks to output transitional probability to guide state transitions and local search using genetic algorithm to refine solutions to a local optimum within each iteration. Our methods are evaluated with the Practical Molecular Optimization (PMO) benchmark framework with a 10K query budget. We further showcase the competitive performance of our method by comparing it against the state-of-the-art genetic algorithms-based method.
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of synthesizable drug design, where existing methods often rely on random search and struggle to efficiently navigate the vast chemical space. The authors propose a quantum-inspired reinforcement learning approach that combines a deterministic REINFORCE algorithm with a quantum-inspired simulated annealing policy neural network to guide state transitions, alongside a genetic algorithm for local refinement. Evaluated on the Practical Molecular Optimization (PMO) benchmark with a 10K query budget, the method demonstrates competitive performance against state-of-the-art genetic algorithm-based methods.
该论文针对可合成药物设计中的问题，现有方法多依赖随机搜索，难以高效探索庞大的化学空间。作者提出了一种量子启发式强化学习方法，结合确定性REINFORCE算法与量子启发式模拟退火策略神经网络来指导状态转移，并利用遗传算法进行局部优化。在Practical Molecular Optimization (PMO)基准框架下，以10K查询预算进行评估，该方法展现出与最先进的遗传算法方法相媲美的竞争性能。
Data-dependent Exploration for Online Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback
Authors: Zhen-Yu Zhang, Yuting Tang, Jiandong Zhang, Lanjihong Ma, Masashi Sugiyama
First: 2026-05-06T03:56:45+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-06T03:56:45+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Online reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF) has emerged as a promising paradigm for aligning large language models (LLMs) by continuously collecting new preference feedback during training. A foundational challenge in this setting is exploration, which requires algorithms that enable the LLMs to generate informative comparisons that improve sample-efficiency in online RLHF. Existing exploration strategies often derive bonuses via on-policy expectations, which are difficult to estimate reliably from the limited historical preference data available during training; as a result, the policy can prematurely down-weight under-explored regions that may contain high-value behaviors. In this paper, we propose data-dependent exploration for preference optimization (DEPO), a simple and scalable method that leverages historical data to construct an extra uncertainty bonus for high-uncertainty regions, encouraging exploration toward potentially high-value data. Theoretically, we provide a data-dependent regret bound for the proposed algorithm, showing that it adapts to the hardness of the learning task itself and can be tighter than worst-case bounds in practice. Empirically, the proposed method consistently outperforms strong baselines across benchmarks, demonstrating improved sample efficiency.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于数据依赖的在线人类反馈强化学习探索方法
在线人类反馈强化学习（RLHF）通过在训练过程中持续收集新的偏好反馈，已成为对齐大语言模型（LLMs）的一种有前景的范式。该场景下的一个基础挑战是探索，这要求算法能够使LLMs生成信息丰富的比较，从而提高在线RLHF的样本效率。现有的探索策略通常通过在线策略期望推导奖励加成，但这类期望难以从训练期间有限的偏好历史数据中可靠估计；因此，策略可能过早降低对可能包含高价值行为的未充分探索区域的权重。本文提出了一种简单且可扩展的方法——基于数据依赖的偏好优化探索（DEPO），该方法利用历史数据为高不确定性区域构建额外的奖励加成，鼓励向潜在高价值数据进行探索。理论上，我们为所提算法提供了数据依赖的遗憾界，表明其能自适应学习任务的难度，并在实践中比最坏情况界更紧。实验表明，该方法在多个基准测试中持续优于强基线，展现出更优的样本效率。
Provable Distributional Value Iteration under Partial Observability
Authors: Larry Preuett, Qiuyi Zhang, Muhammad Aurangzeb Ahmad
First: 2025-05-10T05:19:32+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-06T03:38:04+00:00
Comments: Accepted at the Reinforcement Learning Conference (RLC) 2026. Code available at: https://github.com/lpreuettUW/distributional_point_based_value_iteration
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
In many real-world planning tasks, agents must tackle uncertainty about the environment's state and variability in the outcomes induced by stochastic dynamics and rewards. Motivated by recent progress in world model approaches, where latent models approximate beliefs and support planning, we extend Distributional Reinforcement Learning (DistRL), which models the entire return distribution for fully observable domains, to Partially Observable Markov Decision Processes (POMDPs). Concretely, we introduce new distributional Bellman operators for partial observability and prove their convergence under the supremum p-Wasserstein metric. We also propose a finite representation of these return distributions via psi-vectors, generalizing the classical alpha-vectors in POMDP solvers. Building on this, we develop Distributional Point-Based Value Iteration (DPBVI), which integrates psi-vectors into a standard point-based backup procedure, bridging DistRL and POMDP planning. Our experiments demonstrate that DPBVI recovers classical Point-Based Value Iteration (PBVI) in the risk-neutral case, validating the distributional extension.
中文标题/摘要
标题：部分可观测性下的可证明分布值迭代
在许多现实世界的规划任务中，智能体必须应对环境状态的不确定性以及由随机动态和奖励导致的结果变异性。受近期世界模型方法进展的启发（其中潜在模型近似信念并支持规划），我们将分布强化学习（DistRL，该框架为完全可观测域建模整个回报分布）扩展到部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程（POMDP）。具体而言，我们引入了针对部分可观测性的新分布贝尔曼算子，并证明了它们在 supremum p-Wasserstein 度量下的收敛性。我们还通过 psi-向量提出了这些回报分布的有限表示，推广了 POMDP 求解器中的经典 alpha-向量。在此基础上，我们开发了基于分布点的值迭代（DPBVI），该方法将 psi-向量集成到标准基于点的备份过程中，从而桥接了 DistRL 与 POMDP 规划。我们的实验表明，在风险中性情况下，DPBVI 恢复了经典的基于点的值迭代（PBVI），验证了分布扩展的有效性。

Experiments show that DPBVI recovers classical Point-Based Value Iteration (PBVI) in the risk-neutral case, validating the distributional extension.

Joint Optimization of Trajectory Control, Resource Allocation, and Task Offloading for Multi-UAV-Assisted IoV
Authors: Maoxin Ji, Qiong Wu, Pingyi Fan, Cui Zhang, Nan Cheng, Wen Chen, Khaled B. Letaief
First: 2026-05-06T02:59:18+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-06T02:59:18+00:00
Comments: This paper has been submitted to TMC
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This paper investigates a multi-Unmanned Aerial Vehicle (UAV) joint base station-assisted Internet of Vehicles (IoV) task offloading system in dense urban environments. To minimize system delay and energy consumption under strict coupling constraints, the complex non-convex optimization problem is decoupled into a hierarchical execution framework. First, a sequential distributed optimization algorithm based on Second-Order Cone Programming (SOCP) is proposed to optimize the 3D flight trajectory of each UAV, ensuring adaptive network coverage. Second, a novel hybrid resource scheduling paradigm synergizing Deep Reinforcement Learning (DRL) and Large Language Models (LLMs) is developed. Within this framework, the DRL agent dictates the initial resource allocation, while the LLM acts as a semantic macro-scheduler to rectify long-tail allocation imbalances for failed and surplus tasks. Crucially, a reward decoupling mechanism is introduced to isolate DRL training from external LLM interventions, thereby ensuring policy convergence. Finally, the task offloading ratios are precisely determined via Linear Programming (LP) within an alternating optimization loop. Simulation results demonstrate that the proposed method significantly outperforms traditional multi-agent reinforcement learning baselines in terms of task success rate and system efficiency.

The Implicit Curriculum: Learning Dynamics in RL with Verifiable Rewards
Authors: Yu Huang, Zixin Wen, Yuejie Chi, Yuting Wei, Aarti Singh, Yingbin Liang, Yuxin Chen
Venue: ICML
First: 2026-02-16T16:03:08+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-06T02:53:05+00:00
Comments: Updated version after ICML acceptance
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) has been a main driver of recent breakthroughs in large reasoning models. Yet it remains a mystery how rewards based solely on final outcomes can help overcome the long-horizon barrier to extended reasoning. To understand this, we develop a theory of the training dynamics of RLVR for transformers on compositional reasoning tasks. Our theory shows that mixed-difficulty training naturally follows an implicit curriculum: without any explicit schedule, easier problems become learnable first and shape the frontier for harder ones, creating a learning progression from easy to hard during optimization. The effectiveness of this curriculum is governed by the smoothness of the difficulty spectrum. When the spectrum is smooth, training dynamics enters a well-behaved relay regime, in which persistent gradient signals on easier problems make slightly harder ones tractable and keep training at the edge of competence. When the spectrum contains abrupt discontinuities, training undergoes grokking-type phase transitions with prolonged plateaus before progress recurs. As a technical contribution, our analysis develops and adapts techniques from Fourier analysis on finite groups to our setting. We validate the predicted mechanisms empirically via synthetic experiments.
中文标题/摘要
标题：隐式课程：基于可验证奖励的强化学习中的学习动态
基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）是近期大型推理模型突破的主要驱动力。然而，仅基于最终结果的奖励如何帮助克服长程推理的长期障碍仍是一个谜。为理解这一点，我们针对组合推理任务上的Transformer，建立了RLVR训练动态的理论。我们的理论表明，混合难度训练自然遵循隐式课程：无需任何显式调度，较简单的问题首先变得可学习，并塑造较难问题的前沿，从而在优化过程中形成从易到难的学习进程。该课程的有效性由难度谱的平滑性决定。当谱平滑时，训练动态进入一个行为良好的中继模式，其中对较简单问题的持续梯度信号使稍难问题变得可处理，并使训练保持在能力边缘。当谱中存在突变不连续性时，训练会经历类似grokking的相变，在进展恢复前出现长时间的平台期。作为技术贡献，我们的分析开发并改编了有限群上的傅里叶分析技术以适应我们的场景。我们通过合成实验实证验证了预测的机制。

The analysis employs Fourier analysis on finite groups, and synthetic experiments validate the predicted mechanisms.

A Brief Overview: Agentic Reinforcement Learning In Large Language Models
Authors: Fangming Cui, Ruixiao Zhu, Cheng Fang, Sunan Li, Jiahong Li
First: 2026-04-30T13:43:25+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-06T01:22:36+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning (RL) has traditionally focused on training specialized agents to optimize predefined reward functions within narrowly defined environments. However, the advent of powerful Large Language Models (LLMs) and increasingly complex, open-ended tasks has catalyzed a paradigm shift towards agentic paradigms within RL. This emerging framework extends beyond traditional RL by emphasizing the development of autonomous agents capable of goal-setting, long-term planning, dynamic strategy adaptation, and interactive reasoning in uncertain, real-world environments. Unlike conventional approaches that rely heavily on static objectives and episodic interactions, LLM-based Agentic RL incorporates cognitive-like capabilities such as meta-reasoning, self-reflection, and multi-step decision-making directly into the learning loop. In this paper, we provide a deep insight for looking the conceptual foundations, methodological innovations, and effective designs underlying this trend. Furthermore, we identify critical challenges and outline promising future directions for building LLM-based Agentic RL.

Extending Differential Temporal Difference Methods for Episodic Problems
Authors: Kris De Asis, Mohamed Elsayed, Jiamin He
First: 2026-05-06T00:10:17+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-06T00:10:17+00:00
Comments: RLC 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Differential temporal difference (TD) methods are value-based reinforcement learning algorithms that have been proposed for infinite-horizon problems. They rely on reward centering, where each reward is centered by the average reward. This keeps the return bounded and removes a value function's state-independent offset. However, reward centering can alter the optimal policy in episodic problems, limiting its applicability. Motivated by recent works that emphasize the role of normalization in streaming deep reinforcement learning, we study reward centering in episodic problems and propose a generalization of differential TD. We prove that this generalization maintains the ordering of policies in the presence of termination, and thus extends differential TD to episodic problems. We show equivalence with a form of linear TD, thereby inheriting theoretical guarantees that have been shown for those algorithms. We then extend several streaming reinforcement learning algorithms to their differential counterparts. Across a range of base algorithms and environments, we empirically validate that reward centering can improve sample efficiency in episodic problems.
中文标题/摘要
标题：将差分时序差分方法扩展到情节性问题
差分时序差分方法是针对无限时域问题提出的基于价值的强化学习算法。它们依赖于奖励中心化，即每个奖励都减去平均奖励。这保持了回报的有界性，并消除了价值函数中与状态无关的偏移。然而，奖励中心化可能会改变情节性问题中的最优策略，从而限制了其适用性。受近期强调归一化在流式深度强化学习中作用的研究启发，我们研究了情节性问题中的奖励中心化，并提出了差分时序差分的推广形式。我们证明，这种推广在存在终止条件的情况下保持了策略的排序，从而将差分时序差分扩展到情节性问题。我们展示了其与一种线性时序差分的等价性，从而继承了这些算法已有的理论保证。随后，我们将多种流式强化学习算法扩展到其差分版本。在一系列基础算法和环境上，我们通过实验验证了奖励中心化能够提高情节性问题中的样本效率。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the limitation of differential temporal difference (TD) methods, which were originally designed for infinite-horizon problems and rely on reward centering to keep returns bounded, but can alter optimal policies in episodic problems. The authors propose a generalization of differential TD that maintains policy ordering in the presence of termination, proving its equivalence to a form of linear TD to inherit theoretical guarantees. They extend several streaming reinforcement learning algorithms to their differential counterparts and empirically validate across a range of base algorithms and environments that reward centering improves sample efficiency in episodic problems.
本文针对差分时序差分方法在无限时域问题中依赖奖励中心化以保持回报有界，但在情节性问题中可能改变最优策略的局限性，提出了一种广义差分时序差分方法，证明该方法在存在终止条件时能保持策略排序，并通过与线性时序差分的等价性继承理论保证。作者将多种流式强化学习算法扩展为其差分版本，并在多种基础算法和环境上通过实验验证，奖励中心化能提升情节性问题的样本效率。
Optimal Control with Natural Images: Efficient Reinforcement Learning using Overcomplete Sparse Codes
Authors: Peter N. Loxley
First: 2024-12-12T03:14:47+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-05T23:38:18+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Optimal control and sequential decision making are widely used in many complex tasks. Optimal control over a sequence of natural images is a first step towards understanding the role of vision in control. Here, we formalize this problem as a reinforcement learning task, and derive general conditions under which an image includes enough information to implement an optimal policy. Reinforcement learning is shown to provide a computationally efficient method for finding optimal policies when natural images are encoded into "efficient" image representations. This is demonstrated by introducing a new reinforcement learning benchmark that easily scales to large numbers of states and long horizons. In particular, by representing each image as an overcomplete sparse code, we are able to efficiently solve an optimal control task that is orders of magnitude larger than those tasks solvable using complete codes. Theoretical justification for this behaviour is provided. This work also demonstrates that deep learning is not necessary for efficient optimal control with natural images.
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses optimal control over sequences of natural images by formalizing it as a reinforcement learning problem, deriving conditions for images to contain sufficient information for optimal policies. The method uses overcomplete sparse coding to encode images into efficient representations, enabling computationally efficient reinforcement learning. Experimental results on a new scalable benchmark show that this approach solves control tasks orders of magnitude larger than those solvable with complete codes, demonstrating that deep learning is not required for efficient optimal control with natural images.
该论文将自然图像序列上的最优控制问题形式化为强化学习任务，推导了图像包含足够信息以实现最优策略的一般条件。方法采用过完备稀疏编码将图像编码为高效表示，从而支持计算高效的强化学习。在新提出的可扩展基准测试上的实验结果表明，该方法能解决比使用完备编码大数个数量级的控制任务，并证明深度学习并非实现自然图像高效最优控制的必要条件。
Efficiently Aligning Language Models with Online Natural Language Feedback
Authors: Christine Ye, Joe Benton
First: 2026-05-05T23:25:00+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-05T23:25:00+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards has been used to elicit impressive performance from language models in many domains. But, broadly beneficial deployments of AI may require us to train models with strong capabilities in "fuzzy", hard-to-supervise domains. In this paper, we develop methods to align language models in fuzzy domains where human experts are still able to provide high-quality supervision signal, but only for a small number of model outputs, using online natural language feedback. Specifically, we train models by iteratively optimizing against proxy reward signals, stopping at the point of over-optimization, collecting fresh expert supervision, and updating the proxy reward. We construct proxy reward models from language models using in-context learning (ICL) and fine-tuning. We test our methods by eliciting creative writing and alignment research capabilities in Qwen3-8B and Haiku 4.5 respectively. For Qwen3-8B, ICL methods recover up to 35% of performance with 50x fewer expert samples, while fine-tuning methods recover 80% with up to 20x fewer samples and 100% with 3x fewer samples. For Haiku 4.5, ICL methods recover up to 35% of performance with 30x fewer samples, and fine-tuning methods recover 100% with 10x fewer samples. Our results suggest that online natural language feedback can substantially improve the data efficiency of expert supervision.
中文标题/摘要
标题：利用在线自然语言反馈高效对齐语言模型
基于可验证奖励的强化学习已在多个领域成功激发语言模型的卓越性能。然而，广泛有益的AI部署可能需要我们在“模糊”、难以监督的领域训练具备强大能力的模型。本文开发了在模糊领域中对齐语言模型的方法——人类专家仍能提供高质量监督信号，但仅针对少量模型输出，且采用在线自然语言反馈形式。具体而言，我们通过迭代优化代理奖励信号来训练模型，在过度优化点停止，收集新的专家监督，并更新代理奖励。我们利用上下文学习（ICL）和微调从语言模型构建代理奖励模型。通过分别在Qwen3-8B和Haiku 4.5上激发创意写作与对齐研究能力来测试方法。对于Qwen3-8B，ICL方法以50倍更少的专家样本恢复高达35%的性能，微调方法以20倍更少的样本恢复80%性能，以3倍更少的样本恢复100%性能。对于Haiku 4.5，ICL方法以30倍更少的样本恢复高达35%性能，微调方法以10倍更少的样本恢复100%性能。结果表明，在线自然语言反馈能显著提升专家监督的数据效率。

A semicontinuous relaxation of Saito's criterion and freeness as angular minimization
Authors: Tomás S. R. Silva
First: 2026-04-03T12:20:09+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-05T21:28:00+00:00
Comments: Major revision: section reorganization with computational details moved to appendices. 26 pages, 3 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We introduce a nonnegative functional $\mathfrak{S}$ on the space of line arrangements in $\mathbb{P}^2$ that vanishes precisely on free arrangements, obtained as a semicontinuous relaxation of Saito's criterion. Given an arrangement $\mathcal{A}$ of $n$ lines with candidate exponents $(d_1, d_2)$, we parameterize the spaces of logarithmic derivations of degrees $d_1$ and $d_2$ via the null spaces of the associated derivation matrices and express the Saito determinant as a bilinear map into the space of degree-$n$ polynomials. The functional admits a natural geometric interpretation: it measures the squared sine of the angle between the image of this bilinear map and the direction of the defining polynomial $Q(\mathcal{A})$ in coefficient space, providing a computable measure of how far an arrangement is from admitting a free basis of logarithmic derivations of the expected degrees. We prove that $\mathfrak{S}$ is upper semicontinuous on natural strata, and use this to give a functional reformulation of Terao's conjecture. Beyond its theoretical interest, $\mathfrak{S}$ provides a viable computational handle on the landscape of free arrangements. We illustrate this through two complementary roles: as a smooth reward signal driving a reinforcement learning search for moderate $n$, and as a fast pre-filter accelerating an algebraic extension procedure for larger $n$. For $n \leq 13$, the reinforcement learning system discovers hundreds of verified free arrangements spanning all admissible exponent types. For $n \geq 14$, where the reinforcement learning reward signal becomes insufficient, the hybrid extension procedure -- combined with classical supersolvable constructions -- produces at least one verified free arrangement for every admissible exponent pair $(d_1, d_2)$ with $n \leq 20$.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Saito准则的半连续松弛与作为角度最小化的自由性
我们在射影平面$\mathbb{P}^2$上的线排列空间中引入一个非负泛函$\mathfrak{S}$，该泛函恰好对自由排列为零，是通过Saito准则的半连续松弛得到的。给定一个由$n$条线组成的排列$\mathcal{A}$及其候选指数$(d_1, d_2)$，我们通过关联推导矩阵的零空间参数化次数为$d_1$和$d_2$的对数推导空间，并将Saito行列式表示为从双线性映射到次数为$n$的多项式空间。该泛函具有自然的几何解释：它测量该双线性映射的像与定义多项式$Q(\mathcal{A})$在系数空间中的方向之间夹角的正弦平方，从而提供了一个可计算的度量，用于衡量一个排列与具有预期次数的对数推导自由基的接近程度。我们证明$\mathfrak{S}$在自然分层上是上半连续的，并利用这一点给出了Terao猜想的泛函重述。 除了理论意义外，$\mathfrak{S}$为自由排列的景观提供了可行的计算手段。我们通过两个互补角色来说明这一点：作为驱动中等$n$值强化学习搜索的平滑奖励信号，以及作为加速较大$n$值代数扩展过程的快速预过滤器。对于$n \leq 13$，强化学习系统发现了数百个经过验证的自由排列，涵盖了所有可接受的指数类型。对于$n \geq 14$，当强化学习奖励信号变得不足时，混合扩展过程——结合经典的超可解构造——为每个$n \leq 20$的可接受指数对$(d_1, d_2)$至少产生一个经过验证的自由排列。
Summary / 总结
This paper introduces a nonnegative functional called S that vanishes precisely on free line arrangements in the projective plane, derived as a semicontinuous relaxation of Saito's criterion. The method parameterizes spaces of logarithmic derivations using derivation matrices and expresses the Saito determinant as a bilinear map, interpreting the functional as the squared sine of the angle between the map's image and the defining polynomial's direction in coefficient space, which measures how far an arrangement is from being free. Experimentally, for n up to 13, reinforcement learning using S as a reward signal discovers hundreds of verified free arrangements across all admissible exponent types; for n from 14 to 20, a hybrid extension procedure combined with supersolvable constructions produces at least one verified free arrangement for every admissible exponent pair.
本文引入了一个非负泛函S，它恰好消没于射影平面中的自由线排列，该泛函通过Saito准则的半连续松弛得到。方法利用导子矩阵参数化对数导子空间，并将Saito行列式表示为双线性映射，将泛函解释为该映射像与定义多项式方向在系数空间中夹角的正弦平方，从而衡量排列偏离自由的程度。实验上，对于n不超过13的情况，以S作为奖励信号的强化学习发现了数百个涵盖所有允许指数类型的已验证自由排列；对于n从14到20的情况，结合超可解构造的混合扩展程序为每个允许的指数对至少产生一个已验证的自由排列。
Hardware-Aware Neural Feature Extraction for Resource-Constrained Devices
Authors: Francesco Tosini, Simone Pedroni, Christian Veronesi, Pietro Bartoli, Marco Paracchini, Marco Marcon, Diana Trojaniello
Venue: CVPR
First: 2026-05-05T20:32:00+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-05T20:32:00+00:00
Comments: This paper has been accepted for publication at the IEEE Conference on Computer Vision and Pattern Recognition (CVPR) Workshops, 2026. \c{opyright}IEEE
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Visual SLAM is a core component of spatial computing systems, yet deploying learned local feature extractors on microcontroller-class hardware remains challenging due to memory, bandwidth, and quantization constraints. While modern neural descriptors provide strong robustness, their practical adoption is often hindered by system-level bottlenecks that are not captured by FLOP-based efficiency metrics. In this work, we introduce Gideon, a hardware-aware neural feature extractor explicitly designed for resource-constrained devices. Our approach combines relational knowledge distillation from a SuperPoint teacher with differentiable neural architecture search (DNAS) under strict memory and operator constraints. Unlike conventional design pipelines, we treat quantization stability and dynamic-range compactness as first-class objectives. We show that architectural choices such as replacing Batch Normalization with affine layers significantly improve INT8 robustness, and that descriptor dimensionality directly governs quantization resilience. Deployed on STM32N6, Gideon achieves 9.003 ms inference time (111 fps) while remaining below a 1.5 MB memory footprint. Remarkably, INT8 quantization induces negligible degradation and occasionally matches full-precision performance. These results demonstrate that robust learned feature extraction can be reconciled with embedded hardware constraints through holistic hardware-algorithm co-design.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向资源受限设备的硬件感知神经特征提取
视觉SLAM是空间计算系统的核心组件，然而，由于内存、带宽和量化约束，在微控制器级硬件上部署学习型局部特征提取器仍然具有挑战性。虽然现代神经描述符提供了强大的鲁棒性，但其实际应用常受限于基于FLOP效率指标无法捕捉的系统级瓶颈。在本工作中，我们提出了Gideon，一种专为资源受限设备设计的硬件感知神经特征提取器。我们的方法结合了来自SuperPoint教师的关系知识蒸馏与在严格内存和算子约束下的可微神经架构搜索（DNAS）。与传统设计流程不同，我们将量化稳定性和动态范围紧凑性视为首要目标。我们表明，诸如用仿射层替换批归一化等架构选择能显著提升INT8鲁棒性，且描述符维度直接决定量化弹性。部署在STM32N6上，Gideon在保持低于1.5 MB内存占用的同时实现了9.003毫秒推理时间（111帧/秒）。值得注意的是，INT8量化引起的性能退化可忽略不计，有时甚至与全精度性能相当。这些结果表明，通过全面的硬件-算法协同设计，鲁棒的学习型特征提取可以与嵌入式硬件约束相协调。

Explaining and Preventing Alignment Collapse in Iterative RLHF
Authors: Etienne Gauthier, Francis Bach, Michael I. Jordan
First: 2026-05-05T20:01:36+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-05T20:01:36+00:00
Comments: Code at: https://github.com/GauthierE/fpo
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF) typically assumes a static or non-strategic reward model (RM). In iterative deployment, however, the policy generates the data on which the RM is retrained, creating a feedback loop. Building on the Stackelberg game formulation of this interaction, we derive an analytical decomposition of the policy's true optimization gradient into a standard policy gradient and a parameter-steering term that captures the policy's influence on the RM's future parameters. We show that standard iterative RLHF, which drops this steering term entirely, suffers from alignment collapse: the policy systematically exploits the RM's blind spots, producing low-quality, high-reward outputs whose feedback reinforces the very errors it exploits. To mitigate this, we propose foresighted policy optimization (FPO), a mechanism-design intervention that restores the missing steering term by regularizing the policy's parameter-steering effect on RM updates. We instantiate FPO via a scalable first-order approximation and demonstrate that it prevents alignment collapse on both controlled environments and an LLM alignment pipeline using Llama-3.2-1B.
中文标题/摘要
标题：解释与预防迭代RLHF中的对齐崩溃
基于人类反馈的强化学习（RLHF）通常假设一个静态或非策略性的奖励模型（RM）。然而，在迭代部署中，策略生成用于重新训练RM的数据，从而形成反馈循环。基于这种交互的Stackelberg博弈形式化，我们推导出策略真实优化梯度的解析分解，将其分为标准策略梯度和一个参数引导项，后者捕捉策略对RM未来参数的影响。我们表明，完全忽略这一引导项的标准迭代RLHF会遭受对齐崩溃：策略系统地利用RM的盲点，产生低质量、高奖励的输出，其反馈强化了所利用的错误。为缓解这一问题，我们提出前瞻性策略优化（FPO），这是一种机制设计干预，通过正则化策略对RM更新的参数引导效应来恢复缺失的引导项。我们通过可扩展的一阶近似实例化FPO，并证明其在受控环境和基于Llama-3.2-1B的大语言模型对齐流程中均能防止对齐崩溃。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses alignment collapse in iterative reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF), where the policy generates data for retraining the reward model (RM), creating a feedback loop that leads to exploitation of RM blind spots. The authors derive an analytical decomposition of the policy's true optimization gradient, revealing a missing parameter-steering term in standard iterative RLHF that causes alignment collapse. To mitigate this, they propose foresighted policy optimization (FPO), a mechanism-design intervention that regularizes the policy's influence on RM updates via a scalable first-order approximation. Experiments on controlled environments and an LLM alignment pipeline using Llama-3.2-1B demonstrate that FPO effectively prevents alignment collapse, producing higher-quality outputs.
该论文研究了迭代强化学习从人类反馈（RLHF）中的对齐崩溃问题，其中策略生成的数据用于重新训练奖励模型（RM），形成反馈循环，导致策略系统性地利用RM的盲点。作者推导了策略真实优化梯度的解析分解，揭示了标准迭代RLHF中缺失的参数引导项是导致对齐崩溃的原因。为此，他们提出了前瞻性策略优化（FPO），一种通过可扩展的一阶近似来正则化策略对RM更新影响的机制设计干预。在受控环境和基于Llama-3.2-1B的大语言模型对齐流水线上的实验表明，FPO有效防止了对齐崩溃，生成了更高质量的输出。
Hierarchical Support Vector State Partitioning for Distilling Black Box Reinforcement Learning Policies
Authors: Senne Deproost, Mehrdad Asadi, Ann Nowé
First: 2026-05-05T19:40:05+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-05T19:40:05+00:00
Comments: Accepted for poster presentation at HHAI 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We introduce State Vector Space Partitioning (SVSP), a novel method to mimic a black box reinforcement learning policy using a set of human-interpretable subpolicies. By partitioning a distillation dataset of state action pairs with linear support vector machine splits, SVSP constructs a compact and structured representation of the original policy. Our method improves mean return by +7.4\% over previous critic driven state partitioning attempts such as Voronoi State Partitioning (VSP) and +2.8\% over the original TD3 policy, while reducing the number of required subpolicies against VSP by 82.1\%. Our results pave the path towards a more flexible form of distillation where both the decision boundary and surrogate models can be chosen within a margin of the original black box behavior.
中文标题/摘要
标题：层次化支持向量状态划分：用于蒸馏黑箱强化学习策略
我们提出状态向量空间划分（SVSP），一种通过一组人类可解释的子策略来模仿黑箱强化学习策略的新方法。通过使用线性支持向量机划分对状态-动作对的蒸馏数据集，SVSP构建了原始策略的紧凑且结构化的表示。我们的方法相比先前基于评论家的状态划分尝试（如Voronoi状态划分VSP）平均回报提升+7.4%，相比原始TD3策略提升+2.8%，同时所需子策略数量较VSP减少82.1%。我们的结果为更灵活的蒸馏形式铺平了道路，其中决策边界和替代模型均可在原始黑箱行为的一定范围内选择。

The paper introduces Hierarchical Support Vector State Partitioning (SVSP), a method for distilling black-box reinforcement learning policies into interpretable subpolicies. The motivation is to create human-understandable representations of complex policies by partitioning state-action pairs using linear support vector machine splits. RouteFormer: A Transformer-Based Routing Framework for Autonomous Vehicles
Authors: Yazan Youssef, Paulo Ricardo Marques de Araujo, Aboelmagd Noureldin, Sidney Givigi
First: 2025-04-07T18:23:13+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-05T18:59:15+00:00
Comments: 10 pages, the title and abstract are modified after peer review process to better reflect the scope of the paper. More validation tests were added as well
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Autonomous surveillance missions in Internet of Things (IoT) networks often involve solving NP-hard combinatorial optimization problems to ensure efficient resource utilization. To address the limitations of conventional heuristics in dynamic environments, we propose RouteFormer, a novel framework for single-agent routing in graph-based terrains. RouteFormer creates a synergy between the global context awareness of the transformer self-attention mechanism and the adaptive decision-making capabilities of Reinforcement Learning (RL). This architecture allows the system to output optimized routing decisions that adapt to complex task dependencies and resource availability without requiring labeled training datasets. We evaluated RouteFormer on varying graph sizes designed to resemble realistic reconnaissance missions. The results indicate that our model effectively handles the complexity of missions requiring multiple action profiles, outperforming baseline approaches, in terms of both time and distance. Specifically, RouteFormer achieved 10\% and 7\% reduction in distance compared to the solutions obtained from well-established solvers like Concorde and Lin-Kernighan-Helsgaun-3 (LKH-3). This improvement was achieved by effectively incorporating mission-specific constraints that traditional solvers overlook. The proposed framework serves as a modular, scalable pipeline for diverse autonomous scheduling and routing tasks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：RouteFormer：基于Transformer的自动驾驶车辆路径规划框架
物联网（IoT）网络中的自主监视任务通常需要解决NP难的组合优化问题，以确保高效的资源利用。针对传统启发式方法在动态环境中的局限性，我们提出了RouteFormer，一种用于图基地形中单智能体路径规划的新框架。RouteFormer融合了Transformer自注意力机制的全局上下文感知能力与强化学习（RL）的自适应决策能力。该架构使系统能够输出优化的路径决策，适应复杂的任务依赖关系和资源可用性，而无需标注训练数据集。我们在模拟真实侦察任务的不同规模图上评估了RouteFormer。结果表明，我们的模型有效处理了需要多种行动模式的任务复杂性，在时间和距离上均优于基线方法。具体而言，与Concorde和Lin-Kernighan-Helsgaun-3（LKH-3）等成熟求解器获得的解相比，RouteFormer在距离上减少了10%和7%。这一改进是通过有效整合传统求解器忽略的任务特定约束实现的。该框架可作为模块化、可扩展的流水线，适用于多种自主调度与路径规划任务。

RouteFormer addresses the NP-hard combinatorial optimization problem of single-agent routing in dynamic IoT surveillance environments by proposing a transformer-based framework that integrates self-attention for global context awareness with reinforcement learning for adaptive decision-making, eliminating the need for labeled data. Constraint-Enhanced Reinforcement Learning Based on Dynamic Decoupled Spherical Radial Squashing
Authors: Qijun Liao, Zhaoxin Yu, Jue Yang
First: 2026-05-05T18:24:46+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-05T18:24:46+00:00
Comments: 27 pages, 60 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
When deploying reinforcement learning policies to physical robots, actuator rate constraints -- hard limits on how fast each joint can move per control step -- are unavoidable. These limits vary substantially across joints due to differences in motor inertia, power bandwidth, and transmission stiffness, creating pronounced heterogeneity that existing methods fail to handle geometrically: the per-joint feasible region forms a high-dimensional box in action-increment space, yet QP projection and spherical parameterization methods impose isotropic ball-shaped constraints, exponentially under-covering the true feasible set as heterogeneity grows. This paper proposes Dynamic Decoupled Spherical Radial Squashing (DD-SRad), which resolves this mismatch by computing a position-adaptive radius independently for each actuator, achieving tight alignment with the true per-joint feasible region. DD-SRad satisfies per-step hard constraints with probability~1, preserves well-conditioned gradients throughout training, and admits exact policy gradient backpropagation with zero runtime solver overhead. MuJoCo benchmark experiments demonstrate the highest task return at zero constraint violation -- matching the unconstrained upper bound -- with 30%--50% improvement in constraint-space coverage over spherical baselines. High-fidelity IsaacLab simulations with Unitree H1 and G1 humanoid robots confirm end-to-end optimality parameterized directly from official joint specifications, validating a systematic pathway from hardware datasheets to safe deployment.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于动态解耦球面径向挤压的约束增强强化学习
在将强化学习策略部署到物理机器人时，执行器速率约束——每个关节在每个控制步长内可移动速度的硬限制——是不可避免的。由于电机惯性、功率带宽和传动刚度的差异，这些限制在不同关节间差异显著，形成明显的异质性，而现有方法无法从几何角度处理这一问题：每个关节的可行区域在动作增量空间中构成一个高维盒子，但QP投影和球面参数化方法施加的是各向同性的球状约束，随着异质性增加，对真实可行集的覆盖呈指数级不足。本文提出动态解耦球面径向挤压（DD-SRad），通过为每个执行器独立计算位置自适应半径来解决这一不匹配问题，从而与真实关节可行区域紧密对齐。DD-SRad以概率1满足每步硬约束，在整个训练过程中保持良好条件的梯度，并支持精确的策略梯度反向传播，且运行时求解器开销为零。MuJoCo基准实验表明，在零约束违反的情况下实现了最高任务回报——与无约束上界匹配——相比球面基线方法，约束空间覆盖率提升30%–50%。使用宇树H1和G1人形机器人的高保真IsaacLab仿真验证了直接从官方关节规格参数化的端到端最优性，确立了从硬件数据表到安全部署的系统化路径。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of enforcing heterogeneous actuator rate constraints in reinforcement learning for physical robots, where existing methods like QP projection or spherical parameterization impose isotropic ball-shaped constraints that poorly match the true high-dimensional box-shaped feasible region. The authors propose Dynamic Decoupled Spherical Radial Squashing (DD-SRad), which computes a position-adaptive radius for each joint independently to tightly align with per-joint limits, ensuring hard constraint satisfaction with probability 1, maintaining well-conditioned gradients, and enabling exact policy gradient backpropagation without runtime solvers. MuJoCo experiments show the method achieves the highest task return with zero constraint violation, matching the unconstrained upper bound, and improves constraint-space coverage by 30-50% over spherical baselines, while IsaacLab simulations with Unitree H1 and G1 humanoid robots validate end-to-end optimality using official joint specifications.
本文针对物理机器人强化学习中异构执行器速率约束的挑战，现有方法如QP投影或球形参数化施加各向同性的球状约束，与真实的高维盒状可行区域严重不匹配。作者提出动态解耦球形径向挤压（DD-SRad），为每个关节独立计算位置自适应半径以紧密对齐关节限制，确保硬约束满足概率为1，保持梯度良好条件，并实现精确的策略梯度反向传播而无需运行时求解器。MuJoCo实验表明，该方法在零约束违反下获得最高任务回报，匹配无约束上界，且约束空间覆盖率比球形基线提升30-50%，IsaacLab中Unitree H1和G1人形机器人的仿真验证了从官方关节规格到端到端最优性的系统路径。
How Does the Lagrangian Guide Safe Reinforcement Learning through Diffusion Models?
Authors: Xiaoyuan Cheng, Wenxuan Yuan, Boyang Li, Yuanchao Xu, Yiming Yang, Hao Liang, Bei Peng, Robert Loftin, Zhuo Sun, Yukun Hu
First: 2026-02-02T23:53:53+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-05T18:05:36+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Diffusion policy sampling enables reinforcement learning (RL) to represent multimodal action distributions beyond suboptimal unimodal Gaussian policies. However, existing diffusion-based RL methods primarily focus on offline settings for reward maximization, with limited consideration of safety in online settings. To address this gap, we propose Augmented Lagrangian-Guided Diffusion (ALGD), a novel algorithm for off-policy safe RL. By revisiting optimization theory and energy-based model, we show that the instability of primal-dual methods arises from the non-convex Lagrangian landscape. In diffusion-based safe RL, the Lagrangian can be interpreted as an energy function guiding the denoising dynamics. Counterintuitively, direct usage destabilizes both policy generation and training. ALGD resolves this issue by introducing an augmented Lagrangian that locally convexifies the energy landscape, yielding a stabilized policy generation and training process without altering the distribution of the optimal policy. Theoretical analysis and extensive experiments demonstrate that ALGD is both theoretically grounded and empirically effective, achieving strong and stable performance across diverse environments.
中文标题/摘要
标题：拉格朗日函数如何通过扩散模型引导安全强化学习？
扩散策略采样使强化学习能够表示超越次优单峰高斯策略的多模态动作分布。然而，现有基于扩散的强化学习方法主要关注离线环境下的奖励最大化，对在线环境中的安全性考虑有限。为解决这一问题，我们提出增广拉格朗日引导扩散（ALGD），一种用于离策略安全强化学习的新算法。通过重新审视优化理论和基于能量的模型，我们表明原始-对偶方法的不稳定性源于非凸的拉格朗日景观。在基于扩散的安全强化学习中，拉格朗日函数可解释为引导去噪动力学的能量函数。反直觉的是，直接使用会同时破坏策略生成和训练的稳定性。ALGD通过引入增广拉格朗日函数局部凸化能量景观来解决此问题，在不改变最优策略分布的情况下实现稳定的策略生成和训练过程。理论分析和大量实验表明，ALGD既具有理论依据又具有实证有效性，在多种环境中实现了强大且稳定的性能。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of incorporating safety constraints into reinforcement learning (RL) with diffusion-based policies, which are effective for multimodal action distributions but have been mainly studied in offline reward-maximization settings. The authors propose Augmented Lagrangian-Guided Diffusion (ALGD), a method that revisits optimization theory and energy-based models to stabilize the primal-dual training process in safe RL. They identify that the instability stems from the non-convex Lagrangian landscape and resolve it by introducing an augmented Lagrangian that locally convexifies the energy function, guiding the denoising dynamics without altering the optimal policy distribution. Theoretical analysis and extensive experiments across diverse environments demonstrate that ALGD achieves strong and stable performance, outperforming existing methods in both safety and reward metrics.
该论文针对扩散策略在强化学习中的安全约束问题，现有方法主要关注离线奖励最大化，缺乏对在线安全性的考虑。作者提出增广拉格朗日引导扩散（ALGD）算法，通过重新审视优化理论和能量模型，发现原始-对偶方法的不稳定性源于非凸的拉格朗日景观。ALGD引入增广拉格朗日函数，局部凸化能量景观，从而稳定策略生成和训练过程，且不改变最优策略分布。理论分析和大量实验表明，ALGD在多种环境中均能实现强健且稳定的性能，在安全性和奖励指标上均优于现有方法。
OpenSeeker-v2: Pushing the Limits of Search Agents with Informative and High-Difficulty Trajectories
Authors: Yuwen Du, Rui Ye, Shuo Tang, Keduan Huang, Xinyu Zhu, Yuzhu Cai, Siheng Chen
First: 2026-05-05T17:55:25+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-05T17:55:25+00:00
Comments: 7 pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Deep search capabilities have become an indispensable competency for frontier Large Language Model (LLM) agents, yet their development remains dominated by industrial giants. The typical industry recipe involves a highly resource-intensive pipeline spanning pre-training, continual pre-training (CPT), supervised fine-tuning (SFT), and reinforcement learning (RL). In this report, we show that when fueled with informative and high-difficulty trajectories, a simple SFT approach could be surprisingly powerful for training frontier search agents. By introducing three simple data synthesis modifications: scaling knowledge graph size for richer exploration, expanding the tool set size for broader functionality, and strict low-step filtering, we establish a stronger baseline. Trained on merely 10.6k data points, our OpenSeeker-v2 achieves state-of-the-art performance across 4 benchmarks (30B-sized agents with ReAct paradigm): 46.0% on BrowseComp, 58.1% on BrowseComp-ZH, 34.6% on Humanity's Last Exam, and 78.0% on xbench, surpassing even Tongyi DeepResearch trained with heavy CPT+SFT+RL pipeline, which achieves 43.4%, 46.7%, 32.9%, and 75.0%, respectively. Notably, OpenSeeker-v2 represents the first state-of-the-art search agent within its model scale and paradigm to be developed by a purely academic team using only SFT. We are excited to open-source the OpenSeeker-v2 model weights and share our simple yet effective findings to make frontier search agent research more accessible to the community.
中文标题/摘要
标题：OpenSeeker-v2：利用信息丰富且高难度的轨迹突破搜索智能体的极限
深度搜索能力已成为前沿大语言模型智能体不可或缺的技能，但其发展仍由工业巨头主导。典型的工业方案涉及高度资源密集的流程，涵盖预训练、持续预训练、监督微调和强化学习。本报告表明，当使用信息丰富且高难度的轨迹时，简单的监督微调方法在训练前沿搜索智能体方面可能出奇地有效。通过引入三项简单的数据合成改进：扩展知识图谱规模以促进更丰富的探索、扩大工具集规模以增强功能、以及严格的低步数过滤，我们建立了一个更强的基线。仅使用10.6k数据点训练的OpenSeeker-v2，在4个基准测试（30B规模智能体，采用ReAct范式）中达到了最先进性能：BrowseComp上46.0%，BrowseComp-ZH上58.1%，Humanity's Last Exam上34.6%，xbench上78.0%，甚至超越了使用大量持续预训练+监督微调+强化学习流程训练的Tongyi DeepResearch（其成绩分别为43.4%、46.7%、32.9%和75.0%）。值得注意的是，OpenSeeker-v2是首个由纯学术团队仅使用监督微调在其模型规模和范式内开发的最先进搜索智能体。我们很高兴开源OpenSeeker-v2模型权重，并分享我们简单而有效的发现，使前沿搜索智能体研究更易于社区访问。
