The paper introduces OpenSeeker-v2, a search agent that demonstrates the surprising effectiveness of a simple supervised fine-tuning (SFT) approach when trained on informative and high-difficulty trajectories, challenging the resource-intensive pipelines of pre-training, continual pre-training, SFT, and reinforcement learning typically used by industry. The method involves three key data synthesis modifications: scaling knowledge graph size for richer exploration, expanding the tool set for broader functionality, and applying strict low-step filtering. Trained on only 10.6k data points, OpenSeeker-v2 achieves state-of-the-art performance across four benchmarks for 30B-sized agents with the ReAct paradigm, including 46.0% on BrowseComp, 58.1% on BrowseComp-ZH, 34.6% on Humanity's Last Exam, and 78.0% on xbench, surpassing the Tongyi DeepResearch model trained with a heavy CPT+SFT+RL pipeline, which scores 43.4%, 46.7%, 32.9%, and 75.0% respectively, marking the first state-of-the-art search agent at this scale developed by a purely academic team using only SFT.
本文介绍了OpenSeeker-v2，一种搜索代理，展示了在信息丰富且高难度的轨迹上使用简单的监督微调（SFT）方法时的惊人有效性，挑战了工业界通常采用的包含预训练、持续预训练（CPT）、SFT和强化学习（RL）的资源密集型流程。该方法通过三项关键的数据合成改进：扩大知识图谱规模以促进更丰富的探索、扩展工具集以实现更广泛的功能、以及实施严格的低步过滤。仅使用10.6k数据点进行训练，OpenSeeker-v2在四个基准测试中（针对30B规模、采用ReAct范式的代理）取得了最先进的性能，包括在BrowseComp上达到46.0%，在BrowseComp-ZH上达到58.1%，在Humanity's Last Exam上达到34.6%，在xbench上达到78.0%，超越了使用繁重CPT+SFT+RL流程训练的Tongyi DeepResearch模型（其得分分别为43.4%、46.7%、32.9%和75.0%），标志着首个由纯学术团队仅使用SFT开发的该规模下最先进的搜索代理。
MICA: Multi-granularity Intertemporal Credit Assignment for Long-Horizon Emotional Support Dialogue
Authors: Naifan Zhang, Ruihan Sun, Jinwei Su, Hengjie Yang, Zhengyuan Pan, Zhaohan Chen, Xiaofan Zhang
First: 2026-03-06T12:06:57+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-05T15:53:05+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) for large language models (LLMs) has shown strong performance in single-turn tasks, but extending it to multi-turn interaction remains challenging due to sparse rewards and poor per-turn credit assignment. In emotional support dialogues, responses shape future user states, so matched-state step-wise comparison is unavailable, while trajectory-level supervision is insufficient. We propose MICA (Multi-granularity Intertemporal Credit Assignment), a critic-free RL framework for multi-turn emotional support tasks. MICA derives both immediate and delayed credit from a shared potential function over the user's structured support state. Incremental Distance Reward measures the per-turn decrease in residual distance to the target state, while its Monte Carlo return captures delayed effects. After scope-specific normalization, the two signals form a mixed advantage for stable per-turn optimization without matched-state comparisons, rollout trees, or a learned critic. On EMPA, EQ-Bench, and EmoBench with Qwen2.5-7B-Instruct and Qwen3-8B/14B/32B, MICA consistently outperforms GRPO and REINFORCE++, achieving up to +43.2 on EMPA, while adding no rollout cost and remaining robust to reward judges. These results show that turn-aware credit assignment enables effective and practical multi-turn RL for interactive LLMs.
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of applying reinforcement learning to multi-turn emotional support dialogues, where sparse rewards and poor per-turn credit assignment hinder performance. The authors propose MICA, a critic-free RL framework that derives both immediate and delayed credit from a shared potential function over the user's structured support state, using an Incremental Distance Reward for per-turn improvement and Monte Carlo returns for delayed effects, combined into a mixed advantage after normalization. Experiments on EMPA, EQ-Bench, and EmoBench with Qwen2.5-7B-Instruct and Qwen3-8B/14B/32B show that MICA consistently outperforms GRPO and REINFORCE++, achieving up to +43.2 on EMPA with no additional rollout cost and robustness to reward judges.
该论文针对多轮情感支持对话中强化学习面临的稀疏奖励和每轮信用分配困难的问题，提出了MICA框架。MICA是一种无评论家的强化学习方法，通过共享势函数从用户结构化支持状态中提取即时和延迟信用，利用增量距离奖励衡量每轮向目标状态的残差减少，并结合蒙特卡洛回报捕捉延迟效应，经归一化后形成混合优势用于稳定优化。在EMPA、EQ-Bench和EmoBench上使用Qwen2.5-7B-Instruct和Qwen3-8B/14B/32B的实验表明，MICA在EMPA上最高提升43.2分，且无需额外展开成本，对奖励评判器具有鲁棒性，一致优于GRPO和REINFORCE++。
ReCode: Reinforcing Code Generation with Reasoning-Process Rewards
Authors: Lishui Fan, Yu Zhang, Mouxiang Chen, Zhongxin Liu
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2025-08-07T09:04:10+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-05T15:31:45+00:00
Comments: Accepted to the ACL 2026 Main Conference
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In practice, rigorous reasoning is often a key driver of correct code, while Reinforcement Learning (RL) for code generation often neglects optimizing reasoning quality. Bringing process-level supervision into RL is appealing, but it faces two challenges. First, training reliable reward models to assess reasoning quality is bottlenecked by the scarcity of fine-grained preference data. Second, naively incorporating such neural rewards may suffer from reward hacking. This work proposes ReCode (Reasoning-Reinforced Code Generation), a novel RL training framework comprising: (1) Contrastive Reasoning-Process Reward Learning (CRPL), which trains a reward model with synthesized optimized and degraded reasoning variants to assess the quality of reasoning process; and (2) Consistency-Gated GRPO (CG-GRPO), which integrates the reasoning-process reward model into RL by gating neural reasoning-process rewards with strict execution outcomes, using execution correctness as a hard gate to mitigate reward hacking. Additionally, to assess the reward model's discriminative capability in assessing reasoning-process quality, we introduce LiveCodeBench-RewardBench (LCB-RB), a new benchmark comprising preference pairs of superior and inferior reasoning processes tailored for code generation. Experimental results across HumanEval(+), MBPP(+), LiveCodeBench, and BigCodeBench show that a 7B model trained with ReCode outperforms the base version by 16.1% and reaches performance comparable to GPT-4-Turbo. We further demonstrate the generalizability of ReCode by extending it to the math domain.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ReCode：通过推理过程奖励强化代码生成
在实践中，严谨的推理通常是正确代码的关键驱动因素，而用于代码生成的强化学习往往忽视了对推理质量的优化。将过程级监督引入强化学习颇具吸引力，但面临两个挑战。首先，训练可靠的奖励模型来评估推理质量受到细粒度偏好数据稀缺的制约。其次，简单地将此类神经奖励纳入可能遭受奖励破解问题。本工作提出ReCode（推理强化代码生成），一种新颖的强化学习训练框架，包含：（1）对比推理过程奖励学习，通过合成优化和退化的推理变体来训练奖励模型，以评估推理过程的质量；（2）一致性门控GRPO，通过以严格执行结果作为硬门控来门控神经推理过程奖励，从而将推理过程奖励模型整合到强化学习中，利用执行正确性作为硬门控来缓解奖励破解。此外，为评估奖励模型在评估推理过程质量方面的判别能力，我们引入了LiveCodeBench-RewardBench，这是一个新基准，包含针对代码生成的优质与劣质推理过程的偏好对。在HumanEval(+)、MBPP(+)、LiveCodeBench和BigCodeBench上的实验结果表明，使用ReCode训练的7B模型比基础版本性能提升16.1%，并达到与GPT-4-Turbo相当的性能。我们进一步通过将ReCode扩展到数学领域来证明其泛化能力。
Summary / 总结
ReCode addresses the challenge of improving code generation by reinforcing reasoning quality through reinforcement learning, as rigorous reasoning is often crucial for correct code but is neglected in standard RL approaches. The method introduces Contrastive Reasoning-Process Reward Learning (CRPL) to train a reward model using synthesized optimized and degraded reasoning variants, and Consistency-Gated GRPO (CG-GRPO) to integrate this reward into RL by gating it with strict execution correctness to prevent reward hacking. Experimental results on HumanEval(+), MBPP(+), LiveCodeBench, and BigCodeBench show that a 7B model trained with ReCode outperforms its base version by 16.1% and achieves performance comparable to GPT-4-Turbo, with generalizability also demonstrated in the math domain.
ReCode旨在通过强化学习增强代码生成中的推理质量，因为严谨的推理常是正确代码的关键，但标准RL方法往往忽视这一点。该方法提出了对比推理过程奖励学习（CRPL），利用合成的优化和退化推理变体训练奖励模型，以及一致性门控GRPO（CG-GRPO），通过将推理过程奖励与严格的执行正确性门控结合来防止奖励黑客攻击。在HumanEval(+)、MBPP(+)、LiveCodeBench和BigCodeBench上的实验结果表明，使用ReCode训练的7B模型比基础版本性能提升16.1%，达到与GPT-4-Turbo相当的水平，并且在数学领域也展示了其泛化能力。
Mechanical Conscience: A Mathematical Framework for Dependability of Machine Intelligenc
Authors: Munkhdegerekh Batzorig, Purevbaatar Ganbold, Kyungbin Park, Pilkong Jeong, Kangbin
First: 2026-05-05T15:14:02+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-05T15:14:02+00:00
Comments: 9 pages, 2 figures. Preprint
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Distributed collaborative intelligence (DCI), encompassing edge-to-edge architectures, federated learning, transfer learning, and swarm systems, creates environments in which emergent risk is structurally unavoidable: locally correct decisions by individual agents compose into globally unacceptable behavioral trajectories under uncertainty. Existing approaches such as constrained optimization, safe reinforcement learning, and runtime assurance evaluate acceptability at the level of individual actions rather than across behavioral trajectories, and none addresses the multi-participant, uncertainty-laden nature of DCI deployments. This paper introduces mechanical conscience (MC), a novel concept and simplified mathematical framework that operationalizes trajectory-level normative regulation for both single-agent and distributed intelligent systems. Mechanical conscience is defined as a supervisory filter that minimally corrects a baseline policy's actions to reduce cumulative deviation from a normatively admissible region, while accounting for epistemic uncertainty. We introduce associated constructs, conscience score, mechanical guilt, and resonant dependability, that provide an interpretable vocabulary and computable governance signals for this emerging field. Core theoretical properties are established: admissibility equivalence, existence of optimal regulation, and monotonic deviation reduction. Illustrative results demonstrate that MC-regulated agents maintain trajectory-level normative acceptability where conventional controllers drift outside admissible bounds, and that the framework naturally extends to suppress interaction-induced emergent risk in multi-agent DCI settings.
中文标题/摘要
标题：机械良知：机器智能可信赖性的数学框架
分布式协作智能（DCI），涵盖边缘到边缘架构、联邦学习、迁移学习和群体系统，创造了结构性不可避免的新兴风险环境：在不确定性下，个体智能体局部正确的决策会组合成全局不可接受的行为轨迹。现有方法如约束优化、安全强化学习和运行时保障仅在单个动作层面评估可接受性，而非跨行为轨迹，且均未解决DCI部署中多参与者、充满不确定性的本质。本文提出机械良知（MC），一种新颖概念和简化数学框架，将轨迹层面的规范性调控操作化，适用于单智能体和分布式智能系统。机械良知被定义为一种监督滤波器，在考虑认知不确定性的同时，最小程度地修正基线策略的动作，以减少与规范性可接受区域的累积偏差。我们引入相关构造——良知分数、机械内疚和共振可信赖性——为该新兴领域提供可解释的词汇和可计算的治理信号。建立了核心理论性质：可接受性等价性、最优调控的存在性以及偏差单调递减。示例结果表明，MC调控的智能体在传统控制器漂移出可接受边界时仍能维持轨迹层面的规范性可接受性，且该框架自然扩展以抑制多智能体DCI场景中交互引发的新兴风险。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the problem of emergent risk in distributed collaborative intelligence systems, where locally correct decisions can lead to globally unacceptable behavioral trajectories under uncertainty, a challenge not adequately handled by existing methods like constrained optimization or safe reinforcement learning. The authors propose mechanical conscience, a mathematical framework that acts as a supervisory filter to minimally correct a baseline policy's actions, reducing cumulative deviation from a normatively admissible region while accounting for epistemic uncertainty. Key constructs such as conscience score and mechanical guilt are introduced, and theoretical properties including admissibility equivalence and monotonic deviation reduction are established; illustrative results show that mechanical conscience-regulated agents maintain trajectory-level normative acceptability where conventional controllers drift outside admissible bounds, and the framework effectively suppresses emergent risk in multi-agent settings.
该论文针对分布式协作智能系统中存在的涌现风险问题，即个体局部正确决策在不确定性下可能组合成全局不可接受的行为轨迹，而现有方法如约束优化和安全强化学习未能充分应对。作者提出机械良知这一数学框架，作为监督滤波器，通过最小化修正基线策略的动作，减少与规范可接受区域的累积偏差，并考虑认知不确定性。论文引入了良知分数、机械内疚等概念，建立了可接受性等价、最优调节存在性和偏差单调减少等理论性质；示例结果表明，机械良知调节的智能体能够维持轨迹级规范可接受性，而传统控制器会漂移到可接受边界之外，且该框架能有效抑制多智能体协作中的涌现风险。
SOAR: Real-Time Joint Optimization of Order Allocation and Robot Scheduling in Robotic Mobile Fulfillment Systems
Authors: Yibang Tang, Yifan Yang, Jingyuan Wang, Junhua Chen, Zhen Zhao
First: 2026-05-05T15:09:32+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-05T15:09:32+00:00
Comments: 13 pages, 6 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Robotic Mobile Fulfillment Systems (RMFS) rely on mobile robots for automated inventory transportation, coordinating order allocation and robot scheduling to enhance warehousing efficiency. However, optimizing RMFS is challenging due to strict real-time constraints and the strong coupling of multi-phase decisions. Existing methods either decompose the problem into isolated sub-tasks to guarantee responsiveness at the cost of global optimality, or rely on computationally expensive global optimization models that are unsuitable for dynamic industrial environments. To bridge this gap, we propose SOAR, a unified Deep Reinforcement Learning framework for real-time joint optimization. SOAR transforms order allocation and robot scheduling into a unified process by utilizing soft order allocations as observations. We formulate this as an Event-Driven Markov Decision Process, enabling the agent to perform simultaneous scheduling in response to asynchronous system events. Technically, we employ a Heterogeneous Graph Transformer to encode the warehouse state and integrate phased domain knowledge. Additionally, we incorporate a reward shaping strategy to address sparse feedback in long-horizon tasks. Extensive experiments on synthetic and real-world industrial datasets, in collaboration with Geekplus, demonstrate that SOAR reduces global makespan by 7.5\% and average order completion time by 15.4\% with sub-100ms latency. Furthermore, sim-to-real deployment confirms its practical viability and significant performance gains in production environments. The code is available at https://github.com/200815147/SOAR.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SOAR：机器人移动履行系统中订单分配与机器人调度的实时联合优化
机器人移动履行系统（RMFS）依赖移动机器人实现自动化库存运输，通过协调订单分配与机器人调度来提升仓储效率。然而，由于严格的实时约束和多阶段决策的强耦合性，优化RMFS极具挑战性。现有方法要么将问题分解为孤立的子任务以保证响应性但牺牲全局最优性，要么依赖计算成本高昂的全局优化模型，不适用于动态工业环境。为弥补这一差距，我们提出SOAR——一种用于实时联合优化的统一深度强化学习框架。SOAR通过将软订单分配作为观测，将订单分配与机器人调度转化为统一过程。我们将其建模为事件驱动马尔可夫决策过程，使智能体能够响应异步系统事件执行同步调度。技术上，我们采用异构图变换器编码仓库状态并集成分阶段领域知识。此外，我们引入奖励塑形策略以应对长周期任务中的稀疏反馈。与极智嘉合作在合成与真实工业数据集上的大量实验表明，SOAR在亚100毫秒延迟下将全局完工时间缩短7.5%，平均订单完成时间缩短15.4%。此外，从仿真到实际部署验证了其实际可行性及在生产环境中的显著性能提升。代码见https://github.com/200815147/SOAR。

This paper addresses the challenge of jointly optimizing order allocation and robot scheduling in Robotic Mobile Fulfillment Systems (RMFS) under strict real-time constraints. The authors propose SOAR, a unified Deep Reinforcement Learning framework that transforms the problem into an Event-Driven Markov Decision Process, using soft order allocations as observations and a Heterogeneous Graph Transformer to encode warehouse states with integrated domain knowledge. Extensive experiments on synthetic and real-world industrial datasets show that SOAR reduces global makespan by 7.5% and average order completion time by 15.4% with sub-100ms latency, and sim-to-real deployment confirms its practical viability.
本文针对机器人移动履行系统（RMFS）中在严格实时约束下联合优化订单分配与机器人调度的问题，提出了SOAR框架，这是一个统一的深度强化学习框架，通过将问题转化为事件驱动马尔可夫决策过程，利用软订单分配作为观测，并采用异构图变换器编码仓库状态并集成领域知识。在合成和真实工业数据集上的大量实验表明，SOAR将全局完工时间缩短了7.5%，平均订单完成时间缩短了15.4%，且延迟低于100毫秒，模拟到现实的部署验证了其实际可行性和显著性能提升。
Deep deterministic policy gradient with symmetric data augmentation for lateral attitude tracking control of a fixed-wing aircraft
Authors: Yifei Li, Erik-Jan van Kampen
First: 2024-07-13T08:20:11+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-05T15:09:20+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The symmetry of dynamical systems can be exploited for state-transition prediction and to facilitate control policy optimization. This paper leverages system symmetry to develop sample-efficient offline reinforcement learning (RL) approaches. Under the symmetry assumption for a Markov Decision Process (MDP), a symmetric data augmentation method is proposed. The augmented samples are integrated into the dataset of Deep Deterministic Policy Gradient (DDPG) to enhance its coverage rate of the state-action space. Furthermore, sample utilization efficiency is improved by introducing a second critic trained on the augmented samples, resulting in a dual-critic structure. The aircraft's model is verified to be symmetric, and flight control simulations demonstrate accelerated policy convergence when augmented samples are employed.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于对称数据增强的深度确定性策略梯度在固定翼飞机横向姿态跟踪控制中的应用
动力系统的对称性可用于状态转移预测并促进控制策略优化。本文利用系统对称性开发样本高效的离线强化学习方法。在马尔可夫决策过程的对称性假设下，提出了一种对称数据增强方法。将增强样本集成到深度确定性策略梯度的数据集中，以提高其对状态-动作空间的覆盖率。此外，通过引入基于增强样本训练的第二个评论家，形成双评论家结构，进一步提升了样本利用效率。经验证飞机模型具有对称性，飞行控制仿真表明采用增强样本可加速策略收敛。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of sample inefficiency in offline reinforcement learning for control tasks by exploiting system symmetry. It proposes a symmetric data augmentation method for Markov Decision Processes, which generates augmented samples to improve state-action space coverage in the Deep Deterministic Policy Gradient (DDPG) algorithm. Additionally, a dual-critic structure is introduced, where a second critic is trained on augmented samples to further enhance sample utilization. Flight control simulations for a fixed-wing aircraft confirm the system's symmetry and show that the proposed method accelerates policy convergence compared to standard DDPG.
该论文利用系统对称性来解决离线强化学习在控制任务中样本效率低下的问题。针对马尔可夫决策过程提出了一种对称数据增强方法，通过生成增强样本来提升深度确定性策略梯度算法对状态-动作空间的覆盖范围。此外，引入双评论家结构，利用增强样本训练第二个评论家以进一步提高样本利用率。固定翼飞机的飞行控制仿真验证了系统的对称性，并表明所提方法相比标准DDPG能加速策略收敛。
Fisher Decorator: Refining Flow Policy via a Local Transport Map
Authors: Xiaoyuan Cheng, Haoyu Wang, Wenxuan Yuan, Ziyan Wang, Zonghao Chen, Li Zeng, Zhuo Sun
First: 2026-04-20T07:54:36+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-05T15:00:45+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Recent advances in flow-based offline reinforcement learning (RL) have achieved strong performance by parameterizing policies via flow matching. However, they still face critical trade-offs among expressiveness, optimality, and efficiency. In particular, existing flow policies interpret the $L_2$ regularization as an upper bound of the 2-Wasserstein distance ($W_2$), which can be problematic in offline settings. This issue stems from a fundamental geometric mismatch: the behavioral policy manifold is inherently anisotropic, whereas the $L_2$ (or upper bound of $W_2$) regularization is isotropic and density-insensitive, leading to systematically misaligned optimization directions. To address this, we revisit offline RL from a geometric perspective and show that policy refinement can be formulated as a local transport map: an initial flow policy augmented by a residual displacement. By analyzing the induced density transformation, we derive a local quadratic approximation of the KL-constrained objective governed by the Fisher information matrix, enabling a tractable anisotropic optimization formulation. By leveraging the score function embedded in the flow velocity, we obtain a corresponding quadratic constraint for efficient optimization. Our results reveal that the optimality gap in prior methods arises from their isotropic approximation. In contrast, our framework achieves a controllable approximation error within a provable neighborhood of the optimal solution. Extensive experiments demonstrate state-of-the-art performance across diverse offline RL benchmarks. See project page: https://github.com/ARC0127/Fisher-Decorator.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Fisher装饰器：通过局部传输映射优化流策略
基于流的离线强化学习（RL）的最新进展通过流匹配参数化策略取得了强劲性能。然而，它们仍面临表达能力、最优性和效率之间的关键权衡。特别是，现有流策略将$L_2$正则化解释为2-Wasserstein距离（$W_2$）的上界，这在离线设置中可能存在问题。这一问题源于基本的几何不匹配：行为策略流形本质上是各向异性的，而$L_2$（或$W_2$上界）正则化是各向同性且密度不敏感的，导致优化方向系统性错位。为解决此问题，我们从几何角度重新审视离线RL，并表明策略优化可表述为局部传输映射：一个初始流策略加上残差位移。通过分析诱导的密度变换，我们推导出由Fisher信息矩阵控制的KL约束目标的局部二次近似，从而得到可处理的各向异性优化公式。利用流速度中嵌入的得分函数，我们获得相应的二次约束以实现高效优化。我们的结果表明，先前方法的最优性差距源于其各向同性近似。相比之下，我们的框架在最优解的可证明邻域内实现了可控的近似误差。大量实验表明，该方法在多种离线RL基准上达到了最先进性能。参见项目页面：https://github.com/ARC0127/Fisher-Decorator。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses a geometric mismatch in flow-based offline reinforcement learning, where isotropic L2 regularization misaligns with the anisotropic behavioral policy manifold. The authors propose Fisher Decorator, a method that refines flow policies by formulating policy improvement as a local transport map with a residual displacement, using a Fisher information matrix-based quadratic approximation of the KL-constrained objective to enable anisotropic optimization. Experiments on diverse offline RL benchmarks show state-of-the-art performance, demonstrating that the approach achieves controllable approximation error and provable optimality.
该论文针对基于流的离线强化学习中各向同性L2正则化与各向异性的行为策略流形之间的几何不匹配问题，提出了Fisher Decorator方法。该方法将策略改进建模为局部传输映射，通过残差位移增强初始流策略，并利用Fisher信息矩阵对KL约束目标进行二次近似，实现各向异性优化。在多个离线强化学习基准上的实验表明，该方法达到了最先进的性能，并具有可控的近似误差和可证明的最优性。
Parameter-Efficient Distributional RL via Normalizing Flows and a Geometry-Aware Cramér Surrogate
Authors: Simo Alami C., Rim Kaddah, Jesse Read, Marie-Paule Cani
First: 2025-05-07T10:49:53+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-05T14:58:08+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Distributional Reinforcement Learning (DistRL) improves upon expectation-based methods by modeling full return distributions, but standard approaches often remain far from parsimonious. Categorical methods (e.g., C51) rely on fixed supports where parameter counts scale linearly with resolution, while quantile methods approximate distributions as discrete mixtures whose piecewise-constant densities can be wasteful when modeling complex multi-modal or heavy-tailed returns. We introduce NFDRL, a parsimonious architecture that models return distributions using continuous normalizing flows. Unlike categorical baselines, our flow-based model maintains a compact parameter footprint that does not grow with the effective resolution of the distribution, while providing a dynamic, adaptive support for returns. To train this continuous representation, we propose a Cramér-inspired, geometry-aware distance defined over probability masses obtained from the flow. We show that this distance is a true probability metric, that the associated distributional Bellman operator is a sqrt(gamma)-contraction, and that the resulting objective admits unbiased sample gradients, properties that are typically not simultaneously guaranteed in prior PDF-based DistRL methods. Empirically, NFDRL recovers rich, multi-modal return landscapes on toy MDPs and achieves performance competitive with categorical baselines on the Atari-5 benchmark, while offering substantially better parameter efficiency.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于归一化流与几何感知Cramér替代的参数高效分布强化学习
分布强化学习通过建模完整回报分布改进了基于期望的方法，但标准方法往往不够简洁。分类方法（如C51）依赖固定支撑集，参数数量随分辨率线性增长；分位数方法将分布近似为离散混合，其分段常数密度在建模复杂多模态或重尾回报时可能造成浪费。我们提出NFDRL，一种使用连续归一化流建模回报分布的简洁架构。与分类基线不同，我们的基于流的模型保持紧凑的参数规模，不随分布有效分辨率增长，同时为回报提供动态自适应支撑。为训练这种连续表示，我们提出一种基于Cramér的几何感知距离，该距离定义在从流获得的概率质量上。我们证明该距离是真正的概率度量，关联的分布贝尔曼算子是sqrt(gamma)-压缩，且所得目标函数允许无偏样本梯度——这些性质在先前的基于概率密度函数的分布强化学习方法中通常无法同时保证。实验表明，NFDRL在玩具MDP上恢复了丰富的多模态回报景观，在Atari-5基准上达到与分类基线竞争的性能，同时提供显著更优的参数效率。
Summary / 总结
This paper introduces NFDRL, a parameter-efficient distributional reinforcement learning method that models return distributions using continuous normalizing flows, avoiding the fixed supports and wasteful parameter scaling of categorical or quantile approaches. The authors propose a Cramér-inspired, geometry-aware distance as a training objective, which is proven to be a true probability metric, ensures a sqrt(gamma)-contraction for the distributional Bellman operator, and allows unbiased sample gradients. Experiments show that NFDRL recovers multi-modal return landscapes on toy MDPs and achieves competitive performance on Atari-5 with significantly better parameter efficiency than categorical baselines.
本文提出NFDRL，一种参数高效的分布强化学习方法，通过连续归一化流建模回报分布，避免了分类或分位数方法中固定支撑和参数随分辨率线性增长的问题。作者提出基于Cramér的几何感知距离作为训练目标，该距离被证明是真实概率度量，确保分布贝尔曼算子的sqrt(gamma)-压缩性，并允许无偏样本梯度。实验表明，NFDRL在玩具MDP上恢复多模态回报分布，在Atari-5基准上达到与分类基线相当的性能，同时显著提升参数效率。
RoboAlign-R1: Distilled Multimodal Reward Alignment for Robot Video World Models
Authors: Hao Wu, Yuqi Li, Yuan Gao, Fan Xu, Fan Zhang, Kun Wang, Penghao Zhao, Qiufeng Wang, Yizhou Zhao, Weiyan Wang, Yingli Tian, Xian Wu, Xiaomeng Huang
First: 2026-05-05T14:49:00+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-05T14:49:00+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Existing robot video world models are typically trained with low-level objectives such as reconstruction and perceptual similarity, which are poorly aligned with the capabilities that matter most for robot decision making, including instruction following, manipulation success, and physical plausibility. They also suffer from error accumulation in long-horizon autoregressive prediction. We present RoboAlign-R1, a framework that combines reward-aligned post-training with stabilized long-horizon inference for robot video world models. We construct RobotWorldBench, a benchmark of 10,000 annotated video-instruction pairs collected from four robot data sources, and train a multimodal teacher judge, RoboAlign-Judge, to provide fine-grained six-dimensional evaluation of generated videos. We then distill the teacher into a lightweight student reward model for efficient reinforcement-learning-based post-training. To reduce long-horizon rollout drift, we further introduce Sliding Window Re-encoding (SWR), a training-free inference strategy that periodically refreshes the generation context. Under our in-domain evaluation protocol, RoboAlign-R1 improves the aggregate six-dimension score by 10.1% over the strongest baseline, including gains of 7.5% on Manipulation Accuracy and 4.6% on Instruction Following; these ranking improvements are further supported by an external VLM-based cross-check and a blinded human study. Meanwhile, SWR improves long-horizon prediction quality with only about 1% additional latency, yielding a 2.8% gain in SSIM and a 9.8% reduction in LPIPS. Together, these results show that reward-aligned post-training and stabilized long-horizon decoding improve task consistency, physical realism, and long-horizon prediction quality in robot video world models.
Summary / 总结
Existing robot video world models are trained with low-level objectives that poorly align with robot decision-making capabilities such as instruction following and manipulation success. To address this, the authors propose RoboAlign-R1, a framework that combines reward-aligned post-training with stabilized long-horizon inference. They construct RobotWorldBench, a benchmark of 10,000 annotated video-instruction pairs, and train a multimodal teacher judge, RoboAlign-Judge, for fine-grained six-dimensional evaluation. A lightweight student reward model is distilled from the teacher for efficient reinforcement-learning-based post-training, and Sliding Window Re-encoding (SWR) is introduced to reduce long-horizon rollout drift. Under in-domain evaluation, RoboAlign-R1 improves the aggregate six-dimension score by 10.1% over the strongest baseline, with gains of 7.5% on Manipulation Accuracy and 4.6% on Instruction Following, while SWR improves long-horizon prediction quality with only about 1% additional latency, yielding a 2.8% gain in SSIM and a 9.8% reduction in LPIPS.
现有的机器人视频世界模型通常使用低层次目标进行训练，难以与指令遵循、操作成功等机器人决策关键能力对齐。为此，作者提出RoboAlign-R1框架，结合奖励对齐的后训练与稳定的长时域推理。他们构建了包含10,000个标注视频-指令对的RobotWorldBench基准，并训练多模态教师评判器RoboAlign-Judge进行六维度细粒度评估。通过知识蒸馏得到轻量级学生奖励模型，用于高效的强化学习后训练，同时引入滑动窗口重编码（SWR）这一无需训练的推理策略以减少长时域预测漂移。在域内评估中，RoboAlign-R1将六维度综合得分提升10.1%，其中操作准确率提高7.5%，指令遵循提高4.6%；SWR仅增加约1%延迟，使SSIM提升2.8%，LPIPS降低9.8%。
What You Think is What You See: Driving Exploration in VLM Agents via Visual-Linguistic Curiosity
Authors: Haoxi Li, Qinglin Hou, Jianfei Ma, Jinxiang Lai, Tao Han, Sikai Bai, Jingcai Guo, Jie Zhang, Song Guo
Venue: ICML 2026 Spotlight
First: 2026-05-05T14:08:54+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-05T14:08:54+00:00
Comments: Accepted to ICML 2026 (Spotlight)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
To navigate partially observable visual environments, recent VLM agents increasingly internalize world modeling capabilities into their policies via explicit CoT reasoning, enabling them to mentally simulate futures before acting. However, relying solely on passive reasoning over visited states is insufficient for sparse-reward tasks, as it lacks the epistemic drive to actively uncover the ``known unknown'' required for robust generalization. We ask: Can VLM agents actively find signals that challenge and refine their internal world model through curiosity-driven exploration? In this work, we propose GLANCE, a unified framework that bridges reasoning and exploration by grounding the agent's linguistic world model into the stable visual representations of an evolving target network. Crucially, GLANCE leverages the discrepancy between linguistic prediction and visual reality as an intrinsic curiosity signal within reinforcement learning, steering the agent to actively explore areas where its internal model is uncertain. Extensive experiments across a series of agentic tasks show the effectiveness of GLANCE, and demonstrate that aligning ``what the agent thinks'' with ``what the agent sees'' is key to solving complex or sparse agentic tasks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：所思即所见：通过视觉-语言好奇心驱动VLM智能体探索
为了在部分可观测的视觉环境中导航，最近的VLM智能体越来越多地通过显式思维链推理将世界建模能力内化到其策略中，使其能够在行动前在心理上模拟未来。然而，仅依赖对已访问状态的被动推理对于稀疏奖励任务是不够的，因为它缺乏主动揭示“已知未知”的认知驱动力，而这正是鲁棒泛化所需的。我们提出：VLM智能体能否通过好奇心驱动的探索主动寻找挑战并完善其内部世界模型的信号？在这项工作中，我们提出了GLANCE，这是一个统一框架，通过将智能体的语言世界模型锚定到不断进化的目标网络的稳定视觉表示中，桥接了推理与探索。关键的是，GLANCE利用语言预测与视觉现实之间的差异作为强化学习中的内在好奇心信号，引导智能体主动探索其内部模型不确定的区域。在一系列智能体任务上的大量实验显示了GLANCE的有效性，并证明将“智能体所想”与“智能体所见”对齐是解决复杂或稀疏智能体任务的关键。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of sparse-reward tasks in partially observable visual environments, where VLM agents relying solely on passive reasoning over visited states lack the epistemic drive to explore unknown areas. The authors propose GLANCE, a unified framework that bridges reasoning and exploration by grounding the agent's linguistic world model into stable visual representations of an evolving target network, using the discrepancy between linguistic prediction and visual reality as an intrinsic curiosity signal within reinforcement learning. Extensive experiments across various agentic tasks demonstrate that GLANCE effectively drives exploration and improves performance, showing that aligning what the agent thinks with what it sees is key to solving complex or sparse tasks.
本文针对部分可观测视觉环境中的稀疏奖励任务，指出仅依赖对已访问状态进行被动推理的VLM智能体缺乏主动探索未知区域的认知驱动力。作者提出GLANCE统一框架，通过将智能体的语言世界模型锚定到演化目标网络的稳定视觉表征上，利用语言预测与视觉现实之间的差异作为强化学习中的内在好奇心信号，从而桥接推理与探索。在多种智能体任务上的大量实验表明，GLANCE能有效驱动探索并提升性能，证明对齐智能体所想与所见是解决复杂或稀疏任务的关键。
Lyapunov-Certified Direct Switching Theory for Q-Learning
Authors: Donghwan Lee
First: 2026-04-21T15:22:42+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-05T14:00:33+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Q-learning is a fundamental algorithmic primitive in reinforcement learning. This paper develops a new framework for analyzing Q-learning from a switching-system viewpoint. In particular, we derive a direct stochastic switching-system representation of the Q-learning error. The key observation is that the Bellman maximization error can be expressed exactly as an average of action-wise Q-errors under a suitable stochastic policy. The resulting recursion has a switched linear conditional-mean drift and martingale-difference noise. To the best of our knowledge, this is the first convergence-rate analysis of standard Q-learning whose leading exponential rate is expressed through the joint spectral radius (JSR) of a direct switching family. Since the JSR is the exact worst-case exponential rate of the associated switched linear drift, the resulting rate is among the tightest drift-based rates that can be certified for this Q-learning representation. Building on this representation, we prove finite-time bounds based on a product-defined JSR-induced Lyapunov function and also give an optional common quadratic Lyapunov certificate. The quadratic certificate is only a sufficient condition and hence applies only to instances for which the certificate is feasible, whereas the JSR-induced Lyapunov construction applies to the full direct switching family whenever its JSR is below one. When feasible, the quadratic certificate replaces product-based verification by a computable matrix inequality and gives a simpler stochastic bound. We further extend the framework to Markovian observation models.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于李雅普诺夫认证的直接切换理论的Q学习分析
Q学习是强化学习中的基本算法原语。本文从切换系统视角出发，建立了一种分析Q学习的新框架。具体而言，我们推导了Q学习误差的直接随机切换系统表示。关键发现是：贝尔曼最大化误差可精确表示为在适当随机策略下各动作Q误差的平均值。由此得到的递归具有切换线性条件均值漂移和鞅差噪声。据我们所知，这是首个通过直接切换族的联合谱半径（JSR）表达标准Q学习主导指数收敛速率的分析。由于JSR是关联切换线性漂移的最坏情况指数速率，该速率是此Q学习表示可认证的最紧漂移基速率之一。基于该表示，我们利用乘积定义的JSR诱导李雅普诺夫函数证明了有限时间界，并给出了可选的公共二次李雅普诺夫证书。二次证书仅为充分条件，因此仅适用于证书可行的实例，而JSR诱导的李雅普诺夫构造适用于JSR小于1的完整直接切换族。当可行时，二次证书将基于乘积的验证替换为可计算的矩阵不等式，并给出更简洁的随机界。我们进一步将该框架扩展到马尔可夫观测模型。
Aura-CAPTCHA: A Reinforcement Learning and GAN-Enhanced Multi-Modal CAPTCHA System
Authors: Joydeep Chandra, Prabal Manhas, Ramanjot Kaur, Rashi Sahay
First: 2025-08-20T18:00:08+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-05T13:50:11+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We present Aura-CAPTCHA, a multi-modal verification system that integrates Generative Adversarial Networks (GANs), Reinforcement Learning (RL), and behavioral analysis to create adaptive challenges resistant to classical deep-learning attacks. Our system synthesizes unique visual stimuli via GAN-based generation alongside synchronized audio challenges, while an RL agent adjusts difficulty based on real-time user interaction patterns. A hybrid classifier combining heuristic rules and machine learning distinguishes human from bot interactions. We position Aura-CAPTCHA relative to well-established baselines (text-based schemes, Google reCAPTCHA v2, audio alternatives, and modern invisible risk-analysis systems) and evaluate it against documented state-of-the-art attacks, including convolutional-neural-network solvers, object-detection pipelines (YOLO), and recent agentic vision-language models. Experimental results indicate that Aura-CAPTCHA improves human success rates and lowers classical bypass rates compared to static challenge-based baselines, although, like all explicit-challenge systems, it remains vulnerable to emerging large-model agents. We discuss these limitations transparently and outline future directions toward cognitive-gap-based defenses.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Aura-CAPTCHA：一种基于强化学习和GAN增强的多模态验证码系统
我们提出Aura-CAPTCHA，一种多模态验证系统，它集成了生成对抗网络（GAN）、强化学习（RL）和行为分析，以创建能够抵御经典深度学习攻击的自适应挑战。我们的系统通过基于GAN的生成与同步音频挑战相结合，合成独特的视觉刺激，同时RL代理根据实时用户交互模式调整难度。一个结合启发式规则和机器学习的混合分类器区分人类与机器交互。我们将Aura-CAPTCHA与成熟的基线方案（基于文本的方案、Google reCAPTCHA v2、音频替代方案以及现代隐形风险分析系统）进行对比，并针对文献中记载的最先进攻击（包括卷积神经网络求解器、目标检测流水线（YOLO）以及最近的智能视觉语言模型）进行评估。实验结果表明，与静态挑战基线相比，Aura-CAPTCHA提高了人类成功率并降低了经典绕过率，尽管与所有显式挑战系统一样，它仍然容易受到新兴大型模型代理的攻击。我们透明地讨论了这些局限性，并概述了未来朝向基于认知差距的防御方向。

Ivy-Fake: A Unified Explainable Framework and Benchmark for Image and Video AIGC Detection
Authors: Changjiang Jiang, Wenhui Dong, Zhonghao Zhang, Fengchang Yu, Wei Peng, Xinbin Yuan, Yifei Bi, Ming Zhao, Zian Zhou, Chenyang Si, Caifeng Shan
First: 2025-06-01T12:20:22+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-05T13:47:19+00:00
Comments: Accepted by ICMR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The rapid development of Artificial Intelligence Generated Content (AIGC) techniques has enabled the creation of high-quality synthetic content, but it also raises significant security concerns. Current detection methods face two major limitations: (1) the lack of multidimensional explainable datasets for generated images and videos. Existing open-source datasets (e.g., WildFake, GenVideo) rely on oversimplified binary annotations, which restrict the explainability and trustworthiness of trained detectors. (2) Prior MLLM-based forgery detectors (e.g., FakeVLM) exhibit insufficiently fine-grained interpretability in their step-by-step reasoning, which hinders reliable localization and explanation. To address these challenges, we introduce Ivy-Fake, the first large-scale multimodal benchmark for explainable AIGC detection. It consists of over 106K richly annotated training samples (images and videos) and 5,000 manually verified evaluation examples, sourced from multiple generative models and real world datasets through a carefully designed pipeline to ensure both diversity and quality. Furthermore, we propose Ivy-xDetector, a reinforcement learning model based on Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO), capable of producing explainable reasoning chains and achieving robust performance across multiple synthetic content detection benchmarks. Extensive experiments demonstrate the superiority of our dataset and confirm the effectiveness of our approach. Notably, our method improves performance on GenImage from 86.88% to 96.32%, surpassing prior state-of-the-art methods by a clear margin.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Ivy-Fake：面向图像与视频AIGC检测的统一可解释框架与基准
人工智能生成内容（AIGC）技术的快速发展使得高质量合成内容的创作成为可能，但也引发了重大的安全隐患。当前检测方法面临两大局限：（1）缺乏针对生成图像与视频的多维可解释数据集。现有开源数据集（如WildFake、GenVideo）依赖过于简化的二元标注，限制了训练检测器的可解释性与可信度。（2）先前基于多模态大语言模型的伪造检测器（如FakeVLM）在逐步推理中表现出细粒度可解释性不足，阻碍了可靠的定位与解释。为应对这些挑战，我们提出Ivy-Fake，首个面向可解释AIGC检测的大规模多模态基准。它包含超过10.6万条丰富标注的训练样本（图像与视频）及5000个经人工验证的评估示例，数据源自多种生成模型与真实世界数据集，并通过精心设计的流程确保多样性与质量。此外，我们提出Ivy-xDetector，一种基于分组相对策略优化（GRPO）的强化学习模型，能够生成可解释的推理链，并在多个合成内容检测基准上实现稳健性能。大量实验证明了我们数据集的优越性，并验证了方法的有效性。值得注意的是，我们的方法在GenImage上将性能从86.88%提升至96.32%，显著超越了先前的最优方法。

The authors propose Ivy-Fake, a large-scale multimodal benchmark with over 106K annotated training samples and 5,000 manually verified evaluation examples, along with Ivy-xDetector, a reinforcement learning model based on Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) that generates explainable reasoning chains. Extensive experiments show that Ivy-xDetector significantly improves detection performance, notably increasing accuracy on the GenImage benchmark from 86.88% to 96.32%, surpassing prior state-of-the-art methods.

Exact and Evolutionary Algorithms for Sequential Multi-Objective Transmission Topology Planning
Authors: Job Groeneveld, Miguel Muñoz, Jan Viebahn, Alessandro Zocca
First: 2026-05-05T13:38:30+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-05T13:38:30+00:00
Comments: 29 pages, 6 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We address day-ahead transmission topology planning and congestion management as a sequential, multi-objective optimization problem and develop two complementary algorithms for it: an exact enumeration method and a tailored evolutionary heuristic. The problem is formulated with four operational objectives reflecting real TSO decision criteria: worst-case line loading under $N-1$ security, topological depth, number of switching actions, and time spent in non-reference topologies, over a 24-hour horizon. We introduce the block algorithm, an exact method that exploits the temporal block structure of feasible strategies to enumerate the complete Pareto front; for fixed operational bounds on depth and switch count, its evaluation count grows polynomially with the planning horizon. We complement it with a multi-objective evolutionary algorithm based on NSGA-III, with structure-guided initialization and problem-specific variation operators tailored to the topology-planning structure. Using real operational data from the Dutch high-voltage grid operated by TenneT TSO, we show that the block algorithm computes the full Pareto front for a highly congested day in under three minutes, and that the evolutionary algorithm converges toward but does not recover the exact front. The block algorithm thus provides both a practical decision-support tool and a ground-truth benchmark for future heuristic and learning-based methods on this problem class.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向顺序多目标输电拓扑规划的精确与进化算法
我们将日前输电拓扑规划与阻塞管理建模为顺序多目标优化问题，并为此开发了两种互补算法：精确枚举法和定制化进化启发式算法。该问题包含四个反映实际TSO决策准则的运行目标：N-1安全准则下的最坏情况线路负载、拓扑深度、开关动作次数以及24小时周期内非参考拓扑的持续时间。我们提出了块算法——一种利用可行策略时序块结构精确枚举完整帕累托前沿的方法；在固定深度和开关次数运行边界下，其评估次数随规划周期呈多项式增长。我们将其与基于NSGA-III的多目标进化算法相结合，该算法采用结构引导初始化及针对拓扑规划结构定制的变异算子。利用TenneT TSO运营的荷兰高压电网实际运行数据，我们证明块算法能在三分钟内计算出高度拥堵日的完整帕累托前沿，而进化算法虽能收敛但无法复现精确前沿。因此，块算法既可作为实用决策支持工具，也可为此类问题的未来启发式与学习方法提供基准真值。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses day-ahead transmission topology planning and congestion management as a sequential multi-objective optimization problem, motivated by real transmission system operator (TSO) decision criteria including worst-case line loading under N-1 security, topological depth, number of switching actions, and time in non-reference topologies over a 24-hour horizon. The authors propose two complementary algorithms: an exact block algorithm that exploits the temporal block structure of feasible strategies to enumerate the complete Pareto front with polynomial growth in evaluation count, and a multi-objective evolutionary algorithm based on NSGA-III with structure-guided initialization and problem-specific variation operators. Using real operational data from the Dutch high-voltage grid operated by TenneT TSO, the block algorithm computes the full Pareto front for a highly congested day in under three minutes, while the evolutionary algorithm converges toward but does not recover the exact front, establishing the block algorithm as both a practical decision-support tool and a ground-truth benchmark for future methods.
本文针对日前输电拓扑规划与阻塞管理问题，将其建模为序列多目标优化问题，动机源于真实输电系统运营商（TSO）的决策标准，包括N-1安全准则下的最恶劣线路负载、拓扑深度、开关动作次数以及24小时内处于非参考拓扑的时间。作者提出了两种互补算法：一种精确的块算法，利用可行策略的时间块结构枚举完整帕累托前沿，其评估次数随规划周期呈多项式增长；另一种基于NSGA-III的多目标进化算法，具有结构引导初始化和针对拓扑规划结构的问题特定变异算子。使用荷兰TenneT TSO运营的高压电网真实运行数据，块算法在三分钟内计算出了高度拥堵日的完整帕累托前沿，而进化算法虽收敛但未能恢复精确前沿，从而将块算法确立为实际决策支持工具和未来启发式及学习方法的地面真值基准。
Vanishing L2 regularization for the softmax Multi Armed Bandit
Authors: Stefana-Lucia Anita, Gabriel Turinici
First: 2026-05-05T13:37:13+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-05T13:37:13+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Multi Armed Bandit (MAB) algorithms are a cornerstone of reinforcement learning and have been studied both theoretically and numerically. One of the most commonly used implementation uses a softmax mapping to prescribe the optimal policy and served as the foundation for downstream algorithms, including REINFORCE. Distinct from vanilla approaches, we consider here the L2 regularized softmax policy gradient where a quadratic term is subtracted from the mean reward. Previous studies exploiting convexity failed to identify a suitable theoretical framework to analyze its convergence when the regularization parameter vanishes. We prove here theoretical convergence results and confirm empirically that this regime makes the L2 regularization numerically advantageous on standard benchmarks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：软最大多臂赌博机中消失的L2正则化
多臂赌博机算法是强化学习的基石之一，在理论和数值上均得到广泛研究。最常用的实现之一采用软最大映射来规定最优策略，并作为下游算法（包括REINFORCE）的基础。与标准方法不同，我们在此考虑L2正则化软最大策略梯度，其中从平均奖励中减去二次项。先前利用凸性的研究未能找到合适的理论框架来分析当正则化参数消失时的收敛性。我们在此证明了理论收敛结果，并通过实证确认该机制使L2正则化在标准基准测试中具有数值优势。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of analyzing the convergence of L2 regularized softmax policy gradient in Multi Armed Bandit (MAB) settings, where the regularization parameter vanishes. The motivation stems from the lack of a theoretical framework for this regime, despite its practical use in algorithms like REINFORCE. The method involves proving convergence results for the softmax MAB with vanishing L2 regularization, which subtracts a quadratic term from the mean reward. Main experimental results confirm that this approach is numerically advantageous on standard benchmarks, outperforming vanilla methods.

Neural Surrogate-assisted Glider Wing Design with Stability Analysis and Multi-method Optimization
Authors: Arash Fath Lipaei, AmirHossein Ghaemi, Melika Sabzikari
First: 2025-09-29T17:26:37+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-05T13:12:30+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This paper introduces a modular and scalable design optimization framework for the glider wing design process that enables faster early-phase design while ensuring aerodynamic stability. The pipeline starts with the generation of initial wing geometries and then proceeds to optimize the wing using several algorithms. Aerodynamic performance is assessed using a Vortex Lattice Method (VLM) applied to a carefully selected dataset of wing configurations. These results are employed to develop surrogate neural network models, which can predict lift and drag rapidly and accurately. A timing analysis shows that the surrogate model provides a speedup of approximately 785 times compared to the combined VLM and stability analysis, enabling efficient large-scale optimization. The stability evaluation is implemented by setting the control surfaces and components to fixed positions in order to have realistic flight dynamics. The approach unifies and compares several optimization techniques, including Particle Swarm Optimization (PSO), Genetic Algorithms (GA), gradient-based MultiStart methods, Bayesian optimization, and Lipschitz optimization. Each method ensures constraint management via adaptive strategies and penalty functions, where the targets for lift and design feasibility are enforced. The progression of aerodynamic characteristics and geometries over the optimization iterations will be investigated in order to clarify each algorithm's convergence characteristics and performance efficiency. Our results show improvement in aerodynamic qualities and robust stability properties, offering a mechanism for wing design at speed and precision. In the interest of reproducibility and community development, the complete implementation is publicly available on GitHub.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于神经代理模型的滑翔机机翼设计：稳定性分析与多方法优化
本文介绍了一种模块化、可扩展的滑翔机机翼设计优化框架，能够在确保气动稳定性的同时加速早期设计阶段。该流程首先生成初始机翼几何形状，随后采用多种算法进行优化。气动性能通过涡格法（VLM）对精心挑选的机翼构型数据集进行评估，并利用这些结果开发代理神经网络模型，以快速准确地预测升力和阻力。时序分析表明，与VLM和稳定性分析相结合相比，代理模型实现了约785倍的加速，从而支持高效的大规模优化。稳定性评估通过将控制面和组件固定在特定位置来实现，以模拟真实的飞行动力学。该方法统一并比较了多种优化技术，包括粒子群优化（PSO）、遗传算法（GA）、基于梯度的多起点方法、贝叶斯优化和Lipschitz优化。每种方法均通过自适应策略和惩罚函数进行约束管理，确保升力目标和设计可行性。研究将分析优化迭代过程中气动特性和几何形状的变化，以阐明各算法的收敛特性和性能效率。结果表明，气动质量和稳定性特性均得到改善，为高速高精度的机翼设计提供了机制。为促进可重复性和社区发展，完整实现代码已在GitHub上公开。
Summary / 总结
This paper presents a modular and scalable framework for glider wing design optimization that accelerates early-phase design while ensuring aerodynamic stability. The method generates initial wing geometries, evaluates aerodynamic performance using a Vortex Lattice Method (VLM) on a selected dataset, and trains surrogate neural network models to predict lift and drag rapidly. A timing analysis shows the surrogate model achieves a 785x speedup over combined VLM and stability analysis. The framework unifies multiple optimization techniques including Particle Swarm Optimization, Genetic Algorithms, gradient-based MultiStart, Bayesian optimization, and Lipschitz optimization, with adaptive constraint management. Results demonstrate improved aerodynamic qualities and robust stability properties, with the complete implementation publicly available on GitHub.
本文提出了一种模块化且可扩展的滑翔机机翼设计优化框架，旨在加速早期设计阶段并确保气动稳定性。该方法首先生成初始机翼几何形状，利用涡格法（VLM）对选定数据集进行气动性能评估，并训练替代神经网络模型以快速准确地预测升力和阻力。时间分析表明，与结合VLM和稳定性分析相比，替代模型实现了约785倍的加速。该框架统一并比较了多种优化技术，包括粒子群优化、遗传算法、基于梯度的多起点方法、贝叶斯优化和Lipschitz优化，并通过自适应策略和惩罚函数进行约束管理。结果显示气动特性得到改善且稳定性稳健，完整实现已在GitHub上公开。
Descent-Guided Policy Gradient for Scalable Cooperative Multi-Agent Learning
Authors: Shan Yang, Yang Liu
First: 2026-02-23T17:45:08+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-05T11:51:06+00:00
Comments: 11 pages, 4 figures, 9 tables; plus 19 pages of appendices
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Scaling cooperative multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) is fundamentally limited by cross-agent noise. When agents share a common reward, each agent's learning signal is computed from a shared return that depends on all agents, so the stochasticity of the other agents enters the signal as cross-agent noise that grows with $N$. Fortunately, many engineering systems, such as cloud computing and power systems, have differentiable analytical models that prescribe efficient system states, providing a new reference beyond noisy shared returns. In this work, we propose Descent-Guided Policy Gradient (DG-PG), a framework that augments policy-gradient updates with a noise-free descent signal derived from differentiable analytical models. We prove that DG-PG reduces policy-gradient estimator variance from $\mathcal{O}(N)$ to $\mathcal{O}(1)$, preserves the equilibria of the cooperative game, and achieves agent-independent sample complexity $\widetilde{\mathcal{O}} (1/ε)$. On a heterogeneous cloud resource scheduling task with up to 1500 agents, DG-PG converges within 20 episodes on average, while MAPPO and IPPO fail to converge under identical architectures.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于下降引导策略梯度的可扩展协作多智能体学习
协作多智能体强化学习（MARL）的可扩展性从根本上受到跨智能体噪声的限制。当智能体共享共同奖励时，每个智能体的学习信号基于依赖所有智能体的共享回报计算，因此其他智能体的随机性会以跨智能体噪声的形式进入信号，且该噪声随$N$增长。幸运的是，许多工程系统（如云计算和电力系统）具有可微分的分析模型，能够规定高效的系统状态，从而为超越噪声共享回报提供新的参考。本文提出下降引导策略梯度（DG-PG）框架，通过可微分析模型导出的无噪声下降信号增强策略梯度更新。我们证明DG-PG将策略梯度估计器方差从$\mathcal{O}(N)$降至$\mathcal{O}(1)$，保持协作博弈的均衡，并实现与智能体无关的样本复杂度$\widetilde{\mathcal{O}} (1/ε)$。在包含多达1500个智能体的异构云资源调度任务中，DG-PG平均在20个回合内收敛，而MAPPO和IPPO在相同架构下无法收敛。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the scalability challenge in cooperative multi-agent reinforcement learning caused by cross-agent noise that grows with the number of agents. The authors propose Descent-Guided Policy Gradient (DG-PG), a framework that augments policy-gradient updates with a noise-free descent signal from differentiable analytical models, reducing estimator variance from O(N) to O(1) while preserving game equilibria and achieving agent-independent sample complexity. In a heterogeneous cloud resource scheduling task with up to 1500 agents, DG-PG converges within 20 episodes on average, whereas MAPPO and IPPO fail to converge under identical architectures.
该论文针对合作多智能体强化学习中因智能体间噪声随数量增长而导致的扩展性问题。作者提出了一种名为下降引导策略梯度（DG-PG）的框架，通过从可微分析模型中引入无噪声下降信号来增强策略梯度更新，将估计器方差从O(N)降低到O(1)，同时保持合作博弈的均衡并实现与智能体数量无关的样本复杂度。在最多1500个智能体的异构云资源调度任务中，DG-PG平均在20个回合内收敛，而MAPPO和IPPO在相同架构下无法收敛。
Deep Interest Mining with Cross-Modal Alignment for SemanticID Generation in Generative Recommendation
Authors: Yangchen Zeng, Jinze Wang
First: 2026-03-03T13:36:22+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-05T11:18:30+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Generative Recommendation (GR) has demonstrated remarkable performance in next-token prediction paradigms, which relies on Semantic IDs (SIDs) to compress trillion-scale data into learnable vocabulary sequences. However, existing methods suffer from three critical limitations: (1) Information Degradation: the two-stage compression pipeline causes semantic loss and information degradation, with no posterior mechanism to distinguish high-quality from low-quality SIDs; (2) Semantic Degradation: cascaded quantization discards key semantic information from original multimodal features, as the embedding generation and quantization stages are not jointly optimized toward a unified objective; (3) Modality Distortion: quantizers fail to properly align text and image modalities, causing feature misalignment even when upstream networks have aligned them. To address these challenges, we propose a novel framework integrating three key innovations: Deep Contextual Interest Mining (DCIM), Cross-Modal Semantic Alignment (CMSA), and Quality-Aware Reinforcement Mechanism (QARM). First, we leverage Vision-Language Models (VLMs) to align non-textual modalities into a unified text-based semantic space, mitigating modality distortion. Second, we introduce a deep interest mining mechanism that captures high-level semantic information implicitly present in advertising contexts, encouraging SIDs to preserve critical contextual information through reconstruction-based supervision. Third, we employ a reinforcement learning framework with quality-aware rewards to encourage semantically rich SIDs while suppressing low-quality ones in the posterior stage. Extensive experiments demonstrate that our approach consistently outperforms state-of-the-art SID generation methods, achieving superior performance on multiple benchmarks. Ablation studies further validate the effectiveness of each proposed component
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向生成式推荐的跨模态对齐深度兴趣挖掘语义ID生成
生成式推荐（GR）在下一词元预测范式中展现出卓越性能，其依赖语义ID（SID）将万亿级数据压缩为可学习的词汇序列。然而现有方法存在三个关键局限：（1）信息退化：两阶段压缩流程导致语义损失与信息退化，缺乏后验机制区分高质量与低质量SID；（2）语义退化：级联量化丢弃了原始多模态特征的关键语义信息，因为嵌入生成与量化阶段未针对统一目标进行联合优化；（3）模态扭曲：量化器无法正确对齐文本与图像模态，即使上游网络已对齐特征仍存在特征错位。为解决这些问题，我们提出融合三项关键创新的新框架：深度上下文兴趣挖掘（DCIM）、跨模态语义对齐（CMSA）与质量感知强化机制（QARM）。首先利用视觉语言模型（VLM）将非文本模态对齐至统一文本语义空间以缓解模态扭曲；其次引入深度兴趣挖掘机制，通过重构监督捕获广告上下文中隐含的高层语义信息，促使SID保留关键上下文信息；最后采用带质量感知奖励的强化学习框架，在后验阶段鼓励语义丰富的SID同时抑制低质量SID。大量实验表明，本方法持续优于最先进的SID生成方法，在多个基准上取得更优性能。消融研究进一步验证了各提出组件的有效性。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses three key limitations in generative recommendation systems that rely on Semantic IDs: information degradation from two-stage compression, semantic degradation from cascaded quantization, and modality distortion from misaligned text and image features. The authors propose a framework with three components: Deep Contextual Interest Mining to capture high-level semantic information from advertising contexts, Cross-Modal Semantic Alignment using Vision-Language Models to unify non-textual modalities into a text-based space, and a Quality-Aware Reinforcement Mechanism to reward high-quality SIDs while suppressing low-quality ones. Extensive experiments show that the proposed method consistently outperforms state-of-the-art SID generation methods across multiple benchmarks, with ablation studies confirming the effectiveness of each component.
本文针对生成式推荐系统中语义ID存在的三个关键问题：两阶段压缩导致的信息退化、级联量化造成的语义退化以及文本与图像特征间的模态扭曲。作者提出一个包含三个组件的框架：深度上下文兴趣挖掘以捕捉广告上下文中的高层语义信息，跨模态语义对齐利用视觉语言模型将非文本模态统一到文本语义空间，以及质量感知强化机制通过奖励高质量语义ID并抑制低质量语义ID。大量实验表明，该方法在多个基准测试上持续优于最先进的语义ID生成方法，消融研究进一步验证了每个组件的有效性。
Closed-Loop Vision-Language Planning for Multi-Agent Coordination
Authors: Zhiyuan Li, Wenshuai Zhao, Joni Pajarinen
First: 2025-02-14T13:23:18+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-05T11:18:23+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Cooperative multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) struggles with sample efficiency, interpretability, and generalization. While Large Language Models (LLMs) offer powerful planning capabilities, their application has been hampered by a reliance on text-only inputs and a failure to handle the non-Markovian, partially observable nature of multi-agent tasks. We introduce COMPASS, a multi-agent framework that overcomes these limitations by integrating Vision-Language Models (VLMs) for decentralized, closed-loop decision-making. COMPASS dynamically generates and refines interpretable, code-based strategies stored in a skill library that is bootstrapped from expert demonstrations. To ensure robust coordination, it propagates entity information through a structured multi-hop communication protocol, allowing teams to build a coherent understanding from partial observations. Evaluated on the challenging SMACv2 benchmark, COMPASS significantly outperforms state-of-the-art MARL baselines. Notably, in the symmetric Protoss 5v5 task, COMPASS achieved a 57\% win rate, a 30 percentage point advantage over QMIX (27\%). Project page can be found at https://stellar-entremet-1720bb.netlify.app/.
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the limitations of cooperative multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL), including poor sample efficiency, interpretability, and generalization, by proposing COMPASS, a framework that leverages Vision-Language Models (VLMs) for decentralized, closed-loop planning. The method dynamically generates and refines interpretable, code-based strategies stored in a skill library bootstrapped from expert demonstrations, and uses a structured multi-hop communication protocol to propagate entity information for robust coordination under partial observability. Evaluated on the SMACv2 benchmark, COMPASS significantly outperforms state-of-the-art MARL baselines, achieving a 57% win rate in the symmetric Protoss 5v5 task, a 30 percentage point advantage over QMIX (27%).
该论文针对合作多智能体强化学习（MARL）在样本效率、可解释性和泛化能力方面的局限性，提出了COMPASS框架，通过集成视觉-语言模型（VLM）实现去中心化的闭环决策规划。该方法动态生成并优化存储在技能库中的可解释代码策略，该技能库从专家演示中引导构建，并利用结构化多跳通信协议传播实体信息，以在部分可观测条件下实现稳健协调。在SMACv2基准测试中，COMPASS显著优于最先进的MARL基线，在对称的Protoss 5v5任务中达到57%的胜率，比QMIX（27%）高出30个百分点。
StackFeat RL: Reinforcement Learning over Iterative Dual Criterion Feature Selection for Stable Biomarker Discovery
Authors: A. Yermekov, D. A. Herrera-Martí
First: 2026-04-24T09:52:33+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-05T10:40:40+00:00
Comments: 7 pages. Submitted to eccb2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Feature selection in high-dimensional genomic data ($d \gg n$) demands methods that are simultaneously accurate, sparse, and stable. Existing approaches either require manual threshold specification (mRMR, stability selection), produce unstable selections under data perturbation (Lasso, Boruta), or ignore biological structure entirely. We introduce StackFeat-RL, a meta-learning framework that optimises the hyperparameters of an iterative dual-criterion feature selection algorithm via REINFORCE policy gradients. The dual criterion, requiring both coefficient consistency and selection frequency, guards against two failure modes missed by single-criterion methods, while iterative accumulation provides convergence guarantees via the law of large numbers. On COVID-19 miRNA data (GSE240888, 332 features) and three Alzheimer's disease classification tasks (GSE84422, 13237 genes; Normal vs.\ Possible, Probable, and Definite AD), StackFeat-RL achieves the highest predictive accuracy among all evaluated methods, including ElasticNet, Boruta, mRMR, and stability selection, while requiring 3--4$\times$ fewer features. Keywords: feature selection, reinforcement learning, REINFORCE, elastic net, biomarker discovery, Alzheimer's disease, dual-criterion selection, protein interaction networks
中文标题/摘要
标题：StackFeat RL：基于迭代双准则特征选择的强化学习用于稳定生物标志物发现
高维基因组数据（$d \gg n$）中的特征选择需要同时具备准确性、稀疏性和稳定性的方法。现有方法要么需要手动指定阈值（mRMR、稳定性选择），要么在数据扰动下产生不稳定的选择（Lasso、Boruta），或者完全忽略生物结构。我们提出StackFeat-RL，一种元学习框架，通过REINFORCE策略梯度优化迭代双准则特征选择算法的超参数。该双准则同时要求系数一致性和选择频率，防范了单准则方法遗漏的两种失败模式，而迭代累积通过大数定律提供了收敛保证。在COVID-19 miRNA数据（GSE240888，332个特征）和三个阿尔茨海默病分类任务（GSE84422，13237个基因；正常vs.可能、很可能和确诊AD）上，StackFeat-RL在所有评估方法（包括ElasticNet、Boruta、mRMR和稳定性选择）中实现了最高的预测准确性，同时所需特征数量减少3-4倍。关键词：特征选择、强化学习、REINFORCE、弹性网络、生物标志物发现、阿尔茨海默病、双准则选择、蛋白质相互作用网络

AVA: Attentive VLM Agent for Mastering StarCraft II
Authors: Weiyu Ma, Yuqian Fu, Zecheng Zhang, Bernard Ghanem, Guohao Li
First: 2025-03-07T12:54:25+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-05T08:57:22+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
We introduce AVACraft, a multimodal StarCraft II benchmark supporting both Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning (MARL) and Vision-Language Model (VLM) paradigms. Unlike SMAC-family environments that rely on abstract state representations and exclude VLMs, AVACraft provides RGB visuals, natural language observations, and structured state information, enabling systematic comparison between training-based and zero-shot methods across 21 scenarios spanning micromanagement, coordination, and strategic planning. We establish comprehensive baselines: six MARL algorithms (IQL, QMIX, QTRAN, VDN, MAPPO, IPPO) with Swin-Transformer backbones trained for 5M steps, and multiple VLMs including proprietary (GPT-4o) and open-source (Qwen3-VL) models. Results reveal complementary strengths-MARL peaks at 19.3% win rate after 5M steps, while VLMs achieve 75-90% zero-shot with human-aligned decisions-exposing trade-offs between training efficiency, performance ceilings, interpretability, and deployment cost. Code: https://github.com/camel-ai/VLM-Play-StarCraft2.
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces AVACraft, a multimodal benchmark for StarCraft II that supports both Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning (MARL) and Vision-Language Model (VLM) paradigms, motivated by the limitation of existing SMAC-family environments which rely on abstract states and exclude VLMs. The method provides RGB visuals, natural language observations, and structured state information across 21 scenarios, and establishes baselines with six MARL algorithms using Swin-Transformer backbones trained for 5M steps, alongside proprietary and open-source VLMs. Experimental results show that MARL achieves a peak win rate of 19.3% after training, while VLMs achieve 75-90% zero-shot win rates with human-aligned decisions, revealing trade-offs between training efficiency, performance ceilings, interpretability, and deployment cost.
该论文提出了AVACraft，一个支持多智能体强化学习（MARL）和视觉语言模型（VLM）范式的星际争霸II多模态基准测试，其动机是现有SMAC系列环境依赖抽象状态表示且无法兼容VLM。该方法提供RGB视觉、自然语言观察和结构化状态信息，涵盖21个场景，并建立了基线：使用Swin-Transformer骨干网络训练5M步的六种MARL算法，以及多种专有和开源VLM。实验结果显示，MARL在训练后最高胜率为19.3%，而VLM在零样本情况下达到75-90%的胜率且决策与人类对齐，揭示了训练效率、性能上限、可解释性和部署成本之间的权衡。
Real-Time Evaluation of Autonomous Systems under Adversarial Attacks
Authors: Adithya Mohan, Xujun Xie, Venkatesh Thirugnana Sambandham, Torsten Schön
First: 2026-05-05T08:30:18+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-05T08:30:18+00:00
Comments: Accepted at IEEE ITSC 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Most evaluations of autonomous driving policies under adversarial conditions are conducted in simulation, due to cost efficiency and the absence of physical risk. However, purely virtual testing fails to capture structural inconsistencies, supervision constraints, and state-representation effects that arise in real-world data and fundamentally shape policy robustness. This work presents an offline trajectory-learning and adversarial robustness evaluation framework grounded in real-world intersection driving data. Within a controlled data contract, we train and compare three trajectory-learning paradigms: Multi-Layer Perceptron (MLP)-based Behavior Cloning (BC), Transformer-based object-tokenized BC, and inverse reinforcement learning (IRL) formulated within a Generative Adversarial Imitation Learning (GAIL) framework. Models are evaluated using Average Displacement Error (ADE) and Final Displacement Error (FDE). Inference-time robustness is assessed by subjecting trained policies to gradient-based adversarial perturbations across multiple intersection scenarios, yielding a structured robustness evaluation matrix. Results show that state-structure design and architectural inductive biases critically influence adversarial stability, leading to markedly different robustness profiles despite comparable nominal prediction accuracy (ADE < 0.08). Inference-time Projected Gradient Descent (PGD) attacks induce final displacement errors of up to approximately 8 meters. The proposed framework establishes a scalable benchmark for studying offline trajectory learning and adversarial robustness in real-world autonomous driving settings.
中文标题/摘要
标题：对抗攻击下自主系统的实时评估
大多数对抗条件下自动驾驶策略的评估都在仿真中进行，因为成本效益高且无物理风险。然而，纯虚拟测试无法捕捉现实世界数据中出现的结构不一致性、监督约束和状态表示效应，而这些因素从根本上影响策略的鲁棒性。本文提出一个基于真实路口驾驶数据的离线轨迹学习与对抗鲁棒性评估框架。在受控数据契约下，我们训练并比较三种轨迹学习范式：基于多层感知机（MLP）的行为克隆（BC）、基于Transformer的对象标记化BC，以及在生成对抗模仿学习（GAIL）框架内制定的逆强化学习（IRL）。模型使用平均位移误差（ADE）和最终位移误差（FDE）进行评估。推理时鲁棒性通过将训练好的策略暴露于多个路口场景下的基于梯度的对抗扰动来评估，从而生成结构化的鲁棒性评估矩阵。结果表明，状态结构设计和架构归纳偏差对对抗稳定性有重要影响，导致尽管名义预测精度相当（ADE < 0.08），但鲁棒性特征显著不同。推理时的投影梯度下降（PGD）攻击会引发高达约8米的最终位移误差。所提出的框架为研究真实自动驾驶环境中的离线轨迹学习和对抗鲁棒性建立了可扩展的基准。
Summary / 总结
This work addresses the gap between simulated and real-world evaluations of autonomous driving policies under adversarial attacks by proposing an offline trajectory-learning and robustness evaluation framework grounded in real-world intersection data. The method compares three trajectory-learning paradigms—MLP-based Behavior Cloning, Transformer-based object-tokenized Behavior Cloning, and inverse reinforcement learning within a Generative Adversarial Imitation Learning framework—and assesses inference-time robustness using gradient-based adversarial perturbations. Experimental results show that despite comparable nominal prediction accuracy (ADE < 0.08), state-structure design and architectural inductive biases critically influence adversarial stability, with Projected Gradient Descent attacks causing final displacement errors up to approximately 8 meters.
该工作针对自动驾驶策略在对抗攻击下模拟评估与现实评估之间的差距，提出了一个基于真实路口数据的离线轨迹学习与鲁棒性评估框架。方法比较了三种轨迹学习范式——基于多层感知器的行为克隆、基于Transformer的对象标记化行为克隆以及生成对抗模仿学习框架中的逆强化学习，并通过梯度对抗扰动评估推理时的鲁棒性。实验结果表明，尽管名义预测精度相当（平均位移误差小于0.08），状态结构设计和架构归纳偏差显著影响对抗稳定性，投影梯度下降攻击可导致最终位移误差高达约8米。
MHPR: Multidimensional Human Perception and Reasoning Benchmark for Large Vision-Languate Models
Authors: Kangkang Wang, Qinting Jiang, Wanping Zhang, Bowen Ren, Shengzhao Wen
First: 2026-05-05T08:20:48+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-05T08:20:48+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Multidimensional human understanding is essential for real-world applications such as film analysis and virtual digital humans, yet current LVLM benchmarks largely focus on single-task settings and lack fine-grained, human-centric evaluation. In this work, we introduce MHPR, a comprehensive benchmark for joint perception-reasoning over human-centric scenes spanning individual, multi-person, and human-object interaction dimensions. MHPR comprises a multi-level data design-Captioned Raw Data (C-RD), Supervised Fine-Tuning Data (SFT-D), Reinforcement Learning Data (RL-D), and Test Data (T-D)-together with an automated caption/VQA generation pipeline (ACVG) that performs category-wise attribute decomposition, attribute-specific rewriting, and multi-model voting to ensure high-quality, scalable annotations. We evaluate state-of-the-art vision-language models on fine-grained attributes (appearance, clothing, pose, parts) and high-level semantics (social relations, action semantics, spatial relations, intent and functionality). Our findings show that: 1) format-aligned SFT data substantially improves instruction following and stability; 2) challenge-focused RL data derived from bad-case analysis further enhances perception and reasoning on difficult instances; and 3) training Qwen2.5-VL-7B with MHPR yields significant gains, achieving near-parity with considerably larger models. We release ACVG and MHPR to facilitate reproducible, extensible research on human-centric perception and reasoning.
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces MHPR, a benchmark designed to address the lack of fine-grained, human-centric evaluation in large vision-language models (LVLMs) by focusing on multidimensional human perception and reasoning across individual, multi-person, and human-object interaction scenes. The method involves a multi-level data design including Captioned Raw Data, Supervised Fine-Tuning Data, Reinforcement Learning Data, and Test Data, along with an automated caption/VQA generation pipeline that performs category-wise attribute decomposition and multi-model voting for scalable annotations. Experimental results show that format-aligned supervised fine-tuning data improves instruction following, challenge-focused reinforcement learning data enhances perception on difficult instances, and training Qwen2.5-VL-7B with MHPR achieves significant gains, nearing the performance of much larger models.
该论文提出了MHPR基准，旨在解决当前大型视觉语言模型在细粒度、以人为中心的评估方面的不足，专注于个体、多人及人机交互场景的多维人类感知与推理。方法包括多层级数据设计，如带标题的原始数据、监督微调数据、强化学习数据和测试数据，以及一个自动化标题/VQA生成流程，通过类别属性分解和多模型投票实现可扩展的标注。实验结果表明，格式对齐的监督微调数据提升了指令遵循能力，基于困难案例的强化学习数据增强了感知性能，使用MHPR训练Qwen2.5-VL-7B取得了显著提升，接近更大模型的性能水平。
FINER-SQL: Boosting Small Language Models for Text-to-SQL
Authors: Thanh Dat Hoang, Thanh Trung Huynh, Matthias Weidlich, Thanh Tam Nguyen, Tong Chen, Hongzhi Yin, Quoc Viet Hung Nguyen
First: 2026-05-05T07:51:29+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-05T07:51:29+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Large language models have driven major advances in Text-to-SQL generation. However, they suffer from high computational cost, long latency, and data privacy concerns, which make them impractical for many real-world applications. A natural alternative is to use small language models (SLMs), which enable efficient and private on-premise deployment. Yet, SLMs often struggle with weak reasoning and poor instruction following. Conventional reinforcement learning methods based on sparse binary rewards (0/1) provide little learning signal when the generated SQLs are incorrect, leading to unstable or collapsed training. To overcome these issues, we propose FINER-SQL, a scalable and reusable reinforcement learning framework that enhances SLMs through fine-grained execution feedback. Built on group relative policy optimization, FINER-SQL replaces sparse supervision with dense and interpretable rewards that offer continuous feedback even for incorrect SQLs. It introduces two key reward functions: a memory reward, which aligns reasoning with verified traces for semantic stability, and an atomic reward, which measures operation-level overlap to grant partial credit for structurally correct but incomplete SQLs. This approach transforms discrete correctness into continuous learning, enabling stable, critic-free optimization. Experiments on the BIRD and Spider benchmarks show that FINER-SQL achieves up to 67.73\% and 85\% execution accuracy with a 3B model -- matching much larger LLMs while reducing inference latency to 5.57~s/sample. These results highlight a cost-efficient and privacy-preserving path toward high-performance Text-to-SQL generation. Our code is available at https://github.com/thanhdath/finer-sql.
中文标题/摘要
标题：FINER-SQL：提升小型语言模型在文本到SQL生成中的表现
大型语言模型推动了文本到SQL生成的重大进展，但存在高计算成本、长延迟和数据隐私问题，限制了实际应用。小型语言模型（SLM）作为替代方案，支持高效且私密的本地部署，但常面临推理能力弱和指令遵循差的问题。传统基于稀疏二元奖励（0/1）的强化学习方法在生成的SQL错误时提供的学习信号不足，导致训练不稳定或崩溃。为此，我们提出FINER-SQL，一种可扩展且可复用的强化学习框架，通过细粒度执行反馈增强SLM。基于组相对策略优化，FINER-SQL用密集且可解释的奖励替代稀疏监督，即使对错误SQL也提供连续反馈。它引入两个关键奖励函数：记忆奖励（将推理与已验证轨迹对齐以保持语义稳定性）和原子奖励（衡量操作级重叠，为结构正确但不完整的SQL提供部分分数）。该方法将离散正确性转化为连续学习，实现稳定且无需评论家的优化。在BIRD和Spider基准测试中，FINER-SQL使用3B模型分别达到67.73%和85%的执行准确率，匹配更大LLM的同时将推理延迟降至5.57秒/样本。这些结果展示了高性能文本到SQL生成的高效且隐私保护的路径。代码见https://github.com/thanhdath/finer-sql。

FINER-SQL addresses the limitations of large language models in Text-to-SQL tasks, such as high computational cost and privacy concerns, by enhancing small language models (SLMs) through a reinforcement learning framework. The method replaces sparse binary rewards with fine-grained execution feedback, introducing memory and atomic reward functions to provide continuous learning signals and partial credit for incorrect SQLs. Experiments on BIRD and Spider benchmarks show that FINER-SQL achieves up to 67.73% and 85% execution accuracy with a 3B model, matching larger models while reducing inference latency to 5.57 seconds per sample.

Quantum Hierarchical Reinforcement Learning via Variational Quantum Circuits
Authors: Yu-Ting Lee, Samuel Yen-Chi Chen, Fu-Chieh Chang
First: 2026-05-05T07:14:53+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-05T07:14:53+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning is one of the most challenging learning paradigms where efficacy and efficiency gains are extremely valuable. Hierarchical reinforcement learning is a variant that leverages temporal abstraction to structure decision-making. While parametrized quantum computations have shown success in non-hierarchical reinforcement learning, whether these advantages adapt to hierarchical decision-making remains a critical open question. In this work, we develop a hybrid hierarchical agent based on the option-critic architecture. This hybrid agent substitutes classical components with variational quantum circuits for feature extractors, option-value functions, termination functions, and intra-option policies. Evaluated on standard benchmarking environments, results show that a hybrid agent utilizing a quantum feature extractor can outperform classical baselines while saving up to 66\% trainable parameters. We also identify an architectural bottleneck that quantum option-value estimation severely degrades performance. Further ablation studies reveal how architectural choices of the quantum circuits affect performance. Our work establishes design principles for parameter-efficient hybrid hierarchical agents.
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates whether the advantages of variational quantum circuits in non-hierarchical reinforcement learning can be extended to hierarchical decision-making. The authors propose a hybrid hierarchical agent based on the option-critic architecture, replacing classical components such as feature extractors, option-value functions, termination functions, and intra-option policies with variational quantum circuits. Experimental results on standard benchmarks show that the hybrid agent with a quantum feature extractor outperforms classical baselines while saving up to 66% trainable parameters, but also reveals that quantum option-value estimation severely degrades performance, highlighting key design principles for parameter-efficient hybrid agents.
本文探讨了变分量子电路在非分层强化学习中的优势能否扩展到分层决策中。作者基于选项-评论家架构提出了一种混合分层智能体，用变分量子电路替代了特征提取器、选项价值函数、终止函数和选项内策略等经典组件。在标准基准环境上的实验结果表明，采用量子特征提取器的混合智能体在性能上优于经典基线，同时节省了高达66%的可训练参数，但也揭示了量子选项价值估计会严重降低性能，从而为参数高效的混合智能体建立了关键设计原则。
Poly-EPO: Training Exploratory Reasoning Models
Authors: Ifdita Hasan Orney, Jubayer Ibn Hamid, Shreya S Ramanujam, Shirley Wu, Hengyuan Hu, Noah Goodman, Dorsa Sadigh, Chelsea Finn
First: 2026-04-19T22:54:19+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-05T06:40:59+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Exploration is a cornerstone of learning from experience: it enables agents to find solutions to complex problems, generalize to novel ones, and scale performance with test-time compute. In this paper, we present a framework for post-training language models (LMs) that explicitly encourages optimistic exploration and promotes a synergy between exploration and exploitation. The central idea is to train the LM to generate sets of responses that are collectively accurate under the reward function and exploratory in their reasoning strategies. We first develop a general recipe for optimizing LMs with set reinforcement learning (set RL) under arbitrary objective functions, showing how standard RL algorithms can be adapted to this setting through a modification to the advantage computation. We then propose Polychromic Exploratory Policy Optimization (Poly-EPO), which instantiates this framework with an objective that explicitly synergizes exploration and exploitation. Across a range of reasoning benchmarks, we show that Poly-EPO improves generalization, as evidenced by higher pass@$k$ coverage, preserves greater diversity in model generations, and effectively scales with test-time compute.
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces Poly-EPO, a framework for post-training language models to enhance exploratory reasoning by encouraging optimistic exploration alongside exploitation. The method adapts standard reinforcement learning algorithms to set reinforcement learning, modifying advantage computation to train models to generate diverse yet collectively accurate response sets. Experimental results on reasoning benchmarks demonstrate that Poly-EPO improves generalization through higher pass@k coverage, maintains greater diversity in outputs, and scales effectively with test-time compute.
该论文提出了Poly-EPO框架，用于对语言模型进行后训练，通过鼓励乐观探索与利用的协同来增强探索性推理。该方法将标准强化学习算法适配到集合强化学习场景，通过修改优势计算来训练模型生成多样且整体准确的响应集合。在多个推理基准上的实验结果表明，Poly-EPO通过更高的pass@k覆盖率提升了泛化能力，保持了模型输出的更大多样性，并有效随测试时计算量扩展性能。
Discovering Reinforcement Learning Interfaces with Large Language Models
Authors: Akshat Singh Jaswal, Ashish Baghel, Paras Chopra
First: 2026-05-05T06:27:20+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-05T06:27:20+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Reinforcement learning systems rely on environment interfaces that specify observations and reward functions, yet constructing these interfaces for new tasks often requires substantial manual effort. While recent work has automated reward design using large language models (LLMs), these approaches assume fixed observations and do not address the broader challenge of synthesizing complete task interfaces. We study RL task interface discovery from raw simulator state, where both observation mappings and reward functions must be generated. We propose LIMEN (Code available at https://github.com/Lossfunk/LIMEN), a LLM guided evolutionary framework that produces candidate interfaces as executable programs and iteratively refines them using policy training feedback. Across novel discrete gridworld tasks and continuous control domains spanning locomotion and manipulation, joint evolution of observations and rewards discovers effective interfaces given only a trajectory-level success metric, while optimizing either component alone fails on at least one domain. These results demonstrate that automatic construction of RL interfaces from raw state can substantially reduce manual engineering and that observation and reward components often benefit from co-design, as single-component optimization fails catastrophically on at least one domain in our evaluation suite.
中文标题/摘要

强化学习系统依赖于指定观测和奖励函数的环境接口，然而为新任务构建这些接口通常需要大量人工工作。尽管近期研究已利用大型语言模型（LLM）自动化奖励设计，但这些方法假设观测固定，并未解决合成完整任务接口这一更广泛的挑战。我们研究从原始模拟器状态出发的强化学习任务接口发现，其中观测映射和奖励函数均需生成。我们提出LIMEN（代码见https://github.com/Lossfunk/LIMEN），一种LLM引导的进化框架，将候选接口生成为可执行程序，并利用策略训练反馈迭代优化。在涵盖离散网格世界任务和连续控制领域（包括运动与操作）的新颖任务中，联合进化观测与奖励仅凭轨迹级成功指标即可发现有效接口，而单独优化任一组件至少在一个领域失败。这些结果表明，从原始状态自动构建强化学习接口可大幅减少人工工程，且观测与奖励组件常受益于协同设计，因为单组件优化在我们的评估套件中至少在一个领域灾难性失败。

GRPO-TTA: Test-Time Visual Tuning for Vision-Language Models via GRPO-Driven Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Yujun Li, Hongyuan Zhang, Yuan Yuan
First: 2026-05-05T06:23:20+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-05T06:23:20+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) has recently shown strong performance in post-training large language models and vision-language models. It raises a question of whether the GRPO also significantly promotes the test-time adaptation (TTA) of vision language models. In this paper, we propose Group Relative Policy Optimization for Test-Time Adaptation (GRPO-TTA), which adapts GRPO to the TTA setting by reformulating class-specific prompt prediction as a group-wise policy optimization problem. Specifically, we construct output groups by sampling top-K class candidates from CLIP similarity distributions, enabling probability-driven optimization without access to ground-truth labels. Moreover, we design reward functions tailored to test-time adaptation, including alignment rewards and dispersion rewards, to guide effective visual encoder tuning. Extensive experiments across diverse benchmarks demonstrate that GRPO-TTA consistently outperforms existing test-time adaptation methods, with notably larger performance gains under natural distribution shifts.
